# Surah 23 — Al-Muminun

**Status:** ✅ Publishable · Fidelity 100/100 · Prose overlap (4-gram) 0.087 · Longest prose run 19 words · Em dashes 0

_Translated by claude-sonnet-5 (opus-4.8 on flagged revisions); graded by gemini-3.1-pro-preview at 2026-07-07T11:06:50.984Z. Quality metrics are surah-level. Review each translation against the Arabic below, never against any other translation._

**Overlap spans to check:** "his family who did not believe in him such as his son and his wife and allah knows best"

**Examiner verdict:** The candidate translation is exceptionally accurate, capturing the meaning of the Arabic text with high fidelity and no discernible errors.

## 23:1-11 — verses 1-11 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Tafsir of Surat al-Mu'minun

Meccan.

In the name of Allah, the Most Gracious, the Most Merciful.

Imam Ahmad said: 'Abd al-Razzaq narrated to us, Yunus ibn Sulaym informed me, saying: Yunus ibn Yazid al-Ayli dictated to me, from Ibn Shihab, from 'Urwa ibn al-Zubayr, from 'Abd al-Rahman ibn 'Abd al-Qari who said: I heard 'Umar ibn al-Khattab say: When revelation came down upon the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, a sound like the buzzing of bees was heard near his face. We waited a while, then he faced the qibla and raised his hands and said: "O Allah, increase us and do not diminish us, honor us and do not humiliate us, give us and do not deprive us, favor us and do not favor others over us, and be pleased with us and make us content." Then he said: "Ten verses have been sent down to me. Whoever upholds them will enter Paradise." Then he recited: {Certainly the believers have succeeded} until he finished the ten verses.

Al-Tirmidhi likewise related this in his Tafsir, and al-Nasa'i in the Book of Prayer, from the hadith of 'Abd al-Razzaq, with the same chain.

Al-Tirmidhi said: This is munkar (rejected/unrecognized); we do not know anyone who narrated it besides Yunus ibn Sulaym, and we do not know Yunus.

Al-Nasa'i said in his Tafsir: Qutayba ibn Sa'id informed us, Ja'far narrated to us, from Abu 'Imran, from Yazid ibn Babanus, who said: We said to 'A'isha: O Mother of the Believers, what was the character of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ? She said: The character of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ was the Qur'an. Then she recited: {Certainly the believers have succeeded} until she reached: {and those who are, over their prayers, watchful}. She said: Such was the character of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ.

It has been related from Ka'b al-Ahbar, Mujahid, Abu al-'Aliya, and others: When Allah created the Garden of 'Adn and planted it with His own hand, He looked upon it and said to it: "Speak." So it said: {Certainly the believers have succeeded}. Ka'b al-Ahbar said: Because of the honor prepared for them therein. Abu al-'Aliya said: So Allah revealed that in His Book.

This has also been related from Abu Sa'id al-Khudri as a marfu' (elevated) report. Abu Bakr al-Bazzar said: Muhammad ibn al-Muthanna narrated to us, al-Mughira ibn Salama narrated to us, Wuhayb narrated to us, from al-Jurayri, from Abu Nadra, from Abu Sa'id, who said: Allah created the Garden with one brick of gold and one brick of silver, and He planted it, and said to it: "Speak." So it said: {Certainly the believers have succeeded}. Then the angels entered it and said: "Blessed are you, dwelling place of kings!"

Then he said: Bishr ibn Adam narrated to us, and Yunus ibn 'Ubaydullah al-'Umari narrated to us, 'Adi ibn al-Fadl narrated to us, al-Jurayri narrated to us, from Abu Nadra, from Abu Sa'id, from the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "Allah created the Garden with one brick of gold and one brick of silver, and its mortar is musk." Abu Bakr said: And I saw in another place of this hadith: "The wall of the Garden is one brick of gold and one brick of silver, and its mortar is musk. He said to it: 'Speak.' So it said: {Certainly the believers have succeeded}. Then the angels said: 'Blessed are you, dwelling place of kings!'"

Then al-Bazzar said: We do not know of anyone who related it as marfu' except 'Adi ibn al-Fadl, and he is not a hafiz (a rigorous memorizer of hadith); he is a shaykh who died early.

Al-Hafiz Abu al-Qasim al-Tabarani said: Ahmad ibn 'Ali narrated to us, Hisham ibn Khalid narrated to us, Baqiyya narrated to us, from Ibn Jurayj, from 'Ata', from Ibn 'Abbas, who said: The Prophet ﷺ said: "When Allah created the Garden of 'Adn, He created in it what no eye has seen, [nor ear heard], nor has occurred to the heart of any human being. Then He said to it: 'Speak.' So it said: {Certainly the believers have succeeded}."

Baqiyya's narrations from the Hijazis are weak.

Al-Tabarani said: Muhammad ibn 'Uthman ibn Abi Shayba narrated to us, Minjab ibn al-Harith narrated to us, Hammad ibn 'Isa al-'Absi narrated to us, from Isma'il al-Suddi, from Abu Salih, from Ibn 'Abbas, raising it (as marfu'): "When Allah created the Garden of 'Adn with His hand, and let down its fruits therein, and split open its rivers therein, then He looked upon it and said: {Certainly the believers have succeeded}. He said: 'By My might, no miser shall dwell near Me in you.'"

Abu Bakr ibn Abi al-Dunya said: Muhammad ibn al-Muthanna al-Bazzar narrated to us, Muhammad ibn Ziyad al-Kalbi narrated to us, Ya'ish ibn Husayn narrated to us, from Sa'id ibn Abi 'Aruba, from Qatada, from Anas, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Allah created the Garden of 'Adn with His hand, one brick of white pearl, one brick of red ruby, and one brick of green chrysolite, its mortar is musk, its pebbles are pearls, and its herbage is saffron. Then He said to it: 'Speak.' It said: {Certainly the believers have succeeded}. Then Allah said: 'By My might and My majesty, no miser shall dwell near Me in you.'" Then the Messenger of Allah ﷺ recited: {And whoever is protected from the covetousness of his own soul, those are the successful} [al-Hashr: 9].

His statement, Exalted is He: {Certainly the believers have succeeded}, means: they have triumphed, attained happiness, and achieved success (falah). They are the believers characterized by these qualities.

{Those who, in their prayer, are humbly submissive}. 'Ali ibn Abi Talha said, from Ibn 'Abbas: "Khashi'un (humbly submissive)" means fearful and still. The same has been related from Mujahid, al-Hasan, Qatada, and al-Zuhri.

From 'Ali ibn Abi Talib, may Allah be pleased with him: khushu' (humility/submissiveness) is the humility of the heart. Ibrahim al-Nakha'i said the same.

Al-Hasan al-Basri said: Their khushu' was in their hearts, and because of that they lowered their gazes and lowered their wings (were humble in bearing).

Muhammad ibn Sirin said: The Companions of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ used to raise their eyes to the sky during prayer. When this verse came down: {Certainly the believers have succeeded. Those who, in their prayer, are humbly submissive}, they lowered their eyes to the place of their prostration.

Ibn Sirin said: And they used to say: "His gaze should not go beyond the place of his prayer. If one is accustomed to looking around, let him close his eyes." Ibn Jarir and Ibn Abi Hatim related this.

Then Ibn Jarir related from him, and also from 'Ata' ibn Abi Rabah, as a mursal (report with a gap before the Companion), that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ used to do that until this verse came down.

Khushu' in prayer is only attained by one who empties his heart for it, occupies himself with it to the exclusion of all else, and prefers it over everything else. At that point it becomes a rest for him and a comfort to his eye, as the Prophet ﷺ said in the hadith related by Imam Ahmad and al-Nasa'i, from Anas, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, that he said: "Perfume and women have been made dear to me, and the comfort of my eye has been placed in prayer."

Imam Ahmad said: Waki' narrated to us, Mis'ar narrated to us, from 'Amr ibn Murra, from Salim ibn Abi al-Ja'd, from a man of Aslam, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "O Bilal, give us rest through prayer."

Imam Ahmad also said: 'Abd al-Rahman ibn Mahdi narrated to us, Isra'il narrated to us, from 'Uthman ibn al-Mughira, from Salim ibn Abi al-Ja'd, that Muhammad ibn al-Hanafiyya said: I entered with my father upon an in-law of ours from the Ansar, and the time of prayer came. He said: "O servant girl, bring me water for ablution, that perhaps I may pray and find rest." He saw that we disapproved of that from him, so he said: I heard the Messenger of Allah ﷺ say: "Rise, O Bilal, and give us rest through prayer."

And He said: {And those who turn away from vain talk}, meaning: from falsehood. This encompasses shirk (association of partners with Allah), as some have said, sins, as others have said, and whatever is of no benefit among sayings and deeds, as Allah, Exalted is He, said: {And when they pass by vain talk, they pass by with dignity} [al-Furqan: 72].

Qatada said: By Allah, a command from Allah came to them that struck them senseless away from that.

His statement: {And those who, for zakah, are active} - the majority hold that what is meant by zakah here is the zakah on wealth, even though this verse is Meccan, while zakah was only made obligatory in Medina in the second year after the Hijra. The apparent view is that what was made obligatory in Medina was specifically the zakah with its fixed thresholds (nisab) and specific measures. Otherwise, it appears that the basic obligation of zakah was already in force in Mecca, as Allah, Exalted is He, said in Surat al-An'am, which is Meccan: {And give its due on the day of its harvest} [al-An'am: 141].

It is also possible that what is meant by zakah here is the purification of the soul from shirk and impurity, as in His saying: {He has certainly succeeded who purifies it, and he has failed who corrupts it} [al-Shams: 9-10], and as in His saying: {And woe to the polytheists, those who do not give zakah} [Fussilat: 6-7], according to one of the two opinions in its interpretation.

It is also possible that both meanings are intended together, namely the purification of souls and the zakah on wealth, since giving zakah on wealth is itself part of the purification of the soul. The complete believer is one who undertakes both this and that. And Allah knows best.

And His statement: {And those who guard their private parts}...

{Except from their wives or what their right hands possess, for indeed they are not to be blamed. But whoever seeks beyond that, then those are the transgressors.} That is: those who have guarded their private parts from what is unlawful, so they do not fall into what God has forbidden them of fornication or sodomy, and they do not approach anyone except their wives whom God has made lawful for them, and what their right hands possess of concubines. Whoever engages in what God has made lawful for him incurs no blame and no wrongdoing upon himself. Therefore He said: {for indeed they are not to be blamed. But whoever seeks beyond that}, meaning other than wives and female slaves, {then those are the transgressors}, that is, those who overstep the bounds.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] Qatadah, that a woman took her male slave and said, "I interpreted a verse from the Book of God: {or what their right hands possess}." [He said]: She was brought before Umar ibn al-Khattab, and some of the Companions of the Prophet ﷺ said to him, "She interpreted a verse from the Book of God other than its proper meaning." He said: So he exiled the slave and shaved his head, and said, "You are unlawful for every Muslim after this." This is a gharib (singular) and munqati' (broken-chain) report. Ibn Jarir mentioned it at the beginning of his tafsir of Surat al-Ma'idah, and it is more fitting here. He only made the slave unlawful for [other] men in order to deal with her according to the opposite of her intention, and God knows best.

Imam al-Shafi'i, may God have mercy on him, and those who agreed with him, used this noble verse as evidence for the prohibition of masturbation by hand: {And those who guard their private parts, except from their wives or what their right hands possess}. He said: This act falls outside these two categories, and He has said: {But whoever seeks beyond that, then those are the transgressors}. They also took comfort from a hadith narrated by Imam al-Hasan ibn Arafah in his well-known juz', where he said:

[chain] Anas ibn Malik, from the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "Seven whom God will not look at on the Day of Resurrection, nor purify them, nor gather them with those who do righteous deeds, and He will admit them into the Fire among the first to enter it, unless they repent, and whoever repents, God will accept his repentance: the one who marries his own hand, the active and passive parties [in sodomy], the habitual drinker of wine, the one who strikes his parents until they cry for help, the one who harms his neighbors until they curse him, and the one who has intercourse with his neighbor's wife."

This is a gharib (singular) hadith, and its chain contains someone unknown due to lack of information about him, and God knows best.

His saying: {And those who are keepers of their trusts and their covenants}, that is: when they are entrusted with something they do not betray it, but rather deliver it to its rightful owner, and when they make a covenant or a contract they fulfill it. This is unlike the characteristics of the hypocrites, about whom the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "The sign of the hypocrite is three: when he speaks he lies, when he promises he breaks his promise, and when he is entrusted he betrays the trust."

His saying: {And those who are watchful over their prayers}, that is: they maintain them at their proper times, as Ibn Mas'ud said: I asked the Prophet ﷺ, saying, "O Messenger of God, which deed is most beloved to God?" He said: "Prayer at its proper time." I said, "Then which?" He said: "Kindness to parents." I said, "Then which?" He said: "Struggle (jihad) in the way of God."

Both [Bukhari and Muslim] narrated it in the two Sahihs. And in al-Hakim's Mustadrak it says: "Prayer at the beginning of its time."

Ibn Mas'ud and Masruq said regarding His saying: {And those who are watchful over their prayers}: it means the proper times of prayer. Abu al-Duha, Alqamah ibn Qays, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, and Ikrimah said likewise.

Qatadah said: over its proper times, its bowing, and its prostration.

God began the mention of these praiseworthy qualities with prayer and concluded them with prayer, indicating its superiority, as the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "Be steadfast, though you will never be able to count [all your good deeds], and know that the best of your deeds is prayer, and none maintains ablution consistently except a believer."

When God, exalted is He, described them as possessing these praiseworthy qualities and righteous deeds, He said: {Those are the inheritors, who will inherit al-Firdaws, abiding therein forever.}

It is established in the two Sahihs that the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "When you ask God for Paradise, ask Him for al-Firdaws, for it is the highest part of Paradise and the middle of Paradise, and from it the rivers of Paradise burst forth, and above it is the Throne of the Most Merciful."

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Abu Hurayrah, may God be pleased with him, said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "There is none among you but has two abodes: an abode in Paradise and an abode in the Fire. If he dies and enters the Fire, the people of Paradise inherit his abode. That is [the meaning of] His saying: {Those are the inheritors}."

Ibn Jurayj said, from Layth, from Mujahid: {Those are the inheritors}, he said: There is no servant but has two abodes: an abode in Paradise and an abode in the Fire. As for the believer, his house in Paradise is built up and his house in the Fire is demolished, and as for the disbeliever, his house in Paradise is demolished and his house in the Fire is built up. Something similar has been narrated from Sa'id ibn Jubayr.

So the believers inherit the abodes of the disbelievers, because all of them were created to worship God, exalted is He. When these believers fulfilled what was obligatory upon them of worship, and those others abandoned what they were commanded regarding that for which they were created, these [believers] secured the share of those [disbelievers], which would have been theirs had they obeyed their Lord, mighty and majestic is He. Indeed, something even more far-reaching than this is established in Sahih Muslim, from Abu Burdah, from his father, from the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "On the Day of Resurrection there will come people among the Muslims with sins like mountains, and God will forgive them and place them upon the Jews and Christians instead."

In another wording of his: The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "When the Day of Resurrection comes, God will hand over to every Muslim a Jew or a Christian, and it will be said: 'This is your ransom from the Fire.'" Umar ibn Abd al-Aziz made Abu Burdah swear by God, besides whom there is no other god, three times, that his father had narrated this to him from the Messenger of God ﷺ, and he said: So he swore to him.

I [Ibn Kathir] say: this verse is like His saying, exalted is He: {That is Paradise which We give as inheritance to those of Our servants who were righteous} [Maryam: 63], and like His saying: {And that is Paradise which you are made to inherit for what you used to do} [al-Zukhruf: 73]. Mujahid and Sa'id ibn Jubayr said: al-Jannah in the Roman [Greek/Aramaic] language is al-Firdaws.

Some of the predecessors said: an orchard is not called Firdaws unless it contains grapevines. God knows best.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

تَفْسِيرُ سُورَةِ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ 

مَكِّيَّةٌ.

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَنِ الرَّحِيمِ

* *

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ، أَخْبَرَنِي يُونُسُ بْنُ سُلَيْم قَالَ: أَمْلَى عليَّ يُونُسُ بْنُ يَزِيدَ الْأَيْلِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ شِهَابٍ، عَنْ عُرْوَة بْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ عَبْدٍ الْقَارِيِّ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ عُمَرَ بْنَ الْخَطَّابِ يَقُولُ: كَانَ إِذَا نَزَلَ عَلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم الوحيُ، يُسْمَعُ عِنْدَ وَجْهِهِ كدَوِيّ النَّحْلِ فَمَكثنا سَاعَةً، فَاسْتَقْبَلَ الْقِبْلَةَ وَرَفَعَ يَدَيْهِ، فَقَالَ:"اللَّهُمَّ، زِدْنَا وَلَا تَنْقُصْنا، وَأَكْرِمْنَا وَلَا تُهِنَّا، وَأَعْطِنَا وَلَا تَحْرِمْنَا، وآثِرْنا وَلَا تُؤْثِرْ [عَلَيْنَا، وَارْضَ عَنَّا] وأرضِنا"، ثُمَّ قَالَ: "لَقَدْ أُنْزِلَتْ عَلِيَّ عَشْرُ آيَاتٍ، مَنْ أَقَامَهُنَّ دَخَلَ الْجَنَّةَ"، ثُمَّ قَرَأَ: ﴿قَدْ أَفْلَحَ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ حَتَّى خَتَمَ العَشْر.

وَكَذَا رَوَى التِّرْمِذِيُّ فِي تَفْسِيرِهِ، وَالنَّسَائِيُّ فِي الصَّلَاةِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدِ الرَّزَّاقِ، بِهِ .

وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: مُنْكَرٌ، لَا نَعْرِفُ أَحَدًا رَوَاهُ غَيْرَ يُونُسَ بْنِ سُلَيْمٍ، وَيُونُسُ لَا نَعْرِفُهُ.

وَقَالَ النَّسَائِيُّ فِي تَفْسِيرِهِ: أَنْبَأَنَا قُتَيْبَةَ بْنُ سَعِيدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا جَعْفَرٌ، عَنْ أَبِي عِمْرَانَ عَنْ يَزِيدَ بْنِ بابَنُوس قَالَ: قُلْنَا لِعَائِشَةَ: يَا أُمِّ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، كَيْفَ كَانَ خُلُق رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ؟ قَالَتِ: كَانَ خُلُقِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ الْقُرْآنَ، فَقَرَأَتْ: ﴿قَدْ أَفْلَحَ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ حَتَّى انتَهَتْ إِلَى: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ هُمْ عَلَى صَلَوَاتِهِمْ يُحَافِظُونَ﴾ ، قَالَتْ: هَكَذَا كَانَ خُلُق رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ. 

وقد رُوي عَنْ كَعْبِ الْأَحْبَارِ، وَمُجَاهِدٍ، وَأَبِي الْعَالِيَةِ، وغيرهم: لَمَّا خلق الله جنة عدن، وَغَرَسَهَا بِيَدِهِ، نَظَرَ إِلَيْهَا وَقَالَ لَهَا. تَكَلَّمِي. فَقَالَتْ: ﴿قَدْ أَفْلَحَ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ ، قَالَ كَعْبُ الْأَحْبَارِ: لِمَا أعدَّ لَهُمْ فِيهَا مِنَ الْكَرَامَةِ. وَقَالَ أَبُو الْعَالِيَةِ: فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ ذَلِكَ فِي كِتَابِهِ.

وَقَدْ رُوي ذَلِكَ عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْخُدْرِيِّ مَرْفُوعًا، فَقَالَ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الْبَزَّارُ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ المُثَنَّى، حَدَّثَنَا الْمُغِيرَةُ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا وُهَيْب، عَنِ الجُرَيْري، عَنْ أَبِي نَضْرَة، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ قَالَ: خَلَقَ اللَّهُ الْجَنَّةَ، لَبِنَةً مِنْ ذَهَبٍ وَلَبِنَةٍ مِنْ فِضَّةٍ، وَغَرَسَهَا، وَقَالَ لَهَا: تَكَلَّمِي. فَقَالَتْ: ﴿قَدْ أَفْلَحَ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ ، فَدَخَلَتْهَا الْمَلَائِكَةُ فَقَالَتْ: طُوبَى لَكِ، منزلَ الْمُلُوكِ! . 

ثُمَّ قَالَ : وَحَدَّثَنَا بِشْر بْنُ آدَمَ، وَحَدَّثَنَا يُونُسُ بْنُ عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ العُمَري، حَدَّثَنَا عَدِي بْنُ الْفَضْلِ، حَدَّثَنَا الجُرَيْرِي، عَنْ أَبِي نَضْرَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "خَلَقَ اللَّهُ الْجَنَّةَ، لَبِنَةً مِنْ ذَهَبٍ وَلَبِنَةٍ مِنْ فِضَّةٍ، وَمِلَاطُهَا الْمِسْكُ". قَالَ أَبُو بَكْرٍ: وَرَأَيْتُ فِي مَوْضِعٍ آخَرَ فِي هَذَا الْحَدِيثِ: "حَائِطُ الْجَنَّةِ، لَبِنَةٌ ذَهَبٌ وَلَبِنَةٌ فِضَّةٌ، ومِلاطُها الْمِسْكُ. فَقَالَ لَهَا: تَكَلَّمِي. فَقَالَتْ: ﴿قَدْ أَفْلَحَ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ فَقَالَتِ الْمَلَائِكَةُ: طُوبَى لَكِ، مَنْزِلَ الْمُلُوكِ! ".

ثُمَّ قَالَ الْبَزَّارُ: لَا نَعْلَمُ أَحَدًا رَفَعَهُ إِلَّا عَدِيّ بْنَ الْفَضْلِ، وَلَيْسَ هُوَ بِالْحَافِظِ، وَهُوَ شَيْخٌ مُتَقَدِّمُ الْمَوْتِ .

وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو الْقَاسِمِ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ عَلِيٍّ، حَدَّثَنَا هِشَامُ بْنُ خَالِدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا بَقِيَّة، عَنِ ابْنِ جُرَيْج، عَنْ عَطَاءٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: قَالَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ: "لَمَّا خَلَقَ اللَّهُ جَنَّةَ عَدْن، خَلَقَ فِيهَا مَا لَا عَيْنٌ رَأَتْ، [وَلَا أُذُنٌ سَمِعَتْ] ، وَلَا خَطَرَ عَلَى قَلْبِ بَشَرٍ. ثُمَّ قَالَ لَهَا: تَكَلَّمِي. فَقَالَتْ: ﴿قَدْ أَفْلَحَ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ .

بَقِيًّة: عَنِ الْحِجَازِيِّينَ ضَعِيفٌ.

وَقَالَ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عُثْمَانَ بْنِ أَبِي شَيْبَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا مِنْجَابُ بْنُ الْحَارِثِ، حَدَّثَنَا حماد ابن عِيسَى الْعَبْسِيُّ، عَنْ إِسْمَاعِيلَ السُّدِّيّ، عَنْ أَبِي صَالِحٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ -يَرْفَعُهُ-: "لَمَّا خَلَقَ اللَّهُ جَنَّةَ عَدْن بِيَدِهِ، ودَلَّى فِيهَا ثِمَارَهَا، وَشَقَّ فِيهَا أَنْهَارَهَا، ثُمَّ نَظَرَ إِلَيْهَا فَقَالَ: ﴿قَدْ أَفْلَحَ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ . قَالَ: وَعِزَّتِي لَا يُجَاوِرُنِي فيك بخيل" .

وَقَالَ أَبُو بَكْرٍ بْنُ أَبِي الدُّنْيَا: حَدَّثَنَا محمد بن المثنى البَزَّار، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ زِيَادٍ الْكَلْبِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا يَعِيشُ بْنُ حُسَيْنٍ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ أَبِي عَرُوبَة، عَنْ قَتادة، عَنْ أَنَسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "خَلَقَ اللَّهُ جَنَّةَ عَدْنٍ بِيَدِهِ، لَبِنَةً مِنْ دُرَّة بَيْضَاءَ، وَلَبِنَةً مِنْ يَاقُوتَةٍ حَمْرَاءَ، وَلَبِنَةً مِنْ زَبَرْجَدَةَ خَضْرَاءَ، ملاطُها الْمِسْكُ، وحَصْباؤها اللُّؤْلُؤُ، وحَشِيشها الزَّعْفَرَانُ، ثُمَّ قَالَ لَهَا: انطِقِي. قَالَتْ: ﴿قَدْ أَفْلَحَ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ فَقَالَ اللَّهُ: وَعِزَّتِي، وَجَلَالِي لَا يُجَاوِرُنِي فِيكِ بَخِيلٌ". ثُمَّ تَلَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: ﴿وَمَنْ يُوقَ شُحَّ نَفْسِهِ فَأُولَئِكَ هُمُ الْمُفْلِحُونَ﴾ [الْحَشْرِ: ٩] فَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿قَدْ أَفْلَحَ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ أَيْ: قَدْ فَازُوا وسُعِدُوا وحَصَلوا عَلَى الْفَلَاحِ، وَهُمُ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ الْمُتَّصِفُونَ بِهَذِهِ الْأَوْصَافِ.

﴿الَّذِينَ هُمْ فِي صَلاتِهِمْ خَاشِعُونَ﴾ " قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿خَاشِعُونَ﴾ : خَائِفُونَ سَاكِنُونَ. وَكَذَا رُوِيَ عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، وَالْحَسَنِ، وَقَتَادَةَ، وَالزُّهْرِيِّ .

وَعَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ أَبِي طَالِبٍ، رَضِي اللَّهُ عَنْهُ: الخشوعُ: خشوعُ القلبِ. وَكَذَا قَالَ إِبْرَاهِيمُ النَّخَعِيُّ.

وَقَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ: كَانَ خُشُوعُهُمْ فِي قُلُوبِهِمْ، فَغَضُّوا بِذَلِكَ أَبْصَارَهُمْ، وَخَفَضُوا الْجَنَاحَ.

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ سِيرِينَ: كَانَ أَصْحَابُ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَرْفَعُونَ أَبْصَارَهُمْ إِلَى السَّمَاءِ فِي الصَّلَاةِ، فَلَمَّا نَزَلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ: ﴿قَدْ أَفْلَحَ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ. الَّذِينَ هُمْ فِي صَلاتِهِمْ خَاشِعُونَ﴾ خَفَضُوا أَبْصَارَهُمْ إِلَى مَوْضِعِ سُجُودِهِمْ.

[وَ] قَالَ ابْنُ سِيرِينَ: وَكَانُوا يَقُولُونَ: لَا يُجَاوِزُ بَصَرُهُ مُصَلاه، فَإِنْ كَانَ قَدِ اعْتَادَ النَّظَرَ فَلْيُغْمِضْ. رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ وَابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ.

ثُمَّ رَوَى ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ عَنْهُ، وَعَنْ عَطَاءِ بْنِ أَبِي رَبَاح أَيْضًا مُرْسَلًا أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ كَانَ يَفْعَلُ ذَلِكَ، حَتَّى نَزَلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ.

وَالْخُشُوعُ فِي الصَّلَاةِ إِنَّمَا يَحْصُلُ بِمَنْ فَرَّغ قَلْبَهُ لَهَا، وَاشْتَغَلَ بِهَا عَمَّا عَدَاهَا، وَآثَرَهَا عَلَى غَيْرِهَا، وَحِينَئِذٍ تَكُونُ رَاحَةً لَهُ وقُرَّة عَيْنٍ، كَمَا قَالَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ، فِي الْحَدِيثِ الَّذِي رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ وَالنَّسَائِيُّ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أنه قَالَ: "حُبِّبَ إليَّ الطِّيب وَالنِّسَاءُ، وَجُعِلَتْ قُرَّةُ عَيْنِي فِي الصَّلَاةِ" .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا وَكِيع، حَدَّثَنَا مِسْعَر، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ مُرَّة، عَنْ سَالِمِ بْنِ أبي الجَعْد، عَنْ رَجُلٍ مِنْ أسلَم، أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "يَا بِلَالُ، أَرِحْنَا بِالصَّلَاةِ" .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ أَيْضًا؛ حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ مَهْدِي، حَدَّثَنَا إِسْرَائِيلُ، عَنْ عثمان بن المغيرة، عن سالم ابن أَبِي الْجَعْدِ، أَنَّ مُحَمَّدَ بْنَ الْحَنَفِيَّةِ قَالَ: دَخَلْتُ مَعَ أَبِي عَلَى صِهْرٍ لَنَا مِنَ الْأَنْصَارِ، فحَضَرت الصَّلَاةُ، فَقَالَ: يَا جَارِيَةُ، ائْتِنِي بوَضُوء لَعَلِّي أُصَلِّي فَأَسْتَرِيحَ. فَرَآنَا أَنْكَرْنَا عَلَيْهِ ذَلِكَ ، فَقَالَ: سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "قُمْ يَا بِلَالُ، فَأَرِحْنَا بِالصَّلَاةِ" .

وَقَالَ : ﴿وَالَّذِينَ هُمْ عَنِ اللَّغْوِ مُعْرِضُونَ﴾ أَيْ: عَنِ الْبَاطِلِ، وَهُوَ يَشْمَلُ: الشِّرْكَ -كَمَا قَالَهُ بَعْضُهُمْ-وَالْمَعَاصِي -كَمَا قَالَهُ آخَرُونَ -وَمَا لَا فَائِدَةَ فِيهِ مِنَ الْأَقْوَالِ وَالْأَفْعَالِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِذَا مَرُّوا بِاللَّغْوِ مَرُّوا كِرَامًا﴾ [الْفَرْقَانِ: ٧٢] .

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: أَتَاهُمْ وَاللَّهِ مِنْ أَمْرِ اللَّهِ مَا وقَذَهم عَنْ ذَلِكَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ هُمْ لِلزَّكَاةِ فَاعِلُونَ﴾ : الْأَكْثَرُونَ عَلَى أَنَّ الْمُرَادَ بِالزَّكَاةِ هَاهُنَا زَكَاةُ الْأَمْوَالِ، مَعَ أَنَّ هَذِهِ [الْآيَةَ] مَكِّيَّةٌ، وَإِنَّمَا فُرِضَتِ الزَّكَاةُ بِالْمَدِينَةِ فِي سَنَةِ اثْنَتَيْنِ مِنَ الْهِجْرَةِ. وَالظَّاهِرُ أَنَّ الَّتِي فُرِضَتْ بِالْمَدِينَةِ إِنَّمَا هِيَ ذَاتُ النَّصَب وَالْمَقَادِيرِ الْخَاصَّةِ، وَإِلَّا فَالظَّاهِرُ أَنَّ أَصْلَ الزَّكَاةِ كَانَ وَاجِبًا بِمَكَّةَ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى فِي سُورَةِ الْأَنْعَامِ، وَهِيَ مَكِّيَّةٌ: ﴿وَآتُوا حَقَّهُ يَوْمَ حَصَادِهِ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ١٤١] .

وَقَدْ يُحْتَمَلُ أَنْ يَكُونَ الْمُرَادُ بِالزَّكَاةِ هَاهُنَا: زَكَاةُ النَّفْسِ مِنَ الشِّرْكِ وَالدَّنَسِ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿قَدْ أَفْلَحَ مَنْ زَكَّاهَا. وَقَدْ خَابَ مَنْ دَسَّاهَا﴾ [الشَّمْسِ: ٩، ١٠] ، وَكَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَوَيْلٌ لِلْمُشْرِكِينَ. الَّذِينَ لَا يُؤْتُونَ الزَّكَاةَ﴾ [فُصِّلَتْ: ٦، ٧] ، عَلَى أَحَدِ الْقَوْلَيْنِ فِي تَفْسِيرِهَا.

وَقَدْ يُحْتَمَلُ أَنْ يَكُونَ كِلَا الْأَمْرَيْنِ مُرَادًا، وَهُوَ زَكَاةُ النُّفُوسِ وَزَكَاةُ الْأَمْوَالِ؛ فَإِنَّهُ مِنْ جُمْلَةِ زَكَاةِ النُّفُوسِ، وَالْمُؤْمِنُ الْكَامِلُ هُوَ الَّذِي يَتَعَاطَى هَذَا وَهَذَا، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ هُمْ لِفُرُوجِهِمْ حَافِظُونَ. إِلا عَلَى أَزْوَاجِهِمْ أوْ مَا مَلَكَتْ أَيْمَانُهُمْ فَإِنَّهُمْ غَيْرُ مَلُومِينَ * فَمَنِ ابْتَغَى وَرَاءَ ذَلِكَ فَأُولَئِكَ هُمُ الْعَادُونَ﴾ أَيْ: وَالَّذِينَ قَدْ حَفِظُوا فُرُوجَهُمْ مِنَ الْحَرَامِ، فَلَا يَقَعُونَ فِيمَا نَهَاهُمُ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ مِنْ زِنًا أَوْ لِوَاطٍ، وَلَا يَقْرَبُونَ سِوَى أَزْوَاجَهُمُ الَّتِي أَحَلَّهَا اللَّهُ لَهُمْ، وَمَا مَلَكَتْ أَيْمَانُهُمْ مِنَ السَّرَارِيِّ، وَمَنْ تَعَاطَى مَا أَحَلَّهُ اللَّهُ لَهُ فَلَا لَوْمَ عَلَيْهِ وَلَا حَرَجَ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿فَإِنَّهُمْ غَيْرُ مَلُومِينَ فَمَنِ ابْتَغَى وَرَاءَ ذَلِكَ﴾ أَيْ: غَيْرَ الْأَزْوَاجِ وَالْإِمَاءِ، ﴿فَأُولَئِكَ هُمُ الْعَادُونَ﴾ أَيِ: الْمُعْتَدُونَ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ بَشَّار، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الْأَعْلَى، حَدَّثَنَا سَعِيدٌ، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ، أن امرأة اتَّخَذَتْ مَمْلُوكَهَا، وَقَالَتْ: تأَوّلْت آيَةً مِنْ كِتَابِ اللَّهِ: ﴿أوْ مَا مَلَكَتْ أَيْمَانُهُمْ﴾ [قَالَ] : فأُتي بها عمر ابن الْخَطَّابِ، فَقَالَ لَهُ نَاسٍ مِنْ أَصْحَابِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ: تَأَوَّلَتْ آيَةً مِنْ كِتَابِ اللَّهِ عَلَى غَيْرِ وَجْهِهَا. قَالَ: فَغرب الْعَبْدَ وَجَزَّ رَأْسَهُ: وَقَالَ: أَنْتِ بَعْدَهُ حَرَامٌ عَلَى كُلِّ مُسْلِمٍ. هَذَا أَثَرٌ غَرِيبٌ مُنْقَطِعٌ، ذَكَرَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ فِي أَوَّلِ تَفْسِيرِ سُورَةِ الْمَائِدَةِ ، وَهُوَ هَاهُنَا أَلْيَقُ، وَإِنَّمَا حَرَّمَهَا عَلَى الرِّجَالِ مُعَامَلَةً لَهَا بِنَقِيضِ قَصْدِهَا، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَدِ اسْتَدَلَّ الْإِمَامُ الشَّافِعِيُّ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، وَمَنْ وَافَقَهُ عَلَى تَحْرِيمِ الِاسْتِمْنَاءِ بِالْيَدِ بِهَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ ﴿وَالَّذِينَ هُمْ لِفُرُوجِهِمْ حَافِظُونَ. إِلا عَلَى أَزْوَاجِهِمْ أوْ مَا مَلَكَتْ أَيْمَانُهُمْ﴾ قَالَ: فَهَذَا الصَّنِيعُ خَارِجٌ عَنْ هَذَيْنَ الْقِسْمَيْنِ، وَقَدْ قَالَ: ﴿فَمَنِ ابْتَغَى وَرَاءَ ذَلِكَ فَأُولَئِكَ هُمُ الْعَادُونَ﴾ وَقَدِ اسْتَأْنَسُوا بِحَدِيثٍ رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ الْحَسَنُ بْنُ عَرَفَةَ فِي جُزْئِهِ الْمَشْهُورِ حَيْثُ قَالَ:

حَدَّثَنِي عَلِيُّ بْنُ ثَابِتٍ الجَزَريّ، عَنْ مَسْلَمَةَ بْنِ جَعْفَرٍ، عَنْ حَسَّانَ بْنِ حُمَيْدٍ ، عَنْ أَنَسِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "سَبْعَةٌ لَا يَنْظُرُ اللَّهُ إِلَيْهِمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، وَلَا يُزَكِّيهِمْ، وَلَا يَجْمَعُهُمْ مَعَ الْعَامِلِينَ، وَيُدْخِلُهُمُ النَّارَ أَوَّلَ الدَّاخِلِينَ، إِلَّا أَنْ يَتُوبُوا، فَمَنْ تَابَ تَابَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ: نَاكِحُ يَدِهِ ، وَالْفَاعِلُ، وَالْمَفْعُولُ بِهِ، وَمُدْمِنُ الْخَمْرِ، وَالضَّارِبُ وَالِدَيْهِ حَتَّى يَسْتَغِيثَا، وَالْمُؤْذِي جِيرَانَهُ حَتَّى يَلْعَنُوهُ، وَالنَّاكِحُ حَلِيلَةَ جَارِهِ" .

هَذَا حَدِيثٌ غَرِيبٌ، وَإِسْنَادُهُ فِيهِ مَنْ لَا يُعْرَفُ؛ لِجَهَالَتِهِ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ هُمْ لأمَانَاتِهِمْ وَعَهْدِهِمْ رَاعُونَ﴾ أَيْ: إِذَا اؤْتُمِنُوا لَمْ يَخُونُوا، بَلْ يُؤَدُّونَهَا إِلَى أَهْلِهَا، وَإِذَا عَاهَدُوا أَوْ عَاقَدُوا أَوْفَوْا بِذَلِكَ، لَا كَصِفَاتِ الْمُنَافِقِينَ الَّذِينَ قَالَ فِيهِمْ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "آيَةُ الْمُنَافِقِ ثَلَاثٌ: إِذَا حَدَّث كَذَبَ، وَإِذَا وَعَدَ أَخْلَفَ، وإذا اؤتمن خَانَ".

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ هُمْ عَلَى صَلَوَاتِهِمْ يُحَافِظُونَ﴾ أَيْ: يُوَاظِبُونَ عَلَيْهَا فِي مَوَاقِيتِهَا، كَمَا قَالَ ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ: سَأَلْتُ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ فَقُلْتُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، أَيُّ الْعَمَلِ أَحَبُّ إِلَى اللَّهِ؟ قَالَ: "الصَّلَاةُ عَلَى وَقْتِهَا". قُلْتُ: ثُمَّ أَيٌّ؟ قَالَ: "بِرُّ الْوَالِدَيْنِ". قُلْتُ: ثُمَّ أَيٌّ؟ قَالَ: "الْجِهَادُ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ".

أَخْرَجَاهُ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ . وَفِي مُسْتَدْرَكِ الْحَاكِمِ قَالَ: "الصلاة في أول وقتها" .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ، وَمَسْرُوقٌ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ هُمْ عَلَى صَلَوَاتِهِمْ يُحَافِظُونَ﴾ يَعْنِي: مَوَاقِيتَ الصَّلَاةِ. وَكَذَا قَالَ أَبُو الضُّحَى، وَعَلْقَمَةُ بْنُ قَيْسٍ، وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ، وَعِكْرِمَةُ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: عَلَى مَوَاقِيتِهَا وَرُكُوعِهَا وَسُجُودِهَا.

وَقَدِ افْتَتَحَ اللَّهُ ذِكْرَ هَذِهِ الصِّفَاتِ الْحَمِيدَةِ بِالصَّلَاةِ، وَاخْتَتَمَهَا بِالصَّلَاةِ، فَدَلَّ عَلَى أَفْضَلِيَّتِهَا، كَمَا قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "اسْتَقِيمُوا وَلَنْ تُحْصُوا، وَاعْلَمُوا أَنَّ خَيْرَ أَعْمَالِكُمُ الصَّلَاةُ، وَلَا يُحَافِظُ عَلَى الْوُضُوءِ إِلَّا مُؤْمِنٌ" .

ولَما وَصَفَهم [اللَّهُ] تَعَالَى بِالْقِيَامِ بِهَذِهِ الصِّفَاتِ الْحَمِيدَةِ وَالْأَفْعَالِ الرَّشِيدَةِ قَالَ: ﴿أُولَئِكَ هُمُ الْوَارِثُونَ الَّذِينَ يَرِثُونَ الْفِرْدَوْسَ هُمْ فِيهَا خَالِدُونَ﴾

وَثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِذَا سَأَلْتُمُ اللَّهَ الْجَنَّةَ فَاسْأَلُوهُ الْفِرْدَوْسَ، فَإِنَّهُ أَعْلَى الْجَنَّةِ وَأَوْسَطُ الْجَنَّةِ، وَمِنْهُ تَفَجَّرُ أَنْهَارُ الْجَنَّةِ، وَفَوْقَهُ عَرْشُ الرَّحْمَنِ" .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ سِنَان، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو مُعَاوِيَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنْ أَبِي صَالِحٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَا مِنْكُمْ مِنْ أَحَدٍ إِلَّا وَلَهُ مَنْزِلَانِ: مَنْزِلٌ فِي الْجَنَّةِ وَمَنْزِلٌ فِي النَّارِ، فَإِنْ مَاتَ فَدَخَلَ النَّارَ وَرثَ أَهْلُ الْجَنَّةِ مَنْزِلَهُ، فَذَلِكَ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿أُولَئِكَ هُمُ الْوَارِثُونَ﴾ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْج، عَنْ لَيْث، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: ﴿أُولَئِكَ هُمُ الْوَارِثُونَ﴾ قَالَ: مَا مِنْ عَبْدٍ إِلَّا وَلَهُ مَنْزِلَانِ: مَنْزِلٌ فِي الْجَنَّةِ، وَمَنْزِلٌ فِي النَّارِ، فَأَمَّا الْمُؤْمِنُ فيُبنَى بَيْتُهُ الَّذِي فِي الْجَنَّةِ، ويُهدّم بَيْتُهُ الَّذِي فِي النَّارِ ، وَأَمَّا الْكَافِرُ فيُهْدَم بَيْتُهُ الَّذِي فِي الْجَنَّةِ، ويُبنى بَيْتُهُ الَّذِي فِي النَّارِ. وَرُوِيَ عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْر نَحْوَ ذَلِكَ.

فَالْمُؤْمِنُونَ يَرْثُونَ مَنَازِلَ الْكُفَّارِ؛ لِأَنَّهُمْ [كُلَّهُمْ] خُلِقُوا لِعِبَادَةِ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى ، فَلَمَّا قَامَ هَؤُلَاءِ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ بِمَا وَجَبَ عَلَيْهِمْ مِنَ الْعِبَادَةِ، وترَكَ أُولَئِكَ مَا أمرُوا بِهِ مِمَّا خُلقوا لَهُ -أحرزَ هؤلاء نصيب أُولَئِكَ لَوْ كَانُوا أَطَاعُوا رَبَّهُمْ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، بَلْ أَبْلَغُ مِنْ هَذَا أَيْضًا، وَهُوَ مَا ثَبَتَ فِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ، عَنْ أَبِي بُردَةَ ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "يَجِيءُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ نَاسٌ مِنَ الْمُسْلِمِينَ بِذُنُوبٍ أَمْثَالِ الْجِبَالِ، فَيَغْفِرُهَا اللَّهُ لَهُمْ، ويضَعُها عَلَى الْيَهُودِ وَالنَّصَارَى" .

وَفِي لَفْظٍ لَهُ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِذَا كَانَ يَوْمُ الْقِيَامَةِ دَفَعَ اللَّهُ لِكُلِّ مُسْلِمٍ يَهُودِيًّا أَوْ نَصْرَانِيًّا، فَيُقَالُ : هَذَا فَكَاكُكَ مِنَ النَّارِ". فَاسْتَحْلَفَ عُمر بْنُ عَبْدِ الْعَزِيزِ أَبَا بُردَةَ بِاللَّهِ الَّذِي لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ، ثَلَاثَ مَرَّاتٍ، أَنَّ أَبَاهُ حَدَّثه عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، قال: فَحَلَفَ لَهُ . قُلْتُ: وَهَذِهِ الْآيَةُ كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿تِلْكَ الْجَنَّةُ الَّتِي نُورِثُ مِنْ عِبَادِنَا مَنْ كَانَ تَقِيًّا﴾ [مَرْيَمَ: ٦٣] ، وَكَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَتِلْكَ الْجَنَّةُ الَّتِي أُورِثْتُمُوهَا بِمَا كُنْتُمْ تَعْمَلُونَ﴾ [الزُّخْرُفِ: ٧٣] . وَقَدْ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْر: الْجَنَّةُ بِالرُّومِيَّةِ هِيَ الْفِرْدَوْسُ.

وَقَالَ بَعْضُ السَّلَفِ: لَا يُسَمَّى الْبُسْتَانُ فِرْدَوْسًا إِلَّا إِذَا كَانَ فِيهِ عِنَبٌ، فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ .

---

## 23:12-16 — verses 12-16 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing us about the beginning of the creation of man from an extract of clay, that is Adam (peace be upon him). Allah created him from sounding clay derived from black mud molded into shape.

Al-A'mash said, from al-Minhal ibn Amr, from Abu Yahya, from Ibn Abbas: {from an extract of clay} he said: it means the choicest part of water.

Mujahid said: {from an extract} meaning from the semen of Adam.

Ibn Jarir said: Adam was named "clay" only because he was created from it.

Qatadah said: Adam was drawn out from the clay. This is clearer in meaning and closer to the context, for Adam (peace be upon him) was created from sticky clay, which is the sounding clay derived from black mud molded into shape, and that in turn was created from dust, as the Almighty said: {And among His signs is that He created you from dust, then behold, you are human beings spreading about} [al-Rum: 20].

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] from Abu Musa, from the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "Allah created Adam from a handful that He took from the whole earth. So the children of Adam came out according to the nature of the earth: among them the red, the black, the white, and those in between, and the wicked and the good, and those in between."

Abu Dawud and al-Tirmidhi both related it through several routes from Awf al-A'rabi, with similar wording. Al-Tirmidhi said: hasan sahih (sound, authentic).

{Then We made him a sperm-drop}: this pronoun refers to the genus of mankind, as He said in another verse: {And He began the creation of man from clay, then He made his progeny from an extract of despised water} [al-Sajdah: 7-8], meaning weak, as He said: {Did We not create you from despised water? Then We placed it in a secure resting place}, meaning the womb, prepared and made ready for that, {until a known term, so We determined, and how excellent are We who determine} [al-Mursalat: 22-23], meaning until a known period and a fixed term, until it became firmly established and moved from one state to another, and from one description to another. That is why He says here: {Then We made the sperm-drop into a clinging clot}, meaning then We turned the sperm-drop, which is the gushing fluid that comes out from the loins of the man, that is his back, and the ribs of the woman, that is the bones of her chest between the collarbone and the breast, into a red clinging clot resembling a leech, elongated in shape. Ikrimah said: it is blood.

{Then We made the clot into a lump of flesh}: this is a piece resembling a chunk of meat, having no shape or distinguishing features. {Then We made the lump of flesh into bones} meaning We shaped it, giving it a head, two hands, and two legs, with its bones, sinews, and veins.

Others read it: {Then We made the lump of flesh into bones}.

Ibn Abbas said: this refers to the bone of the spine.

In the Sahih, from the hadith of Abu al-Zinad, from al-A'raj, from Abu Hurairah, who said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Every part of the son of Adam decays except the coccyx (the tailbone); from it he was created and from it he will be reassembled."

{Then We clothed the bones with flesh} meaning We placed over that what would cover it, hold it together, and strengthen it. {Then We brought him into being as another creation} meaning then We breathed into him the spirit, so he moved and became {another creation} possessing hearing, sight, perception, movement, and activity. {So blessed is Allah, the best of creators}.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] from Zaid ibn Ali, from his father, from Ali ibn Abi Talib, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: When the sperm-drop completes four months, an angel is sent to it and breathes the spirit into it amid the three darknesses. That is His saying: {Then We brought him into being as another creation}, meaning We breathed the spirit into him.

It has been related from Abu Sa'id al-Khudri that this refers to the breathing of the spirit.

Ibn Abbas said: {Then We brought him into being as another creation} means by it: the spirit. Mujahid, Ikrimah, al-Sha'bi, al-Hasan, Abu al-Aliyah, al-Dahhak, al-Rabi' ibn Anas, al-Suddi, and Ibn Zaid said the same, and Ibn Jarir preferred this view.

Al-Awfi said, from Ibn Abbas: {Then We brought him into being as another creation} means: We move him from one state to another, until he comes out as an infant, then grows up as a small child, then reaches puberty, then becomes a young man, then middle-aged, then elderly, then decrepit with age.

From Qatadah and al-Dahhak similarly. There is no contradiction here, for from the very beginning of the breathing of the spirit into him, these transitions and states began. And Allah knows best.

Imam Ahmad said in his Musnad: [chain] from Abdullah, that is Ibn Mas'ud, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ told us, and he is the truthful one whose truthfulness is confirmed: "Indeed, each of you has his creation gathered together in his mother's womb for forty days, then he is a clot for a like period, then he is a lump of flesh for a like period, then the angel is sent to him and breathes the spirit into him, and he is commanded with four matters: his provision, his lifespan, his deeds, and whether he is wretched or fortunate. By the One besides whom there is no god, one of you may do the deeds of the people of Paradise until there is nothing between him and it except an arm's length, but then what has been written overtakes him, and he is sealed with the deeds of the people of the Fire, and so he enters it. And one of you may do the deeds of the people of the Fire, until there is nothing between him and it except an arm's length, but then what has been written overtakes him, and he is sealed with the deeds of the people of Paradise, and so he enters it."

Both al-Bukhari and Muslim related it from the hadith of Sulaiman ibn Mihran al-A'mash.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] from Khaithamah, who said: Abdullah, that is Ibn Mas'ud, said: When the sperm-drop falls into the womb, it flies about into every hair and nail, and remains for forty days, then it descends into the womb and becomes a clot.

Imam Ahmad also said: [chain] from Abdullah, who said: A Jew passed by the Messenger of Allah ﷺ while he was speaking to his companions, and the Quraysh said: O Jew, this man claims to be a prophet. He said: I will ask him about something that only a prophet would know. So he came and sat down and said: O Muhammad, from what is man created? He said: "O Jew, from all of it he is created, from the sperm-drop of the man and the sperm-drop of the woman. As for the man's sperm-drop, it is thick fluid from which come the bones and sinews, and as for the woman's sperm-drop, it is thin fluid from which come the flesh and blood." The Jew stood up and said: This is how those before you used to say.

Imam Ahmad also said: [chain] from Abu al-Tufail Hudhaifah ibn Usaid al-Ghifari, who said: I heard the Messenger of Allah ﷺ say: "The angel comes to the sperm-drop after it has settled in the womb for forty nights, and says: O Lord, what shall it be? Wretched or fortunate? Male or female? Then Allah says, and they write it down. Then they say: what shall it be, male or female? Then Allah, mighty and majestic, says, and they write it down, and his deeds, his effect, his affliction, and his provision are written. Then the scroll is folded up, and nothing is added to what is in it nor is anything taken away."

Muslim related it in his Sahih, from the hadith of Sufyan ibn Uyainah, from Amr, that is Ibn Dinar, with similar wording. And through other routes, from Abu al-Tufail Amir ibn Wathilah, from Hudhaifah ibn Usaid Abu Sarihah al-Ghifari, with similar wording. And Allah knows best.

The hafiz Abu Bakr al-Bazzar said: [chain] from Anas, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, said: "Allah has appointed an angel over the womb, who says: O Lord, a sperm-drop. O Lord, a clot. O Lord, a lump of flesh. Then when Allah wills to create it, he says: O Lord, male or female? Wretched or fortunate? What shall the provision and lifespan be?" He said: "That is then written while he is in his mother's womb."

Both al-Bukhari and Muslim related it from the hadith of Hammad ibn Zaid, with the same content.

As for His saying: {So blessed is Allah, the best of creators}, this means: when He mentioned His power and His subtle skill in creating this sperm-drop, moving it from state to state and form to form, until it took the shape it eventually attained, that of a sound human being, complete in creation, He said: {So blessed is Allah, the best of creators}.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] from Anas, who said: Umar, that is Ibn al-Khattab, may Allah be pleased with him, said: I agreed with my Lord and He agreed with me in four matters. This verse was revealed: {And indeed We created man from an extract of clay}, and I said: "So blessed is Allah, the best of creators." Then {So blessed is Allah, the best of creators} was revealed.

He also said: [chain] from Zaid ibn Thabit al-Ansari, who said: The Messenger of Allah dictated to me this verse: {And indeed We created man from an extract of clay} up to His saying: {another creation}, and Mu'adh said: "So blessed is Allah, the best of creators." The Messenger of Allah ﷺ laughed. Mu'adh said to him: Why did you laugh, O Messenger of Allah? He said: "It was sealed with it: {So blessed is Allah, the best of creators}."

Jabir ibn Yazid al-Ju'fi is very weak, and this report of his contains severe irregularity, for this surah is Meccan, while Zaid ibn Thabit only wrote down revelation in Medina, and likewise Mu'adh ibn Jabal's acceptance of Islam only occurred in Medina as well. And Allah knows best.

As for His saying: {Then indeed, after that, you will die}, meaning after this first coming into being out of nonexistence, you proceed toward death. {Then indeed you will be resurrected on the Day of Resurrection}, meaning the second coming into being, {then Allah brings about the second coming into being} [al-Ankabut: 20], meaning on the Day of Return, when spirits and bodies are raised up, and He will call creatures to account and pay each doer in full for his deed, if good then good, and if evil then evil.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنِ ابْتِدَاءِ خَلْقِ الْإِنْسَانِ مِنْ سُلَالَةٍ مِنْ طِينٍ، وَهُوَ آدَمُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، خَلَقَهُ اللَّهُ مِنْ صَلْصَالٍ مِنْ حَمَأٍ مَسْنُونٍ.

وَقَالَ الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنِ المِنْهال بْنِ عَمْرٍو، عَنْ أَبِي يَحْيَى، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿مِنْ سُلالَةٍ مِنْ طِينٍ﴾ قَالَ: صَفوةُ الْمَاءِ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: ﴿مِنْ سُلالَةٍ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ مَنِيِّ آدَمَ.

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: وَإِنَّمَا سُمِّيَ آدَمُ طِينًا لِأَنَّهُ مَخْلُوقٌ مِنْهُ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: استُلّ آدمُ مِنَ الطِّينِ. وَهَذَا أَظْهَرُ فِي الْمَعْنَى، وَأَقْرَبُ إِلَى السِّيَاقِ، فَإِنَّ آدَمَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، خُلِقَ مِنْ طِينٍ لَازِبٍ، وَهُوَ الصَّلْصَالُ مِنَ الْحَمَأِ الْمَسْنُونِ، وَذَلِكَ مَخْلُوقٌ مِنَ التُّرَابِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمِنْ آيَاتِهِ أَنْ خَلَقَكُمْ مِنْ تُرَابٍ ثُمَّ إِذَا أَنْتُمْ بَشَرٌ تَنْتَشِرُونَ﴾ [الروم: ٢٠] .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ سَعِيدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عَوْف، حَدَّثَنَا قَسَامة بْنُ زُهَيْر، عَنْ أَبِي مُوسَى، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ خَلَقَ آدَمَ مِنْ قَبْضَةٍ قَبَضَهَا مِنْ جَمِيعِ الْأَرْضِ، فَجَاءَ بَنُو آدَمَ عَلَى قَدْر الْأَرْضِ، جَاءَ مِنْهُمُ الْأَحْمَرُ وَالْأَسْوَدُ وَالْأَبْيَضُ، وَبَيْنَ ذَلِكَ، وَالْخَبِيثُ وَالطَّيِّبُ، وَبَيْنَ ذَلِكَ".

وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ، مِنْ طُرُقٍ، عَنْ عَوْفٍ الْأَعْرَابِيِّ، بِهِ نَحْوَهُ . وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: حَسَنٌ صَحِيحٌ.

﴿ثُمَّ جَعَلْنَاهُ نُطْفَةً﴾ : هَذَا الضَّمِيرُ عَائِدٌ عَلَى جِنْسِ الْإِنْسَانِ، كَمَا قَالَ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿وَبَدَأَ خَلْقَ الإنْسَانِ مِنْ طِينٍ * ثُمَّ جَعَلَ نَسْلَهُ مِنْ سُلالَةٍ مِنْ مَاءٍ مَهِينٍ﴾ [السَّجْدَةِ: ٧، ٨] أَيْ: ضَعِيفٍ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿أَلَمْ نَخْلُقْكُمْ مِنْ مَاءٍ مَهِينٍ. فَجَعَلْنَاهُ فِي قَرَارٍ مَكِينٍ﴾ ، يَعْنِي: الرحمُ مُعَد لِذَلِكَ مُهَيَّأٌ لَهُ، ﴿إِلَى قَدَرٍ مَعْلُومٍ * فَقَدَرْنَا فَنِعْمَ الْقَادِرُونَ﴾ [الْمُرْسَلَاتِ: ٢٢، ٢٣] ، أَيْ: [إِلَى] مُدَّةٍ مَعْلُومَةٍ وَأَجَلٍ مُعَيَّنٍ حَتَّى اسْتَحْكَمَ وتنَقَّل مِنْ حَالٍ إِلَى حَالٍ، وَصِفَةٍ إِلَى صِفَةٍ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿ثُمَّ خَلَقْنَا النُّطْفَةَ عَلَقَةً﴾ أَيْ: ثُمَّ صَيَّرنا النُّطْفَةَ، وَهِيَ الْمَاءُ الدَّافِقُ الَّذِي يَخْرُجُ مِنْ صُلْبِ الرَّجُلِ -وَهُوَ ظَهْرُهُ-وَتَرَائِبِ الْمَرْأَةِ-وَهِيَ عِظَامُ صَدْرِهَا مَا بَيْنَ التَّرْقُوَةِ إِلَى الثَّنْدُوَةِ-فَصَارَتْ عَلَقَةً حَمْرَاءَ عَلَى شَكْلِ الْعَلَقَةِ مُسْتَطِيلَةً. قَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ: وَهِيَ دَمٌ.

﴿فَخَلَقْنَا الْعَلَقَةَ مُضْغَةً﴾ : وَهِيَ قِطْعَةٌ كالبَضعة مِنَ اللَّحْمِ، لَا شَكْلَ فِيهَا وَلَا تَخْطِيطَ، ﴿فَخَلَقْنَا الْمُضْغَةَ عِظَامًا﴾ يَعْنِي: شَكَّلْنَاهَا ذَاتَ رَأْسٍ وَيَدَيْنِ وَرِجْلَيْنِ بِعِظَامِهَا وَعَصَبِهَا وَعُرُوقِهَا.

وَقَرَأَ آخَرُونَ: ﴿فَخَلَقْنَا الْمُضْغَةَ عِظَامًا ﴾ .

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: وَهُوَ عَظْمُ الصُّلْبِ.

وَفِي الصَّحِيحِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي الزِّنَاد، عَنِ الْأَعْرَجِ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "كُلُّ جَسَدِ ابْنِ آدَمَ يَبْلَى إِلَّا عَجْبُ الذَّنَب، مِنْهُ خُلِقَ وَمِنْهُ يُرَكَّبُ" .

﴿فَكَسَوْنَا الْعِظَامَ لَحْمًا﴾ أَيْ: وَجَعَلْنَا عَلَى ذَلِكَ مَا يَسْتُرُهُ وَيَشُدُّهُ وَيُقَوِّيهِ، ﴿ثُمَّ أَنْشَأْنَاهُ خَلْقًا آخَرَ﴾ أَيْ: ثُمَّ نَفَخْنَا فِيهِ الرُّوحَ، فَتَحَرَّكَ وَصَارَ ﴿خَلْقًا آخَرَ﴾ ذَا سَمْعٍ وَبَصَرٍ وَإِدْرَاكٍ وَحَرَكَةٍ وَاضْطِرَابٍ ﴿فَتَبَارَكَ اللَّهُ أَحْسَنُ الْخَالِقِينَ﴾

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ الْحُسَيْنِ، حَدَّثَنَا جَعْفَرُ بْنُ مُسافر، حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ حَسَّانَ، حَدَّثَنَا النَّضْرُ -يَعْنِي: ابْنَ كَثِيرٍ، مَوْلَى بَنِي هَاشِمٍ-حَدَّثَنَا زَيْدُ بْنُ عَلِيٍّ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ أَبِي طَالِبٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: إِذَا أَتَمَّتِ النُّطْفَةُ أَرْبَعَةَ أَشْهُرٍ، بُعِث إِلَيْهَا مَلك فَنَفَخَ فِيهَا الرُّوحَ في الظُّلُمَاتِ الثَّلَاثِ، فَذَلِكَ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿ثُمَّ أَنْشَأْنَاهُ خَلْقًا آخَرَ﴾ يَعْنِي: نَفَخْنَا فِيهِ الرُّوحَ .

ورُوي عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْخُدْرِيِّ أَنَّهُ نَفْخُ الرُّوحِ.

قَالَ ابن عباس: ﴿ثُمَّ أَنْشَأْنَاهُ خَلْقًا آخَرَ﴾ يعني بِهِ: الرُّوحَ . وَكَذَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَعِكْرِمَةُ، وَالشَّعْبِيُّ، وَالْحَسَنُ، وَأَبُو الْعَالِيَةِ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ، وَالرَّبِيعُ بْنُ أَنَسٍ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ، وابنُ زَيْدٍ، وَاخْتَارَهُ ابنُ جَرِيرٍ .

وَقَالَ العَوْفِيّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿ثُمَّ أَنْشَأْنَاهُ خَلْقًا آخَرَ﴾ يَعْنِي: نَنْقُلُهُ مِنْ حَالٍ إِلَى حَالٍ، إِلَى أَنْ خَرَجَ طِفْلًا ثُمَّ نَشَأَ صَغِيرًا، ثُمَّ احْتَلَمَ، ثُمَّ صَارَ شَابًّا، ثُمَّ كَهْلًا ثُمَّ شَيْخًا، ثُمَّ هَرِمًا.

وَعَنْ قَتَادَةَ، وَالضَّحَّاكِ نَحْوُ ذَلِكَ. وَلَا مُنَافَاةَ، فَإِنَّهُ مِنَ ابْتِدَاءِ نَفْخِ الرُّوحِ [فِيهِ] شَرَع فِي هَذِهِ التَّنَقُّلَاتِ وَالْأَحْوَالِ. وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ فِي مُسْنَدِهِ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو مُعَاوِيَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ وَهْبٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ -هُوَ ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ-قَالَ: حَدَّثَنَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، وَهُوَ الصَّادِقُ الْمَصْدُوقُ: "إِنَّ أَحَدَكُمْ ليُجمع خَلقُه فِي بَطْنِ أُمِّهِ أَرْبَعِينَ يَوْمًا، ثُمَّ يَكُونُ عَلَقَةً مِثْلَ ذَلِكَ، ثُمَّ يَكُونُ مُضْغَةً مِثْلَ ذَلِكَ، ثُمَّ يُرْسِلُ إِلَيْهِ الْمَلَكُ فَيَنْفُخُ فِيهِ الرُّوحَ، وَيُؤْمَرُ بِأَرْبَعِ كَلِمَاتٍ: رِزْقِهِ، وَأَجَلِهِ، وَعَمَلِهِ، وَهَلْ هُوَ شَقِيٌّ أَوْ سَعِيدٌ، فَوَالَّذِي لَا إِلَهَ غَيْرُهُ، إِنَّ أَحَدَكُمْ لَيَعْمَلُ بِعَمَلِ أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ حَتَّى مَا يَكُونُ بَيْنَهُ وَبَيْنَهَا إِلَّا ذِرَاعٌ، فَيَسْبِقُ عَلَيْهِ الْكِتَابُ، فَيُخْتَمُ لَهُ بِعَمَلِ أَهْلِ النَّارِ فَيَدْخُلَهَا، وَإِنَّ الرَّجُلَ لَيَعْمَلُ بِعَمَلِ أَهْلِ النَّارِ، حَتَّى مَا يَكُونُ بَيْنَهُ وَبَيْنَهَا إِلَّا ذِرَاعٌ، فَيَسْبِقُ عَلَيْهِ الْكِتَابُ، فَيُخْتَمُ لَهُ بِعَمَلِ أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ فَيَدْخُلُهَا".

أَخْرَجَاهُ مِنْ حَدِيثِ سليمانَ بْنِ مِهْرَان الْأَعْمَشِ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ سِنَان، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو مُعَاوِيَةَ عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ، عَنْ خَيْثَمَة قَالَ: قَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ -يَعْنِي: ابْنَ مَسْعُودٍ-إِنَّ النُّطْفَةَ إِذَا وَقَعَتْ فِي الرَّحِمِ، طَارَتْ فِي كُلِّ شَعْرٍ وَظُفْرٍ، فَتَمْكُثُ أَرْبَعِينَ يَوْمًا، ثُمَّ تَتَحَدَّرُ فِي الرَّحِمِ فَتَكُونُ عَلَقَةً.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا حُسَيْنُ بْنُ الْحَسَنِ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو كُدَيْنة، عَنْ عَطَاءِ بْنِ السَّائِبِ، عَنِ الْقَاسِمُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ قَالَ: مَرَّ يَهُودِيٌّ بِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَهُوَ يُحَدِّثُ أَصْحَابَهُ، فَقَالَتْ قُرَيْشٌ: يَا يَهُودِيُّ، إِنَّ هَذَا يَزعمُ أَنَّهُ نَبِيٌّ. فَقَالَ: لَأَسْأَلَنَّهُ عَنْ شَيْءٍ لَا يَعْلَمُهُ إِلَّا نَبِيٌّ. قَالَ: فَجَاءَهُ حَتَّى جَلَسَ، فَقَالَ: يَا مُحَمَّدُ، مِمَّ يُخْلَقُ الإنسان؟ فقال: "يا يهودي، من كلٍّ يُخْلَقُ، مِنْ نُطْفَةِ الرَّجُلِ وَمِنْ نُطْفَةِ الْمَرْأَةِ، فَأَمَّا نُطْفَةُ الرَّجُلِ فَنُطْفَةٌ غَلِيظَةٌ مِنْهَا الْعَظْمُ والعَصَب، وَأَمَّا نُطْفَةُ الْمَرْأَةِ فَنُطْفَةٌ رَقِيقَةٌ مِنْهَا اللَّحْمُ وَالدَّمُ" فَقَامَ الْيَهُودِيُّ فَقَالَ: هَكَذَا كَانَ يَقُولُ مَنْ قَبْلَكَ. 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ عَنْ عَمْرٍو، عَنْ أَبِي الطُّفَيْل، حُذَيْفَة بْنِ أُسَيْد الْغِفَارِيِّ قَالَ: سمعتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "يَدْخُلُ المَلك عَلَى النُّطْفَةِ بَعْدَ مَا تَسْتَقِرُّ فِي الرَّحِمِ بِأَرْبَعِينَ لَيْلَةً، فَيَقُولُ: يَا رَبِّ، مَاذَا؟ أَشَقِيٌّ أَمْ سَعِيدٌ؟ أَذَكَرٌ أَمْ أُنْثَى؟ فَيَقُولُ اللَّهُ، فَيَكْتُبَانِ . فَيَقُولَانِ: مَاذَا؟ أَذَكَرٌ أَمْ أُنْثَى؟ فَيَقُولُ اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، فَيَكْتُبَانِ ويُكْتَبُ عَمَلُهُ، وَأَثَرُهُ، وَمُصِيبَتُهُ، وَرِزْقُهُ، ثُمَّ تُطْوَى الصَّحِيفَةُ، فَلَا يُزاد عَلَى مَا فِيهَا وَلَا يُنْقَصُ".

وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ فِي صَحِيحِهِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ سُفْيَانَ بْنِ عُيَيْنَةَ، عَنْ عَمْرٍو -وَهُوَ ابْنُ دِينَارٍ-بِهِ نَحْوَهُ. وَمِنْ طُرَق أخرَى، عَنْ أَبِي الطُّفَيْلِ عَامِرِ بْنِ وَاثِلَةَ، عَنْ حذيفة بن أسيد أَبِي سُرَيْحَةَ الْغِفَارِيِّ بِنَحْوِهِ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ .

وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الْبَزَّارُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ عَبْدَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادُ بْنُ زَيْدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عُبَيْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ أَبِي بَكْرٍ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ؛ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عليه وسلم قال: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ وَكَّلَ بِالرَّحِمِ مَلكًا فَيَقُولُ: أَيْ رَبِّ، نُطْفَةٌ. أيْ رَبِّ، عَلَقَةٌ أَيْ رَبِّ، مُضْغَةٌ. فَإِذَا أَرَادَ اللَّهُ خَلْقَهَا قَالَ: يَا رب، ذكر أو أنثى؟ شقي أو سعيد؟ فَمَا الرِّزْقُ وَالْأَجَلُ؟ " قَالَ: "فَذَلِكَ يُكْتَبُ فِي بَطْنِ أُمِّهِ".

أَخْرَجَاهُ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ مِنْ حَدِيثِ حَمَّادِ بْنِ زَيْدٍ بِهِ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَتَبَارَكَ اللَّهُ أَحْسَنُ الْخَالِقِينَ﴾ يَعْنِي: حِينَ ذَكَرَ قُدْرَتَهُ وَلُطْفَهُ فِي خَلْقِ هَذِهِ النُّطْفَةِ مِنْ حَالٍ إِلَى حَالٍ، وَشَكْلٍ إِلَى شَكْلٍ، حَتَّى تَصَوَّرَتْ إِلَى مَا صَارَتْ إِلَيْهِ مِنَ الْإِنْسَانِ السَّوِيّ الْكَامِلِ الْخَلْقِ، قَالَ: ﴿فَتَبَارَكَ اللَّهُ أَحْسَنُ الْخَالِقِينَ﴾

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا يُونُسُ بْنُ حَبِيبٍ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو دَاوُدَ، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادُ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ زَيْدٍ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ، قَالَ: قَالَ عُمَرُ -يَعْنِي: ابْنَ الْخَطَّابِ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ-: وَافَقْتُ رَبِّي وَوَافَقَنِي فِي أَرْبَعٍ: نَزَلَتْ هذه الآية: ﴿وَلَقَدْ خَلَقْنَا الإنْسَانَ مِنْ سُلالَةٍ مِنْ طِينٍ﴾ الْآيَةَ، قُلْتُ أَنَا: فَتَبَارَكَ اللَّهُ أَحْسَنُ الْخَالِقِينَ. فَنَزَلَتْ: ﴿فَتَبَارَكَ اللَّهُ أَحْسَنُ الْخَالِقِينَ﴾

وَقَالَ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا آدَمُ بْنُ أَبِي إِيَاسٍ، حَدَّثَنَا شَيْبَان، عَنْ جَابِرٍ الجُعْفِي، عَنْ عَامِرٍ الشَّعْبِيِّ، عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ ثَابِتٍ الْأَنْصَارِيِّ قَالَ: أَمْلَى عليَّ رسولُ اللَّهِ هَذِهِ الآية: ﴿وَلَقَدْ خَلَقْنَا الإنْسَانَ مِنْ سُلالَةٍ مِنْ طِينٍ﴾ إِلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿خَلْقًا آخَرَ﴾ ، فَقَالَ مُعَاذٌ: ﴿فَتَبَارَكَ اللَّهُ أَحْسَنُ الْخَالِقِينَ﴾ ، فَضَحِكَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ. فَقَالَ لَهُ مُعَاذٌ: مِمَّ ضَحِكْتَ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ؟ قَالَ: "بِهَا خُتِمَتْ ﴿فَتَبَارَكَ اللَّهُ أَحْسَنُ الْخَالِقِينَ﴾ .

جَابِرُ بْنُ يَزِيدَ الجُعْفِي ضَعِيفٌ جِدًّا، وَفِي خَبَرِهِ هَذَا نَكَارة شَديدة، وَذَلِكَ أَنَّ هَذِهِ السُّورَةَ مَكِّيَّةٌ، وَزَيْدُ بْنُ ثَابِتٍ إِنَّمَا كَتَبَ الْوَحْيَ بِالْمَدِينَةِ، وَكَذَلِكَ إِسْلَامُ مُعَاذِ بْنِ جَبَلٍ إِنَّمَا كَانَ بِالْمَدِينَةِ أَيْضًا، فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿ثُمَّ إِنَّكُمْ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ لَمَيِّتُونَ﴾ يَعْنِي: بَعْدَ هَذِهِ النَّشْأَةِ الْأُولَى مِنَ الْعَدَمِ تَصيرون إِلَى الْمَوْتِ، ﴿ثُمَّ إِنَّكُمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ تُبْعَثُونَ﴾ يَعْنِي: النَّشْأَةَ الْآخِرَةَ، ﴿ثُمَّ اللَّهُ يُنْشِئُ النَّشْأَةَ الآخِرَةَ﴾ [الْعَنْكَبُوتِ:٢٠] يَعْنِي: يَوْمَ الْمَعَادِ، وَقِيَامَ الْأَرْوَاحِ وَالْأَجْسَادِ، فَيُحَاسِبُ الْخَلَائِقَ، وَيُوَفِّي كُلَّ عَامِلٍ عَمَلَهُ، إِنْ خَيْرًا فَخَيْرٌ، وَإِنَّ شَرًّا فَشَرٌّ.

---

## 23:17 — verse 17

### Translation

When the Exalted mentioned the creation of man, He followed it with the mention of the creation of the seven heavens. The Exalted frequently mentions the creation of the heavens and the earth together with the creation of man, as He, the Exalted, said: {The creation of the heavens and the earth is indeed greater than the creation of mankind} [Ghafir: 57]. And likewise at the beginning of {Alif Lam Mim} of al-Sajdah, which the Messenger of Allah ﷺ used to recite on the morning of Friday, at its start is the creation of the heavens and the earth, then the explanation of the creation of man from an extract of clay, and in it is the matter of the resurrection and recompense, and other purposes besides that.

As for His saying: {seven paths}, Mujahid said: it means the seven heavens. This is like His saying, the Exalted: {The seven heavens and the earth and whoever is in them glorify Him} [al-Isra: 44], {Do you not see how Allah has created seven heavens in layers} [Nuh: 15], {Allah is He who created seven heavens and of the earth their like, the command descends between them so that you may know that Allah has power over all things and that Allah has encompassed all things in knowledge} [al-Talaq: 12]. And likewise He said here: {And We have indeed created above you seven paths, and We are not unaware of the creation}, meaning: He knows what enters into the earth and what comes out of it, and what descends from the sky and what ascends into it, and He is with you wherever you are, and Allah is Seeing of what you do. He, Glorified is He, is not veiled from any heaven by another heaven, nor any earth by another earth, and there is no mountain but He knows what is in its rugged terrain, and no sea but He knows what is in its depth. He knows the number of what is in the mountains, the hills, the sands, the seas, the deserts, and the trees, {And not a leaf falls but He knows it, nor a grain in the darkness of the earth, nor anything moist or dry, but it is in a clear record} [al-An'am: 59].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لَمَّا ذَكَرَ تَعَالَى خَلْق الْإِنْسَانِ، عَطَفَ بِذِكْرِ خَلْقِ السموات السبع، وكثيرًا ما يذكر تعالى خلق السموات وَالْأَرْضِ مَعَ خَلْقِ الْإِنْسَانِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿لَخَلْقُ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ أَكْبَرُ مِنْ خَلْقِ النَّاسِ﴾ [غَافِرٍ:٥٧] . وَهَكَذَا فِي أَوَّلِ ﴿الم﴾ السَّجْدَةِ، الَّتِي كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقْرَأُ بِهَا [فِي] صَبِيحَةِ يَوْمِ الْجُمُعَةِ، فِي أولها خَلْقُ السموات وَالْأَرْضِ، ثُمَّ بَيَانُ خَلْقِ الْإِنْسَانِ مِنْ سُلَالَةٍ مِنْ طِينٍ، وَفِيهَا أَمْرُ الْمَعَادِ وَالْجَزَاءِ، وَغَيْرُ ذَلِكَ مِنَ الْمَقَاصِدِ.

فَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿سَبْعَ طَرَائِقَ﴾ : قَالَ مجاهد: يعني السموات السَّبْعَ، وَهَذِهِ كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿تُسَبِّحُ لَهُ السَّمَاوَاتُ السَّبْعُ وَالأرْضُ وَمَنْ فِيهِنَّ﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ٤٤] ، ﴿أَلَمْ تَرَوْا كَيْفَ خَلَقَ اللَّهُ سَبْعَ سَمَاوَاتٍ طِبَاقًا﴾ [نُوحٍ:١٥] ، ﴿اللَّهُ الَّذِي خَلَقَ سَبْعَ سَمَاوَاتٍ وَمِنَ الأرْضِ مِثْلَهُنَّ يَتَنزلُ الأمْرُ بَيْنَهُنَّ لِتَعْلَمُوا أَنَّ اللَّهَ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ وَأَنَّ اللَّهَ قَدْ أَحَاطَ بِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ عِلْمًا﴾ [الطَّلَاقِ:١٢] . وَهَكَذَا قَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿وَلَقَدْ خَلَقْنَا فَوْقَكُمْ سَبْعَ طَرَائِقَ وَمَا كُنَّا عَنِ الْخَلْقِ غَافِلِينَ﴾ أي: ويعلم مَا يَلِجُ فِي الْأَرْضِ وَمَا يَخْرُجُ مِنْهَا، وَمَا يَنْزِلُ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ وَمَا يعرُج فِيهَا، وَهُوَ مَعَكُمْ أَيْنَمَا كُنْتُمْ، وَاللَّهُ بِمَا تَعْمَلُونَ بَصِيرٌ. وَهُوَ -سُبْحَانَهُ-لَا يَحجبُ عَنْهُ سَمَاءٌ سَمَاءً، وَلَا أَرْضٌ أَرْضًا، وَلَا جَبَلٌ إِلَّا يَعْلَمُ مَا فِي وَعْره، وَلَا بَحْرٌ إِلَّا يَعْلَمُ مَا فِي قَعْره، يَعْلَمُ عَدَدَ مَا فِي الْجِبَالِ وَالتِّلَالِ وَالرِّمَالِ، وَالْبِحَارِ وَالْقِفَارِ وَالْأَشْجَارِ، ﴿وَمَا تَسْقُطُ مِنْ وَرَقَةٍ إِلا يَعْلَمُهَا وَلا حَبَّةٍ فِي ظُلُمَاتِ الأرْضِ وَلا رَطْبٍ وَلا يَابِسٍ إِلا فِي كِتَابٍ مُبِينٍ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ٥٩] .

---

## 23:18-22 — verses 18-22 (shared commentary)

### Translation

He, exalted, mentions His favors upon His servants, which cannot be counted or enumerated, in His sending down the rain from the sky {in measure}, that is, according to need: not so much that it would corrupt the land and its cultivation, nor so little that it would not suffice the crops and fruits, but rather in the measure of what is needed for irrigation, drinking, and benefiting from it. So much so that the lands which need much water for their cultivation, but whose soil cannot tolerate rain falling directly upon it, He drives water to them from other countries, as in the land of Egypt, which is called "the barren land" (al-ard al-juruz). God drives to it the water of the Nile, carrying with it red silt which it sweeps up from the lands of Abyssinia during their rainy season. The water comes bearing red silt and waters the land of Egypt, and the silt settles upon their land so that they may cultivate it, because their land is salt-flat and dominated by sand. Glory be to the Subtle, the All-Aware, the Merciful, the Forgiving.

His saying, {and We made it settle in the earth}: meaning, We made the water, when it descends from the clouds, remain lodged in the earth, and We placed in the earth a capacity to receive it, so that it drinks it in and the grain and seed-kernels within it are nourished by it.

His saying, {and indeed We are able to take it away}: meaning, if We willed that it should not rain, We would do so. And if We willed, We would divert it away from you to the salt-flats, the wastelands, [and the seas], and the barren deserts, We would do so. And if We willed, We would make it bitter and undrinkable, of no use for drinking or irrigation, We would do so. And if We willed, We would make it not sink into the earth but instead run off across its surface, We would do so. And if We willed, We would make it, once it descends into the earth, sink down to a depth you could not reach and could not benefit from, We would do so. But by His subtle kindness and mercy, He sends down upon you water from the clouds, sweet, fresh, and clear, and makes it settle in the earth, and channels it into springs within the earth, opening up wells and rivers, so that crops and fruits are watered by it, and you and your animals and your livestock drink from it, and you wash yourselves with it and purify yourselves and cleanse yourselves with it. So to Him belongs all praise and all favor.

His saying, {and We caused to grow for you thereby gardens of palms and grapevines}: meaning, We brought forth for you, by means of the water We sent down, {gardens}, that is, orchards and gardens possessing delightful beauty, that is, having a pleasing appearance.

His saying, {of palms and grapevines}: meaning, in them are palms and grapevines. This was what the people of the Hijaz were accustomed to, and there is no difference between a thing and its like; likewise for every people of a region, they have among their fruits, from God's favor upon them, that for which they are incapable of rendering due thanks.

His saying, {for you therein are many fruits}: meaning, of all kinds of fruit, as He said: {He causes to grow for you thereby crops, olives, palms, grapevines, and fruits of every kind} [al-Nahl: 11].

His saying, {and from them you eat}: it is as though this is connected to something implied, its sense being: you look upon its beauty and its ripening, and from it you eat.

His saying, {and a tree that grows out of Mount Sinai}: meaning, the olive tree. And al-Tur means the mountain. Some have said: it is only called Tur when it has trees upon it; if it is bare of them it is called a mountain (jabal), not a Tur. And God knows best. Mount Sinai (Tur Sayna) is Tur Sininin, the mountain upon which God spoke to Moses son of Amran (peace be upon him), along with the mountains around it upon which the olive trees grow.

His saying, {yielding oil}: some have said that the letter "ba" here is extra, its sense being "yielding the oil," as in the Arabs' saying "so-and-so cast down bi-yadihi," meaning "his hand." According to those who take the verb to imply an additional sense, its meaning would be "coming forth with oil" or "bringing oil." Hence He said, {and a condiment}, that is, a seasoning (udm), as Qatada said. {for those who eat}: meaning, in it is what may be benefited from, both oil and seasoning, as Imam Ahmad said:

[chain] from Abu Usayd, whose name was Malik ibn Rabi'ah al-Sa'idi al-Ansari, who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said, "Eat olive oil and anoint yourselves with it, for it is from a blessed tree."

Abd ibn Humayd said in his Musnad and his Tafsir: [chain] from Umar, that the Messenger of God ﷺ said, "Season your food with olive oil and anoint yourselves with it, for it comes forth from a blessed tree."

Al-Tirmidhi and Ibn Majah both narrated it through more than one route from Abd al-Razzaq. Al-Tirmidhi said: it is not known except through his report, and he was inconsistent in it, sometimes mentioning Umar and sometimes not mentioning him.

Abu al-Qasim al-Tabarani said: [chain] who said: I was a guest of Umar ibn al-Khattab on the night of Ashura, and he fed me from a cold camel's head, and he gave us olive oil to eat, and said: this is the blessed olive oil which God mentioned to His Prophet ﷺ.

His saying, {And indeed for you in the cattle is a lesson: We give you drink from what is in their bellies, and for you in them are many benefits, and from them you eat, and upon them and upon ships you are carried}: He, exalted, mentions what He has made for His creation of benefits in cattle. That is, they drink from their milk, which comes forth from between dung and blood, and they eat of their offspring, and they wear clothing from their wool, their fur, and their hair, and they ride upon their backs, and load upon them heavy burdens to distant lands, as He, exalted, said: {and it carries your loads to a land you could not have reached except with great hardship to yourselves; indeed your Lord is Most Kind, Most Merciful} [al-Nahl: 7]. And He, exalted, said: {Have they not seen that We have created for them, among the things Our hands have made, cattle which they possess? And We have subjected them for them, so that some of them they ride and some of them they eat. And for them therein are benefits and drinks, will they not then give thanks?} [Ya-Sin: 71-73].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَذْكُرُ تَعَالَى نِعَمَهُ عَلَى عَبِيدِهِ الَّتِي لَا تُعَدُّ وَلَا تُحْصَى، فِي إِنْزَالِهِ القَطْر مِنَ السَّمَاءِ ﴿بِقَدَرٍ﴾ أَيْ: بِحَسْبِ الْحَاجَةِ، لَا كَثِيرًا فَيُفْسِدُ الْأَرْضَ وَالْعُمْرَانَ، وَلَا قَلِيلًا فَلَا يَكْفِي الزُّرُوعَ وَالثِّمَارَ، بَلْ بِقَدْرِ الْحَاجَةِ إِلَيْهِ مِنَ السَّقْيِ وَالشُّرْبِ وَالِانتِفَاعِ بِهِ، حَتَّى إِنَّ الْأَرَاضِيَ الَّتِي تَحْتَاجُ مَاءً كَثِيرًا لِزَرْعِهَا وَلَا تَحْتَمِلُ دِمْنتها إِنْزَالَ الْمَطَرِ عَلَيْهَا، يَسُوقُ إِلَيْهَا الْمَاءَ مِنْ بِلَادٍ أُخْرَى، كَمَا فِي أَرْضِ مِصْرَ، وَيُقَالُ لَهَا: "الْأَرْضُ الجرُز"، يَسُوقُ اللَّهُ إِلَيْهَا مَاءَ النِّيلِ مَعَهُ طِينٌ أَحْمَرُ يَجْتَرِفُهُ مِنْ بِلَادِ الْحَبَشَةِ فِي زَمَانِ أَمْطَارِهَا، فَيَأْتِي الْمَاءُ يَحْمِلُ طِينًا أَحْمَرَ، فَيَسْقِي أَرْضَ مِصْرَ، وَيَقَرُّ الطِّينُ عَلَى أرضهم ليزدرعوا فِيهِ، لِأَنَّ أَرْضَهُمْ سِبَاخٌ يَغْلِبُ عَلَيْهَا الرِّمَالُ، فَسُبْحَانَ اللَّطِيفِ الْخَبِيرِ الرَّحِيمِ الْغَفُورِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَأَسْكَنَّاهُ فِي الأرْضِ﴾ أَيْ: جَعَلَنَا الْمَاءَ إِذَا نَزَلَ مِنَ السَّحَابِ يَخْلُدُ فِي الْأَرْضِ، وَجَعَلَنَا فِي الْأَرْضِ قابليَّة لَهُ، تَشْرَبُهُ وَيَتَغَذَّى بِهِ مَا فِيهَا مِنَ الْحَبِّ وَالنَّوَى.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِنَّا عَلَى ذَهَابٍ بِهِ لَقَادِرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: لَوْ شِئْنَا أَلَّا تُمْطِرَ لَفَعَلْنَا، وَلَوْ شِئْنَا لَصَرَفْنَاهُ عَنْكُمْ إِلَى السِّبَاخِ وَالْبَرَارِيِّ [وَالْبِحَارِ] وَالْقِفَارِ لَفَعَلْنَا، وَلَوْ شِئْنَا لَجَعَلْنَاهُ أُجَاجًا لَا يُنْتَفَعُ بِهِ لشُرب وَلَا لِسَقْيٍ لَفَعَلْنَا، وَلَوْ شِئْنَا لَجَعَلْنَاهُ لَا يَنْزِلُ فِي الْأَرْضِ، بَلْ ينجَرّ عَلَى وَجْهِهَا لَفَعَلْنَا. وَلَوْ شِئْنَا لَجَعَلْنَاهُ إِذَا نَزَلَ فِيهَا يَغُورُ إِلَى مَدَى لَا تَصِلُونَ إِلَيْهِ وَلَا تَنْتَفِعُونَ بِهِ لَفَعَلْنَا. وَلَكِنْ بِلُطْفِهِ وَرَحْمَتِهِ يُنَزِّلُ عَلَيْكُمُ الْمَاءَ مِنَ السَّحَابِ عَذْبًا فُرَاتًا زُلَالًا فَيُسْكِنُهُ فِي الْأَرْضِ ويَسْلُكُه يَنَابِيعَ فِي الْأَرْضِ، فَيَفْتَحُ الْعُيُونَ وَالْأَنْهَارَ، فَيَسْقِي بِهِ الزُّرُوعَ وَالثِّمَارَ، وَتَشْرَبُونَ منه ودوابكم وأنعامكم، وتغتسلون منه وتتطهرون وَتَتَنَظَّفُونَ، فَلَهُ الْحَمْدُ وَالْمِنَّةُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَأَنْشَأْنَا لَكُمْ بِهِ جَنَّاتٍ مِنْ نَخِيلٍ وَأَعْنَابٍ﴾ يَعْنِي: فَأَخْرَجْنَا لَكُمْ بِمَا أَنْزَلْنَا مِنَ الْمَاءِ ﴿جَنَّاتٍ﴾ أَيْ: بَسَاتِينَ وَحَدَائِقَ ذَاتَ بَهْجَةٍ، أَيْ: ذَاتَ مَنْظَرٍ حَسَنٍ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿مِنْ نَخِيلٍ وَأَعْنَابٍ﴾ أَيْ: فِيهَا نَخِيلٌ وَأَعْنَابٌ. وَهَذَا مَا كَانَ يَأْلَفُ أَهْلُ الْحِجَازِ، وَلَا فَرْقَ بَيْنَ الشَّيْءِ وَبَيْنَ نَظِيرِهِ، وَكَذَلِكَ فِي حَقِّ كُلِّ أَهْلِ إِقْلِيمٍ، عِنْدَهُمْ مِنَ الثِّمَارِ مِنْ نِعْمَةِ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِمْ مَا يَعْجِزُون عَنِ الْقِيَامِ بِشُكْرِهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لَكُمْ فِيهَا فَوَاكِهُ كَثِيرَةٌ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ جَمِيعِ الثِّمَارِ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿يُنْبِتُ لَكُمْ بِهِ الزَّرْعَ وَالزَّيْتُونَ وَالنَّخِيلَ وَالأعْنَابَ وَمِنْ كُلِّ الثَّمَرَاتِ﴾ [النَّحْلِ: ١١] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمِنْهَا تَأْكُلُونَ﴾ كَأَنَّهُ مَعْطُوفٌ عَلَى شَيْءٍ مُقَدَّرٍ، تَقْدِيرُهُ: تَنْظُرُونَ إِلَى حُسْنِهِ وَنُضْجِهِ، وَمِنْهُ تَأْكُلُونَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَشَجَرَةً تَخْرُجُ مِنْ طُورِ سَيْنَاءَ﴾ يَعْنِي: الزَّيْتُونَةَ. وَالطُّورُ: هُوَ الْجَبَلُ. وَقَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: إِنَّمَا يُسَمَّى طُورًا إِذَا كَانَ فِيهِ شَجَرٌ، فَإِنْ عَرى عَنْهَا سُمِّيَ جَبَلا لَا طُورًا، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ. وَطُورُ سَيْنَاءَ: هُوَ طُورُ سِينِينَ، وَهُوَ الْجَبَلُ الَّذِي كَلَّم [اللَّهُ] عَلَيْهِ مُوسَى بْنَ عِمْرَانَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَمَا حَوْلَهُ مِنَ الْجِبَالِ الَّتِي فِيهَا شَجَرُ الزَّيْتُونِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿تَنْبُتُ بِالدُّهْنِ﴾ : قَالَ بَعْضُهُمُ: الْبَاءُ زَائِدَةٌ، وَتَقْدِيرُهُ: تَنْبُتُ الدُّهْنَ، كَمَا فِي قَوْلِ الْعَرَبِ: أَلْقَى فَلَانٌ بِيَدِهِ، أَيْ: يَدَهُ. وَأَمَّا عَلَى قَوْلِ مَنْ يُضَمِّن الْفِعْلَ فَتَقْدِيرُهُ: تَخْرُجُ بِالدُّهْنِ، أَوْ تَأْتِي بِالدُّهْنِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَصِبْغٍ﴾ أَيْ: أدْم، قَالَهُ قَتَادَةُ. ﴿لِلآكِلِينَ﴾ أَيْ: فِيهَا مَا يَنْتَفِعُ بِهِ مِنَ الدُّهْنِ وَالِاصْطِبَاغِ، كَمَا قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا وَكِيع، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عِيسَى، عَنْ عَطَاءٍ الشَّامِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِي أسَيْد -وَاسْمُهُ مَالِكُ بْنُ رَبِيعَةَ السَّاعِدِيُّ الْأَنْصَارِيِّ-قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "كُلُوا الزَّيْتَ وَادَّهِنُوا بِهِ ؛ فَإِنَّهُ مِنْ شَجَرَةٍ مُبَارَكَةٍ" .

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ بْنُ حُمَيد فِي مُسْنَدِهِ وَتَفْسِيرُهُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ، أَخْبَرَنَا مَعْمَر، عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ عُمَرَ؛ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "ائْتَدِمُوا بِالزَّيْتِ وَادَّهِنُوا بِهِ، فَإِنَّهُ يَخْرُجُ مِنْ شَجَرَةٍ مُبَارَكَةٍ".

وَرَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ مِنْ غَيْرِ وَجْهٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّزَّاقِ . قَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: وَلَا يُعْرَفُ إلا من حَدِيثِهِ، وَكَانَ يَضْطَرِبُ فِيهِ، فَرُبَّمَا ذَكَرَ فِيهِ عُمَرَ وَرُبَّمَا لَمْ يَذْكُرْهُ.

قَالَ أَبُو الْقَاسِمِ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ أَحْمَدَ بْنِ حَنْبَلٍ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ بْنُ عُيَيْنَةَ، حَدَّثَنِي الصَّعْب بْنُ حَكِيمِ بْنِ شَرِيكِ بْنِ نَمْلَةَ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ عَنْ جَدِّهِ، قَالَ: ضِفْت عمرَ بْنَ الْخَطَّابِ لَيْلَةَ عَاشُورَاءَ ، فَأَطْعَمَنِي مِنْ رَأْسِ بَعِيرٍ بَارِدٍ، وَأَطْعَمَنَا زَيْتًا، وَقَالَ: هَذَا الزَّيْتُ الْمُبَارَكُ الَّذِي قَالَ اللَّهُ لِنَبِيِّهِ ﷺ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِنَّ لَكُمْ فِي الأنْعَامِ لَعِبْرَةً نُسْقِيكُمْ مِمَّا فِي بُطُونِهَا وَلَكُمْ فِيهَا مَنَافِعُ كَثِيرَةٌ وَمِنْهَا تَأْكُلُونَ وَعَلَيْهَا وَعَلَى الْفُلْكِ تُحْمَلُونَ﴾ : يَذْكُرُ تَعَالَى مَا جَعَلَ لِخَلْقِهِ فِي الْأَنْعَامِ مِنَ الْمَنَافِعِ، وَذَلِكَ أَنَّهُمْ يَشْرَبُونَ مِنْ ألْبَانِهَا الْخَارِجَةِ مِنْ بَيْنِ فرْث وَدَمٍ، وَيَأْكُلُونَ مِنْ حُمْلَانِهَا، وَيَلْبَسُونَ مِنْ أَصْوَافِهَا وَأَوْبَارِهَا وَأَشْعَارِهَا، وَيَرْكَبُونَ ظُهُورَهَا وُيُحَمِّلُونَهَا الْأَحْمَالَ الثِّقَالَ إِلَى الْبِلَادِ النَّائِيَةِ عَنْهُمْ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَتَحْمِلُ أَثْقَالَكُمْ إِلَى بَلَدٍ لَمْ تَكُونُوا بَالِغِيهِ إِلا بِشِقِّ الأنْفُسِ إِنَّ رَبَّكُمْ لَرَءُوفٌ رَحِيمٌ﴾ [النَّحْلِ: ٧] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَوَلَمْ يَرَوْا أَنَّا خَلَقْنَا لَهُمْ مِمَّا عَمِلَتْ أَيْدِينَا أَنْعَامًا فَهُمْ لَهَا مَالِكُونَ. وَذَلَّلْنَاهَا لَهُمْ فَمِنْهَا رَكُوبُهُمْ وَمِنْهَا يَأْكُلُونَ. وَلَهُمْ فِيهَا مَنَافِعُ وَمَشَارِبُ أَفَلا يَشْكُرُونَ﴾ [يس: ٧١-٧٣] .

---

## 23:23-25 — verses 23-25 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs us about Noah (peace be upon him), when He sent him to his people to warn them of God's punishment and His severe might, and His vengeance against whoever ascribed partners to Him, opposed His command, and denied His messengers: {So he said: O my people, worship God, you have no god other than Him. Will you not then fear Him?} meaning: do you not fear God regarding your associating partners with Him?!

The notables said, and they were the chiefs and great men among them: {This is nothing but a man like yourselves who wishes to exalt himself above you}, meaning: he wants to rise above you and make himself great through the claim of prophethood, while he is a human being just like you. So how could revelation have come to him and not to you? {And if God had willed, He would have sent down angels}, meaning: if He had wished to send a prophet, He would have sent an angel from His presence and it would not have been a human being! {We have not heard of this}, meaning: of a human being being sent as a messenger, among our forefathers of old. By this they meant their predecessors, their ancestors, and the nations that had passed.

His saying: {He is nothing but a man possessed by madness}, meaning: mad, according to their claim, in asserting that God sent him to you and singled him out from among you with revelation. {So wait concerning him for a time}, meaning: wait for the misfortune of death to overtake him, and be patient regarding him for a period until you are relieved of him.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ نُوحٍ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، حِينَ بَعَثَهُ إِلَى قَوْمِهِ، لِيُنْذِرَهُمْ عَذَابَ اللَّهِ وَبَأْسَهُ الشَّدِيدَ، وَانتِقَامَهُ مِمَّنْ أَشْرَكَ بِهِ وَخَالَفَ أَمْرَهُ وَكَذَّبَ رُسُلَهُ، ﴿فَقَالَ يَا قَوْمِ اعْبُدُوا اللَّهَ مَا لَكُمْ مِنْ إِلَهٍ غَيْرُهُ أَفَلا تَتَّقُونَ﴾ أَيْ: أَلَا تَخَافُونَ مِنَ اللَّهِ فِي إِشْرَاكِكُمْ بِهِ؟!

فَقَالَ الْمَلَأُ -وَهُمُ السَّادَةُ وَالْأَكَابِرُ مِنْهُمْ-: ﴿مَا هَذَا إِلا بَشَرٌ مِثْلُكُمْ يُرِيدُ أَنْ يَتَفَضَّلَ عَلَيْكُمْ﴾ يَعْنُونَ: يَتَرَفَّعُ عَلَيْكُمْ وَيَتَعَاظَمُ بِدَعْوَى النُّبُوَّةِ، وَهُوَ بَشَرٌ مِثْلُكُمْ. فَكَيْفَ أُوحِيَ إِلَيْهِ دُونَكُمْ؟ ﴿وَلَوْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ لأنزلَ مَلائِكَةً﴾ أَيْ: لَوْ أَرَادَ أَنْ يَبْعَثَ نَبِيًّا، لَبَعَثَ مَلَكًا مِنْ عِنْدِهِ وَلَمْ يَكُنْ بَشَرًا! ﴿مَا سَمِعْنَا بِهَذَا﴾ أَيْ: بِبَعْثَةِ الْبَشَرِ فِي آبَائِنَا الْأَوَّلِينَ. يَعْنُونَ بهذا أسلافهم وأجدادهم والأمم الماضية.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنْ هُوَ إِلا رَجُلٌ بِهِ جِنَّةٌ﴾ أَيْ: مَجْنُونٌ فِيمَا يَزْعُمُهُ، مِنْ أَنَّ اللَّهَ أَرْسَلَهُ إِلَيْكُمْ، وَاخْتَصَّهُ مِنْ بَيْنِكُمْ بِالْوَحْيِ ﴿فَتَرَبَّصُوا بِهِ حَتَّى حِينٍ﴾ أَيِ: انتَظِرُوا بِهِ رَيْبَ الْمَنُونِ، وَاصْبِرُوا عَلَيْهِ مُدَّةً حَتَّى تَسْتَرِيحُوا مِنْهُ.

---

## 23:26-30 — verses 26-30 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing about Nuh (peace be upon him), that he called upon his Lord seeking His help against his people, as the Almighty says, informing about him, in the other verse: {So he called upon his Lord, "I am overcome, so help me"} [al-Qamar: 10]. And He says here: {[He said], "My Lord, help me because they have denied me."} At that point, Allah the Almighty commanded him to build the ship, to make it sound and well-constructed, and to carry in it two of every pair, that is, a male and a female from every kind of animal, plant, fruit, and other things, and to carry in it his family, {except him against whom the word has already gone forth}, that is, the one concerning whom the decree of Allah for destruction had already preceded, and they were those among his family who did not believe in him, such as his son and his wife. And Allah knows best.

His saying: {And do not address Me concerning those who have wronged; indeed, they are to be drowned} means: at the moment of witnessing the descent of the great rain, let no compassion for your people take hold of you, nor pity for them, nor hope of delaying them so that perhaps they might believe. For I have decreed that they shall be drowned, given the state of disbelief and transgression they are in. The story has already been given in full in Surat Hud, in a manner that makes it unnecessary to repeat here.

His saying: {And when you and those with you have settled on the ship, say: "Praise be to Allah who saved us from the wrongdoing people"}, is like His saying: {And He has made for you ships and cattle on which you ride. That you may settle yourselves upon their backs and then remember the favor of your Lord when you have settled upon them, and say: "Exalted is He who has subjected this to us, and we could not have done it ourselves. And indeed, to our Lord we will return"} [al-Zukhruf: 12-14]. Nuh (peace be upon him) complied with this, as the Almighty says: {And he said, "Embark in it; in the name of Allah is its course and its anchorage"} [Hud: 41]. So he mentioned Allah the Almighty at the beginning of its voyage and at its end. And the Almighty says: {And say, "My Lord, let me land at a blessed landing place, and You are the best of those who bring to land."}

His saying: {Indeed, in that are signs} means: indeed, in this deed, that is, the saving of the believers and the destruction of the disbelievers, {are signs}, that is, clear proofs and evidences of the truthfulness of the prophets in what they brought from Allah the Almighty, and that He, the Almighty, does whatever He wills, and that He is able over all things, and knowing of all things.

His saying: {And indeed, We were to test} means: We were indeed to test the servants by sending the messengers.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ نُوحٍ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، أَنَّهُ دَعَا رَبَّهُ يَسْتَنْصِرُهُ عَلَى قَوْمِهِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا [عَنْهُ] فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿فَدَعَا رَبَّهُ أَنِّي مَغْلُوبٌ فَانْتَصِرْ﴾ [الْقَمَرِ: ١٠] ، وَقَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿ [قَالَ] رَبِّ انْصُرْنِي بِمَا كَذَّبُونِ﴾ فَعِنْدَ ذَلِكَ أَمَرَهُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى بِصَنْعَةِ السَّفِينَةِ وَإِحْكَامِهَا وَإِتْقَانِهَا، وَأَنْ يَحْمِلَ فِيهَا مِنْ كُلٍّ زَوْجَيْنِ اثْنَيْنِ، أَيْ: ذَكَرًا وَأُنْثَى مِنْ كُلِّ صِنْفٍ مِنَ الْحَيَوَاناتِ وَالنَّبَاتَاتِ وَالثِّمَارِ، وَغَيْرِ ذَلِكَ، وَأَنْ يَحْمِلَ فِيهَا أَهْلَهُ ﴿إِلا مَنْ سَبَقَ عَلَيْهِ الْقَوْلُ﴾ أَيْ: سَبَقَ فِيهِ الْقَوْلُ مِنَ اللَّهِ بِالْهَلَاكِ، وَهُمُ الَّذِينَ لَمْ يُؤْمِنُوا بِهِ مِنْ أَهْلِهِ، كَابْنِهِ وَزَوْجَتِهِ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلا تُخَاطِبْنِي فِي الَّذِينَ ظَلَمُوا إِنَّهُمْ مُغْرَقُونَ﴾ أَيْ: عِنْدَ مُعَايَنَةِ إِنْزَالِ الْمَطَرِ الْعَظِيمِ، لَا تَأْخُذَنَّكَ رَأْفَةٌ بِقَوْمِكَ، وَشَفَقَةٌ عَلَيْهِمْ، وطَمَع فِي تَأْخِيرِهِمْ لَعَلَّهُمْ يُؤْمِنُونَ، فَإِنِّي قَدْ قَضَيْتُ أَنَّهُمْ مُغْرَقُونَ عَلَى مَا هُمْ عَلَيْهِ مِنَ الْكُفْرِ وَالطُّغْيَانِ. وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَتِ الْقِصَّةُ مَبْسُوطَةً فِي سُورَةِ "هُودٍ" بِمَا يُغْنِي عَنْ إِعَادَةِ ذَلِكَ هَاهُنَا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَإِذَا اسْتَوَيْتَ أَنْتَ وَمَنْ مَعَكَ عَلَى الْفُلْكِ فَقُلِ الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ الَّذِي نَجَّانَا مِنَ الْقَوْمِ الظَّالِمِينَ﴾ ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَجَعَلَ لَكُمْ مِنَ الْفُلْكِ وَالأنْعَامِ مَا تَرْكَبُونَ. لِتَسْتَوُوا عَلَى ظُهُورِهِ ثُمَّ تَذْكُرُوا نِعْمَةَ رَبِّكُمْ إِذَا اسْتَوَيْتُمْ عَلَيْهِ وَتَقُولُوا سُبْحَانَ الَّذِي سَخَّرَ لَنَا هَذَا وَمَا كُنَّا لَهُ مُقْرِنِينَ. وَإِنَّا إِلَى رَبِّنَا لَمُنْقَلِبُونَ﴾ [الزُّخْرُفِ: ١٢-١٤] . وَقَدِ امْتَثَلَ نُوحٌ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، هَذَا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَقَالَ ارْكَبُوا فِيهَا بِسْمِ اللَّهِ مَجْرَاهَا وَمُرْسَاهَا﴾ [هُودٍ:٤١] . فذَكَر اللهَ تَعَالَى عِنْدَ ابْتِدَاءِ سَيْرِهِ وَعِنْدَ انْتِهَائِهِ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَقُلْ رَبِّ أَنزلْنِي مُنزلا مُبَارَكًا وَأَنْتَ خَيْرُ الْمُنزلِينَ﴾ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّ فِي ذَلِكَ لآيَاتٍ﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّ فِي هَذَا الصَّنِيعِ -وَهُوَ إِنْجَاءُ المؤمنين وإهلاك الكافرين- ﴿لآيَاتٍ﴾ أَيْ: لَحُجَجًا وَدَلَالَاتٍ وَاضِحَاتٍ عَلَى صِدْقِ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ فِيمَا جَاءُوا بِهِ عَنِ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى، وَأَنَّهُ تَعَالَى فَاعِلٌ لِمَا يَشَاءُ، وَقَادِرٌ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ، عَلِيمٌ بِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِنْ كُنَّا لَمُبْتَلِينَ﴾ أَيْ: لَمُخْتَبِرِينَ لِلْعِبَادِ بِإِرْسَالِ الْمُرْسَلِينَ.

---

## 23:31-41 — verses 31-41 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs that He raised up, after the people of Nuh, another generation. It is said that what is meant by them is 'Ad, for they were made successors after them. It is also said that what is meant by these is Thamud, on account of His saying {Then the shout seized them in truth}. And that He, Exalted is He, sent among them a messenger from among themselves, who called them to worship God alone, without partner. But they denied him and opposed him, and refused to follow him because he was a human being like themselves, and disdained to follow a human messenger. So they denied the meeting with God on the Day of Resurrection, and rejected the bodily resurrection, and said: {Does he promise you that when you die and become dust and bones, you will be brought forth? Far off, far off is that which you are promised}, meaning: that is far off, far off.

{He is only a man who has fabricated a lie against God}, meaning: regarding what he brought you of the message, the warning, and the report of the resurrection. {And we are not believers in him.
