He said: My Lord, help me because they have denied me}, meaning: the messenger sought victory over them and sought his Lord's aid against them, and He answered his supplication. {He said: In a little while they will surely become regretful}, meaning: because of their opposition and stubbornness regarding what he brought them,

{Then the shout seized them in truth}, meaning: and they deserved that from God because of their disbelief and their transgression.

The apparent meaning is that a shout gathered against them together with the cold, powerful, raging wind, {destroying everything by the command of its Lord, so they became such that nothing could be seen except their dwellings} [al-Ahqaf: 25].

And His saying: {So We made them as scum}, meaning: fallen, destroyed, like the scum of a flood, which is that worthless, insignificant, perishing thing from which no benefit can be derived. {So away with the wrongdoing people}, like His saying: {And We did not wrong them, but it was they who were the wrongdoers} [al-Zukhruf: 76], meaning: because of their disbelief, their stubbornness, and their opposition to the messenger of God. So let those who hear beware of denying their messenger.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ أَنْشَأَ بَعْدَ قَوْمِ نُوحٍ قَرْنًا آخَرِينَ -قِيلَ: الْمُرَادُ بِهِمْ عَادٌ، فَإِنَّهُمْ كَانُوا مُسْتَخْلَفِينَ بَعْدَهُمْ. وَقِيلَ: الْمُرَادُ بِهَؤُلَاءِ ثَمُودُ؛ لِقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَأَخَذَتْهُمُ الصَّيْحَةُ بِالْحَقِّ﴾ -وَأَنَّهُ تَعَالَى أَرْسَلَ فِيهِمْ رَسُولًا مِنْهُمْ، فَدَعَاهُمْ إِلَى عِبَادَةِ اللَّهِ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ. فَكَذَّبُوهُ وَخَالَفُوهُ، وَأَبَوْا مِنَ اتِّبَاعِهِ لِكَوْنِهِ بَشَرًا مِثْلَهُمْ، وَاسْتَنْكَفُوا عَنِ اتِّبَاعِ رَسُولٍ بَشَرِيٍّ، فَكَذَّبُوا بِلِقَاءِ اللَّهِ فِي الْقِيَامَةِ، وَأَنْكَرُوا الْمَعَادَ الْجُثْمَانِيَّ، وَقَالُوا ﴿أَيَعِدُكُمْ أَنَّكُمْ إِذَا مِتُّمْ وَكُنْتُمْ تُرَابًا وَعِظَامًا أَنَّكُمْ مُخْرَجُونَ. هَيْهَاتَ هَيْهَاتَ لِمَا تُوعَدُونَ﴾ أَيْ: بَعِيدٌ بَعِيدٌ ذَلِكَ.

﴿إِنْ هُوَ إِلا رَجُلٌ افْتَرَى عَلَى اللَّهِ كَذِبًا﴾ أَيْ: فِيمَا جَاءَكُمْ بِهِ مِنَ الرِّسَالَةِ وَالنِّذَارَةِ وَالْإِخْبَارِ بِالْمَعَادِ. ﴿وَمَا نَحْنُ لَهُ بِمُؤْمِنِينَ. قَالَ رَبِّ انْصُرْنِي بِمَا كَذَّبُونِ﴾ أَيِ: اسْتَفْتَحَ عَلَيْهِمُ الرَّسُولُ واستنصَرَ ربَّه عَلَيْهِمْ، فَأَجَابَ دُعَاءَهُ، ﴿قَالَ عَمَّا قَلِيلٍ لَيُصْبِحُنَّ نَادِمِينَ﴾ أَيْ: بِمُخَالَفَتِكَ وَعِنَادِكَ فِيمَا جِئْتَهُمْ بِهِ،

﴿فَأَخَذَتْهُمُ الصَّيْحَةُ بِالْحَقِّ﴾ أَيْ: وَكَانُوا يَسْتَحِقُّونَ ذَلِكَ مِنَ اللَّهِ لِكُفْرِهِمْ وَطُغْيَانِهِمْ.

وَالظَّاهِرُ أَنَّهُ اجْتَمَعَ عَلَيْهِمْ صَيْحَةٌ مَعَ الرِّيحِ الصَّرْصر الْعَاصِفِ الْقَوِيِّ الْبَارِدَةِ، ﴿تُدَمِّرُ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ بِأَمْرِ رَبِّهَا فَأَصْبَحُوا لَا يُرَى إِلا مَسَاكِنُهُمْ﴾ [الْأَحْقَافِ: ٢٥] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَجَعَلْنَاهُمْ غُثَاءً﴾ أَيْ: صَرْعَى هَلْكى كَغُثَاءِ السَّيْلِ، وَهُوَ الشَّيْءُ الْحَقِيرُ التافه الهالك الذي لَا يُنْتَفَعُ بِشَيْءٍ مِنْهُ. ﴿فَبُعْدًا لِلْقَوْمِ الظَّالِمِينَ﴾ ، كَقَوْلِهِ : ﴿وَمَا ظَلَمْنَاهُمْ وَلَكِنْ كَانُوا هُمُ الظَّالِمِينَ﴾ [الزُّخْرُفِ:٧٦] أَيْ: بِكُفْرِهِمْ وَعِنَادِهِمْ وَمُخَالَفَةِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ، فَلْيَحْذَرِ السَّامِعُونَ أَنْ يُكَذِّبُوا رَسُولَهُمْ.

---

## 23:42-44 — verses 42-44 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says: {Then We raised up after them other generations}, that is, nations and peoples, {No nation can outstrip its term, nor can they delay it}, meaning: rather they are seized according to what He, the Almighty, had decreed for them in the Preserved Tablet (al-Lawh al-Mahfuz) and knew before their coming into being, nation after nation, generation after generation, age after age, and successor after predecessor.

{Then We sent Our messengers in succession}: Ibn Abbas said, meaning one following another. This is like His saying, the Almighty: {And We certainly sent into every nation a messenger, saying: Worship Allah and avoid false gods. Then among them were those whom Allah guided, and among them were those upon whom error was justly decreed} [al-Nahl: 36], and His saying: {Every time a messenger came to a nation, they denied him}, meaning: the majority and the greater part of them, as in His saying, the Almighty: {Alas for the servants! There never came to them a messenger except that they mocked him} [Ya-Sin: 30].

And His saying: {So We caused them to follow one another}, that is, We destroyed them, as in His saying: {And how many generations have We destroyed after Noah} [al-Isra: 17].

{And We made them narratives}, that is, reports and tales for the people, as in His saying: {So We made them narratives and scattered them in complete dispersal} [the verse] [Saba: 19] [{So away with a people who do not believe}].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿ثُمَّ أَنْشَأْنَا مِنْ بَعْدِهِمْ قُرُونًا آخَرِينَ﴾ أَيْ: أَمَّمَا وَخَلَائِقَ، ﴿مَا تَسْبِقُ مِنْ أُمَّةٍ أَجَلَهَا وَمَا يَسْتَأْخِرُونَ﴾ يَعْنِي : بَلْ يُؤْخَذون حَسَب مَا قَدَّرَ لَهُمْ تَعَالَى فِي كِتَابِهِ الْمَحْفُوظِ وَعَلِمَهُ قَبْلَ كَوْنِهِمْ، أُمَّةً بَعْدَ أُمَّةٍ، وَقَرْنًا بَعْدَ قَرْنٍ، وَجِيلًا بَعْدَ جِيلٍ، وخَلفًا بَعْدَ سَلَفٍ.

﴿ثُمَّ أَرْسَلْنَا رُسُلَنَا تَتْرَى﴾ : قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: يَعْنِي يَتْبَعُ بَعْضُهُمْ بَعْضًا. وَهَذِهِ كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَقَدْ بَعَثْنَا فِي كُلِّ أُمَّةٍ رَسُولا أَنِ اُعْبُدُوا اللَّهَ وَاجْتَنِبُوا الطَّاغُوتَ فَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ هَدَى اللَّهُ وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ حَقَّتْ عَلَيْهِ الضَّلالَةُ﴾ [النَّحْلِ: ٣٦] ، وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿كُلَّ مَا جَاءَ أُمَّةً رَسُولُهَا كَذَّبُوهُ﴾ يَعْنِي: جُمْهُورَهُمْ وَأَكْثَرَهُمْ، كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَا حَسْرَةً عَلَى الْعِبَادِ مَا يَأْتِيهِمْ مِنْ رَسُولٍ إِلا كَانُوا بِهِ يَسْتَهْزِئُونَ﴾ [يس:٣٠] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَأَتْبَعْنَا بَعْضَهُمْ بَعْضًا﴾ أَيْ: أَهْلَكْنَاهُمْ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَكَمْ أَهْلَكْنَا مِنَ الْقُرُونِ مِنْ بَعْدِ نُوحٍ﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ١٧] .

﴿وَجَعَلْنَاهُمْ أَحَادِيثَ﴾ أَيْ: أَخْبَارًا وَأَحَادِيثَ لِلنَّاسِ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَجَعَلْنَاهُمْ أَحَادِيثَ وَمَزَّقْنَاهُمْ كُلَّ مُمَزَّقٍ﴾ [الْآيَةَ] [سَبَأٍ: ١٩] [ ﴿فَبُعْدًا لِقَوْمٍ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ ] .

## 23:45-49 — verses 45-49 (shared commentary)

### Translation

God, exalted is He, informs that He sent His messenger Moses (peace be upon him) and his brother Aaron to Pharaoh and his chiefs, with the signs, the crushing proofs, and the decisive demonstrations. And that Pharaoh and his people showed arrogant refusal to follow them and submit to their command, because the two of them were mere human beings, just as the past nations had denied the sending of messengers from among mankind. Their hearts resembled one another. So God destroyed Pharaoh and his chiefs, and drowned them all together in a single day. And He sent down upon Moses the Book, that is the Torah, containing His rulings, His commands, and His prohibitions. That was after God had shattered Pharaoh and the Copts and seized them with the seizing of One mighty and all-powerful. And after God sent down the Torah, He did not destroy any nation in its entirety, but rather commanded the believers to fight the disbelievers, as He, exalted is He, said: {And We certainly gave Moses the Book, after We had destroyed the former generations, as insights for mankind, and guidance and mercy, that they might remember} [al-Qasas: 43].

Then He, exalted is He, said:

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ بَعَثَ رَسُولَهُ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَأَخَاهُ هَارُونَ إِلَى فِرْعَوْنَ وَمَلَئِهِ، بِالْآيَاتِ وَالْحُجَجِ الدَّامِغَاتِ، وَالْبَرَاهِينِ الْقَاطِعَاتِ، وَأَنَّ فِرْعَوْنَ وَقَوْمَهُ اسْتَكْبَرُوا عَنِ اتِّبَاعِهِمَا، وَالِانقِيَادِ لِأَمْرِهِمَا، لِكَوْنِهِمَا بَشرين كَمَا أَنْكَرَتِ الْأُمَمُ الْمَاضِيَةُ بِعْثَةَ الرُّسُلِ مِنَ الْبَشَرِ، تَشَابَهَتْ قُلُوبُهُمْ، فَأَهْلَكَ اللَّهُ فِرْعَوْنَ وَمَلَأَهُ، وَأَغْرَقَهُمْ فِي يَوْمٍ وَاحِدٍ أَجْمَعِينَ، وَأَنْزَلَ عَلَى مُوسَى الْكِتَابَ -وَهُوَ التَّوْرَاةُ-فِيهَا أَحْكَامُهُ وَأَوَامِرُهُ وَنَوَاهِيهِ، وَذَلِكَ بَعْدَ مَا قَصَمَ اللَّهُ فِرْعَوْنَ وَالْقِبْطَ، وأخذهم أخذ عزيز مقتدر؛ وبعد أن أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ التَّوْرَاةَ لَمْ يُهْلِكْ أُمَّةً بِعَامَّةٍ، بَلْ أَمَرَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ بِقِتَالِ الْكَافِرِينَ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَقَدْ آتَيْنَا مُوسَى الْكِتَابَ مِنْ بَعْدِ مَا أَهْلَكْنَا الْقُرُونَ الأولَى بَصَائِرَ لِلنَّاسِ وَهُدًى وَرَحْمَةً لَعَلَّهُمْ يَتَذَكَّرُونَ﴾ [الْقَصَصِ: ٤٣] .

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى:

## 23:50 — verse 50

### Translation

The Exalted says, informing about His servant and messenger Jesus son of Mary (peace be upon them both), that He made the two of them a sign for people: that is, a decisive proof of His power to do as He wills, for He created Adam without father or mother, and created Eve from a male without a female, and created Jesus from a female without a male, and created the rest of mankind from a male and a female.

As for His saying: {And We gave them shelter on a hillock possessed of level ground and flowing water}, al-Dahhak said, on the authority of Ibn Abbas: the rabwah (elevated hillock) is a raised place on the earth, and it is the best place for vegetation to grow. Mujahid, Ikrimah, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, and Qatadah said likewise.

Ibn Abbas said concerning His words {possessed of level ground}: it means possessed of fertility, and {and flowing water} means visible, flowing water.

Mujahid said: a level hillock.

Sa'id ibn Jubayr said: {possessed of level ground and flowing water} means the water was level and settled within it. Mujahid and Qatadah said: {and flowing water} means running water.

The commentators then differed as to the location of this hillock, in which of God's lands it was. Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam said: the elevated hillocks (al-ruba) are found only in Egypt. When the water is released, the villages sit upon the elevated hillocks, and were it not for these hillocks the villages would be drowned.

Something similar was reported from Wahb ibn Munabbih, though this is very far-fetched.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Sa'id ibn al-Musayyab said, concerning the words of the Exalted {And We gave them shelter on a hillock possessed of level ground and flowing water}: it is Damascus.

He said: something similar was reported from Abdullah ibn Salam, al-Hasan, Zayd ibn Aslam, and Khalid ibn Ma'dan.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Ibn Abbas said concerning {possessed of level ground and flowing water}: the rivers of Damascus.

Layth ibn Abi Sulaym said, on the authority of Mujahid, concerning {And We gave them shelter on a hillock [possessed of level ground and flowing water]}: it refers to Jesus son of Mary and his mother, when they took shelter in the Ghutah of Damascus and its surroundings.

Abd al-Razzaq said, [chain] Abu Hurayrah said, concerning His words {on a hillock possessed of level ground and flowing water}: it is al-Ramlah in Palestine.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Murrah al-Bahzi said: I heard the Prophet ﷺ say to a man, "You will die at al-Rabwah," and he died at al-Ramlah. This is a hadith that is gharib (singular) in the extreme.

The closest of these sayings to the truth is what al-Awfi reported from Ibn Abbas concerning His words {And We gave them shelter on a hillock possessed of level ground and flowing water}, who said: al-ma'in (flowing water) is running water, and it is the river which God the Exalted mentioned when He said {Your Lord has placed beneath you a stream} [Maryam: 24].

Al-Dahhak and Qatadah said likewise: {on a hillock possessed of level ground and flowing water} refers to Jerusalem (Bayt al-Maqdis). This, and God knows best, is the most apparent view, because it is what is mentioned in the other verse, and the Qur'an explains itself by itself. This is the most fitting means of interpretation, followed by sound hadiths, then by reports (athar).

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبَرًا عَنْ عَبْدِهِ وَرَسُولِهِ عِيسَى ابْنِ مَرْيَمَ، عَلَيْهِمَا السَّلَامُ، أَنَّهُ جَعَلَهُمَا آيَةً لِلنَّاسِ: أَيْ حُجَّةً قَاطِعَةً عَلَى قُدْرَتِهِ عَلَى مَا يَشَاءُ، فَإِنَّهُ خَلَقَ آدَمَ مِنْ غَيْرِ أَبٍ وَلَا أُمٍّ، وَخَلَقَ حَوَّاءَ مِنْ ذَكَرٍ بِلَا أُنْثَى، وَخَلَقَ عِيسَى مِنْ أُنْثَى بِلَا ذَكَرٍ، وَخَلَقَ بَقِيَّةَ النَّاسِ مِنْ ذَكَرٍ وَأُنْثَى.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَآوَيْنَاهُمَا إِلَى رَبْوَةٍ ذَاتِ قَرَارٍ وَمَعِينٍ﴾ قَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: الرَّبْوَةُ: الْمَكَانُ الْمُرْتَفِعُ مِنَ الْأَرْضِ، وَهُوَ أَحْسَنُ مَا يَكُونُ فِيهِ النَّبَاتُ. وَكَذَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَعِكْرِمَةُ، وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ، وقَتَادَةُ.

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿ذَاتِ قَرَارٍ﴾ يَقُولُ: ذَاتُ خِصْبٍ ﴿وَمَعِينٍ﴾ يَعْنِي: مَاءً ظَاهِرًا .

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: رَبْوَةٌ مُسْتَوِيَةٌ.

وَقَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ: ﴿ذَاتِ قَرَارٍ وَمَعِينٍ﴾ : اسْتَوَى الْمَاءُ فِيهَا. وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وقَتَادَةُ: ﴿وَمَعِينٍ﴾ : الْمَاءُ الْجَارِي.

ثُمَّ اخْتَلَفَ الْمُفَسِّرُونَ فِي مَكَانِ هَذِهِ الرَّبْوَةِ فِي أَيِّ أَرْضِ [اللَّهِ] هِيَ؟ فَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: لَيْسَ الرُّبَى إِلَّا بِمِصْرَ. وَالْمَاءُ حِينَ يُرْسَلُ يَكُونُ الرُّبَى عَلَيْهَا الْقُرَى، وَلَوْلَا الرُّبَى غَرِقَتِ الْقُرَى.

وَرُوِيَ عَنْ وَهْبِ بْنِ مُنَبِّه نَحْوُ هَذَا، وَهُوَ بَعِيدٌ جِدًّا.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ يَزِيدَ الْمُقْرِئُ، حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ، عَنْ يَحْيَى بْنِ سَعِيدٍ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ الْمُسَيَّبِ فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَآوَيْنَاهُمَا إِلَى رَبْوَةٍ ذَاتِ قَرَارٍ وَمَعِينٍ﴾ ، قَالَ: هِيَ دِمَشْقُ .

قَالَ: ورُوي عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ سَلَامٍ، وَالْحَسَنِ، وَزَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ، وَخَالِدِ بْنِ مَعْدان نَحْوُ ذَلِكَ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو سَعِيدٍ الْأَشَجُّ، حَدَّثَنَا وَكِيع، عَنْ إِسْرَائِيلُ، عَنْ سِمَاك، عَنْ عِكْرِمَة، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿ذَاتِ قَرَارٍ وَمَعِينٍ﴾ قال: أنهار دمشق.

وَقَالَ لَيْثُ بْنُ أَبِي سُلَيْمٍ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: ﴿وَآوَيْنَاهُمَا إِلَى رَبْوَةٍ [ذَاتِ قَرَارٍ وَمَعِينٍ] ﴾ ، قَالَ: عِيسَى ابْنُ مَرْيَمَ وَأُمُّهُ، حِينَ أَوَيَا إِلَى غَوْطَةِ دِمَشْقَ وَمَا حَوْلَهَا.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ، عَنْ بِشْرِ بْنِ رَافِعٍ، عَنْ أَبِي عَبْدِ اللَّهِ ابْنِ عَمِّ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ أَبَا هُرَيْرَةَ يَقُولُ: فِي قَوْلِهِ : ﴿: إِلَى رَبْوَةٍ ذَاتِ قَرَارٍ وَمَعِينٍ﴾ قَالَ: هِيَ الرَّمَلَةُ مِنْ فِلَسْطِينَ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ يُوسُفَ الفرْيابي، حَدَّثَنَا رَوّاد بْنُ الْجَرَّاحِ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبَّادُ بْنُ عَبَّادٍ الْخَوَّاصُ أَبُو عُتْبَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا السَّيْبَانِيُّ ، عَنِ ابْنِ وَعْلَة، عَنْ كُرَيْب السَّحولي، عَنْ مُرَّة البَهْزِي قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ يَقُولُ لِرَجُلٍ: "إِنَّكَ مَيِّتٌ بِالرَّبْوَةِ" فَمَاتَ بِالرَّمَلَةِ. وَهَذَا حَدِيثٌ غَرِيبٌ جِدًّا.

وَأَقْرَبُ الْأَقْوَالِ فِي ذَلِكَ مَا رَوَاهُ العَوْفِيّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَآوَيْنَاهُمَا إِلَى رَبْوَةٍ ذَاتِ قَرَارٍ وَمَعِينٍ﴾ ، قَالَ: الْمَعِينُ الْمَاءُ الْجَارِي، وَهُوَ النَّهْرُ الَّذِي قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿قَدْ جَعَلَ رَبُّكِ تَحْتَكِ سَرِيًّا﴾ [مَرْيَمَ: ٢٤] .

وَكَذَا قَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ، وقَتَادَةُ: ﴿إِلَى رَبْوَةٍ ذَاتِ قَرَارٍ وَمَعِينٍ﴾ : هُوَ بَيْتُ الْمَقْدِسِ. فَهَذَا وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ هُوَ الْأَظْهَرُ؛ لِأَنَّهُ الْمَذْكُورُ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى. وَالْقُرْآنُ يُفَسِّرُ بَعْضُهُ بَعْضًا. وَهُوَ أَوْلَى مَا يُفَسَّرُ بِهِ، ثُمَّ الْأَحَادِيثُ الصَّحِيحَةُ، ثُمَّ الْآثَارُ.

---

## 23:51-56 — verses 51-56 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty commands His messenger servants, upon them all be prayer and peace, to eat from what is lawful and to perform righteous deeds. This indicates that the lawful is an aid to righteous action. The prophets, peace be upon them, carried this out most completely, and they combined every good thing: word, deed, guidance, and sincere counsel. May God reward them on behalf of His servants with the best of reward.

Al-Hasan al-Basri said concerning His statement, {O messengers, eat from the good things}: "By God, they were not commanded regarding your yellow or your red foods, nor your sweet or your sour ones, but rather He said: confine yourselves to what is lawful from it."

Sa'id ibn Jubayr and al-Dahhak said: {eat from the good things} means: the lawful.

Abu Ishaq al-Sabi'i reported from Abu Maysarah ibn Shurahbil: "Jesus son of Mary used to eat from his mother's spinning."

In the Sahih: "There is no prophet but that he shepherded sheep." They said: "And you, O Messenger of God?" He said: "Yes, I used to shepherd them for wages, in exchange for a few qirats, for the people of Mecca."

In the Sahih: David, peace be upon him, used to eat from the earnings of his own hand.

In the two Sahihs: "The most beloved fasting to God is the fasting of David, and the most beloved prayer at night to God is the prayer of David. He used to sleep half the night, stand in prayer a third of it, and sleep a sixth of it. He used to fast one day and break his fast the next, and he would not flee when he met the enemy."

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] that Umm Abd Allah, the sister of Shaddad ibn Aws, sent to the Prophet ﷺ a bowl of milk at the time of his breaking his fast, while he was fasting. This was in the early part of the day and in intense heat. He sent her messenger back, asking: "From where did you get this sheep?" She said: "I bought it with my own money." So he drank from it. The next day Umm Abd Allah, the sister of Shaddad, came to him and said: "O Messenger of God, I sent you milk out of pity for you because of the length of the day and the intensity of the heat, so why did you send the messenger back to me about it?" He said to her: "The messengers were commanded with that: that they eat nothing but what is good, and do nothing but what is righteous."

It is established in Sahih Muslim, in the Jami' of al-Tirmidhi, and in the Musnad of Imam Ahmad, and the wording is his, from the hadith of Fudayl ibn Marzuq, from Adi ibn Thabit, from Abu Hazim, from Abu Hurayrah, may God be pleased with him, who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "O people, God is good (tayyib) and accepts nothing but what is good. God has commanded the believers with what He commanded the messengers, for He said: {O messengers, eat from the good things and do righteousness. Indeed, I am aware of what you do}, and He said: {O you who believe, eat from the good things We have provided for you} [al-Baqarah: 172]." Then he mentioned the man who prolongs a journey, disheveled and dust-covered, who raises his hands to the sky saying "O Lord, O Lord," while his food is unlawful, his drink is unlawful, his clothing is unlawful, and he has been nourished with what is unlawful: "How then could he be answered?"

Al-Tirmidhi said: hasan gharib (a sound but singularly transmitted report); we do not know it except from the hadith of Fudayl ibn Marzuq.

Regarding His statement: {And indeed this, your nation, is one nation}, meaning: your religion, O company of prophets, is one religion and one creed, which is the call to the worship of God alone, without partner. This is why He said: {and I am your Lord, so fear Me}. The discussion of this has already preceded in Surat al-Anbiya, and {one nation} is in the accusative case as a circumstantial qualifier (hal).

Regarding His statement: {But they divided their affair among themselves into sects}, meaning: the nations to whom the prophets were sent, {each faction rejoicing in what they have}, meaning: they rejoice in the misguidance they are in, because they believe themselves to be rightly guided. This is why He said, threatening and warning them: {So leave them in their confusion}, meaning: in their error and misguidance, {for a time}, meaning: until the time of their appointed end and destruction, just as the Almighty said: {So give the disbelievers respite, a gentle respite} [al-Tariq: 17], and the Almighty said: {Leave them to eat and enjoy themselves, and let hope distract them, for they are going to know} [al-Hijr: 3].

Regarding His statement: {Do they think that what We extend to them of wealth and children * is Us hastening to them the good things? Rather, they do not perceive}, meaning: do these deluded ones suppose that what We give them of wealth and children is due to their honor before Us and their status with Us? No, the matter is not as they claim in their statement: {We have more wealth and children, and we will not be punished} [Saba: 35]. They have indeed erred in that, and their hope has been disappointed. Rather We only do that to them as a gradual leading on, a giving of respite, and a granting of time. This is why He said: {Rather, they do not perceive}, just as the Almighty said: {So let not their wealth or their children impress you. God only intends to punish them through them in worldly life, and that their souls should depart while they are disbelievers} [al-Tawbah: 55], and the Almighty said: {We only grant them respite that they may increase in sin} [Al Imran: 178], and the Almighty said: {So leave Me with whoever denies this narration; We will progressively lead them on from where they do not know. And I will grant them respite; indeed, My plan is firm} [al-Qalam: 44-45], and He said: {Leave Me with the one I created alone, and to whom I granted extensive wealth, and children present with him, and for whom I smoothed the way, then he desires that I add more. No indeed, he has been stubbornly opposed to Our signs} [al-Muddaththir: 11-16], and the Almighty said: {And it is not your wealth or your children that bring you nearer to Us in position, but only those who believe and do righteous deeds. For them there is a double reward for what they did, and they will be secure in the high dwellings} [Saba: 37]. The verses on this theme are numerous.

Qatadah said concerning His statement: {Do they think that what We extend to them of wealth and children * is Us hastening to them the good things? Rather, they do not perceive}: "By God, the people have been deceived through their wealth and their children. O son of Adam, do not measure people by their wealth and children, but measure them by faith and righteous action."

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] from Abd Allah ibn Mas'ud, may God be pleased with him, who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "God has distributed your characters among you just as He has distributed your provisions among you. God gives worldly things to whomever He loves and to whomever He does not love, but He gives religion only to whomever He loves. So whoever God has given religion, He has indeed loved him. By the One in whose hand is my soul, no servant submits (becomes Muslim) until his heart and his tongue submit, and no one believes until his neighbor is safe from his evils." They said: "What are his evils, O Prophet of God?" He said: "His oppression and his injustice." "And no servant earns wealth unlawfully and then spends from it, for it will not be blessed for him; nor gives it in charity, for it will not be accepted from him; nor leaves it behind him, except that it becomes his provision to the Fire. Indeed, God does not erase evil with evil, but He erases evil with good. Indeed, the impure does not erase the impure."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَأْمُرُ تَعَالَى عِبَادَهُ الْمُرْسَلِينَ، عَلَيْهِمُ الصَّلَاةُ وَالسَّلَامُ أَجْمَعِينَ، بِالْأَكْلِ مِنَ الْحَلَالِ، وَالْقِيَامِ بِالصَّالِحِ مِنَ الْأَعْمَالِ، فَدَلَّ هَذَا عَلَى أَنَّ الْحَلَالَ عَون عَلَى الْعَمَلِ الصَّالِحِ، فَقَامَ الْأَنْبِيَاءُ، عَلَيْهِمُ السَّلَامُ، بِهَذَا أَتَمَّ الْقِيَامِ. وَجَمَعُوا بَيْنَ كُلِّ خَيْرٍ، قَوْلًا وَعَمَلًا وَدَلَالَةً وَنُصْحًا، فَجَزَاهُمُ اللَّهُ عَنِ الْعِبَادِ خَيْرًا.

قَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ فِي قَوْلُهُ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا الرُّسُلُ كُلُوا مِنَ الطَّيِّبَاتِ﴾ قَالَ: أَمَا وَاللَّهِ مَا أُمِرُوا بِأَصْفَرِكُمْ وَلَا أَحْمَرِكُمْ، وَلَا حُلْوِكُمْ وَلَا حَامِضِكُمْ، وَلَكِنْ قَالَ: انتَهُوا إِلَى الْحَلَالِ مِنْهُ.

وَقَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ: ﴿كُلُوا مِنَ الطَّيِّبَاتِ﴾ يعني: الحلال.

وَقَالَ أَبُو إِسْحَاقَ السَّبِيعي، عَنْ أَبِي مَيْسَرَةَ بْنِ شُرَحْبِيل: كَانَ عِيسَى ابْنُ مَرْيَمَ يَأْكُلُ مِنْ غَزْلِ أُمِّهِ.

وَفِي الصَّحِيحِ: "مَا مِنْ نَبِيٍّ إِلَّا رَعَى الْغَنَمَ". قَالُوا: وَأَنْتَ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ؟ قَالَ: "نَعَمْ، كُنْتُ أَرْعَاهَا عَلَى قَرَارِيطَ لِأَهْلِ مَكَّةَ" .

وَفِي الصَّحِيحِ: أَنَّ دَاوُدَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، كَانَ يَأْكُلُ مِنْ كَسْبِ يَدِهِ .

وَفِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ: "إِنَّ أَحَبَّ الصِّيَامِ إِلَى اللَّهِ صِيَامُ دَاوُدَ، وَأَحَبَّ الْقِيَامِ إِلَى اللَّهِ قِيَامُ دَاوُدَ، كَانَ يَنَامُ نِصْفَ اللَّيْلِ، وَيَقُومُ ثُلُثَهُ وَيَنَامُ سُدسَه، وَكَانَ يَصُومُ يَوْمًا وَيُفْطِرُ يَوْمًا، وَلَا يَفر إِذَا لَاقَى" .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو الْيَمَانِ الْحَكَمُ بْنُ نَافِعٍ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو بَكْرِ بْنِ أَبِي مَرْيَمَ، عَنْ ضَمْرَة بْنِ حَبِيبٍ، أَنَّ أُمَّ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، أُخْتَ شَدَّادِ بْنِ أَوْسٍ بَعَثَتْ إِلَى النَّبِيِّ ﷺ بِقَدَحِ لَبَنٍ عِنْدَ فِطْرِهِ وَهُوَ صَائِمٌ، وَذَلِكَ فِي أَوَّلِ النَّهَارِ وَشِدَّةِ الْحَرِّ، فَرَدَّ إِلَيْهَا رَسُولَهَا: أنَّى كَانَتْ لَكِ الشَّاةُ؟ فَقَالَتِ: اشْتَرَيْتُهَا مِنْ مَالِي، فَشَرِبَ مِنْهُ، فَلَمَّا كَانَ الْغَدُ أَتَتْهُ أُمُّ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ أُخْتُ شَدَّادٍ فَقَالَتْ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ، بعثتُ إِلَيْكَ بِلَبَنٍ مَرثيةً لَكَ مِنْ طُولِ النَّهَارِ وَشِدَّةِ الْحَرِّ، فَرَدَدْتَ إليَّ الرَّسُولَ فِيهِ؟. فَقَالَ لَهَا: "بِذَلِكَ أُمِرَتِ الرُّسُلُ، أَلَّا تَأْكُلَ إِلَّا طَيَّبًا، وَلَا تَعْمَلَ إِلَّا صَالِحًا" .

وَقَدْ ثَبَتَ فِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ، وَجَامِعِ التِّرْمِذِيِّ، وَمُسْنَدِ الْإِمَامِ أَحْمَدَ -وَاللَّفْظُ لَهُ-مِنْ حَدِيثِ فُضَيْل بْنُ مَرْزُوقٍ، عَنْ عَدِيّ بْنِ ثَابِتٍ، عَنْ أَبِي حَازِمٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ، إنَّ اللَّهَ طَيِّبٌ لَا يَقْبَلُ إِلَّا طَيَّبًا، وَإِنَّ اللَّهَ أَمَرَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ بِمَا أَمَرَ بِهِ الْمُرْسَلِينَ، فَقَالَ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا الرُّسُلُ كُلُوا مِنَ الطَّيِّبَاتِ وَاعْمَلُوا صَالِحًا إِنِّي بِمَا تَعْمَلُونَ عَلِيمٌ﴾ . وَقَالَ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا كُلُوا مِنْ طَيِّبَاتِ مَا رَزَقْنَاكُمْ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ١٧٢] . ثُمَّ ذَكَرَ الرَّجُلَ يُطِيلُ السَّفَرَ أَشْعَثَ أَغْبَرَ، وَمَطْعَمُهُ حَرَامٌ، وَمَشْرَبُهُ حَرَامٌ، وَمَلْبَسُهُ حَرَامٌ، وغُذِّي بِالْحَرَامِ، يَمُدُّ يَدَيْهِ إِلَى السَّمَاءِ: يَا رَبِّ، يَا رَبِّ، فأنَّى يُسْتَجَابُ لِذَلِكَ" .

وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: حَسَنٌ غَرِيبٌ، لَا نَعْرِفُهُ إِلَّا مِنْ حَدِيثِ فُضيل بْنِ مَرْزُوقٍ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِنَّ هَذِهِ أُمَّتُكُمْ أُمَّةً وَاحِدَةً﴾ أَيْ : دِينُكُمْ -يَا مَعْشَرَ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ-دِينٌ وَاحِدٌ، وَمِلَّةٌ وَاحِدَةٌ، وَهُوَ الدَّعْوَةُ إِلَى عِبَادَةِ اللَّهِ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَأَنَا رَبُّكُمْ فَاتَّقُونِ﴾ ، وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ الْكَلَامُ عَلَى ذَلِكَ فِي سُورَةِ "الْأَنْبِيَاءِ"، وَأَنَّ قَوْلَهُ: ﴿أُمَّةً وَاحِدَةً﴾ مَنْصُوبٌ عَلَى الْحَالِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَتَقَطَّعُوا أَمْرَهُمْ بَيْنَهُمْ زُبُرًا﴾ أَيِ: الْأُمَمُ الَّذِينَ بُعث إِلَيْهِمُ الْأَنْبِيَاءُ، ﴿كُلُّ حِزْبٍ بِمَا لَدَيْهِمْ فَرِحُونَ﴾ أَيْ: يَفْرَحُونَ بِمَا هُمْ فِيهِ مِنَ الضَّلَالِ؛ لِأَنَّهُمْ يَحْسَبُونَ أَنَّهُمْ مُهْتَدُونَ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ مُتَهَدِّدًا لَهُمْ وَمُتَوَاعِدًا: ﴿فَذَرْهُمْ فِي غَمْرَتِهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: فِي غَيِّهِمْ وَضَلَالِهِمْ ﴿حَتَّى حِينٍ﴾ أَيْ: إِلَى حِينِ حِينِهِمْ وَهَلَاكِهِمْ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَمَهِّلِ الْكَافِرِينَ أَمْهِلْهُمْ رُوَيْدًا﴾ [الطَّارِقِ: ١٧] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿ذَرْهُمْ يَأْكُلُوا وَيَتَمَتَّعُوا وَيُلْهِهِمُ الأمَلُ فَسَوْفَ يَعْلَمُونَ﴾ [الْحِجْرِ: ٣] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَيَحْسَبُونَ أَنَّمَا نُمِدُّهُمْ بِهِ مِنْ مَالٍ وَبَنِينَ * نُسَارِعُ لَهُمْ فِي الْخَيْرَاتِ بَل لَا يَشْعُرُونَ﴾ يَعْنِي: أَيُظَنُّ هَؤُلَاءِ الْمَغْرُورُونَ أَنَّ مَا نُعْطِيهِمْ مِنَ الْأَمْوَالِ وَالْأَوْلَادِ لِكَرَامَتِهِمْ عَلَيْنَا وَمَعَزَّتِهِمْ عِنْدَنَا؟! كَلَّا لَيْسَ الْأَمْرُ كَمَا يَزْعُمُونَ فِي قَوْلِهِمْ: ﴿نَحْنُ أَكْثَرُ أَمْوَالا وَأَوْلادًا وَمَا نَحْنُ بِمُعَذَّبِينَ﴾ [سبأ:٣٥] ، لقد أخطؤوا فِي ذَلِكَ وَخَابَ رَجَاؤُهُمْ، بَلْ إِنَّمَا نَفْعَلُ بِهِمْ ذَلِكَ اسْتِدْرَاجًا وَإِنْظَارًا وَإِمْلَاءً؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿بَل لَا يَشْعُرُونَ﴾ ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَلا تُعْجِبْكَ أَمْوَالُهُمْ وَلا أَوْلادُهُمْ إِنَّمَا يُرِيدُ اللَّهُ لِيُعَذِّبَهُمْ بِهَا فِي الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا وَتَزْهَقَ أَنْفُسُهُمْ وَهُمْ كَافِرُونَ﴾ [التَّوْبَةِ: ٥٥] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّمَا نُمْلِي لَهُمْ لِيَزْدَادُوا إِثْمًا﴾ [آلِ عِمْرَانَ: ١٧٨] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَذَرْنِي وَمَنْ يُكَذِّبُ بِهَذَا الْحَدِيثِ سَنَسْتَدْرِجُهُمْ مِنْ حَيْثُ لَا يَعْلَمُونَ * وَأُمْلِي لَهُمْ إِنَّ كَيْدِي مَتِينٌ﴾ [الْقَلَمِ: ٤٤، ٤٥] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿ذَرْنِي وَمَنْ خَلَقْتُ وَحِيدًا * وَجَعَلْتُ لَهُ مَالا مَمْدُودًا * وَبَنِينَ شُهُودًا * وَمَهَّدْتُ لَهُ تَمْهِيدًا * ثُمَّ يَطْمَعُ أَنْ أَزِيدَ * كَلا إِنَّهُ كَانَ لآيَاتِنَا عَنِيدًا﴾ [الْمُدَّثِّرِ: ١١-١٦] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا أَمْوَالُكُمْ وَلا أَوْلادُكُمْ بِالَّتِي تُقَرِّبُكُمْ عِنْدَنَا زُلْفَى إِلا مَنْ آمَنَ وَعَمِلَ صَالِحًا فَأُولَئِكَ لَهُمْ جَزَاءُ الضِّعْفِ بِمَا عَمِلُوا وَهُمْ فِي الْغُرُفَاتِ آمِنُونَ﴾ [سَبَأٍ: ٣٧] وَالْآيَاتُ فِي هَذَا كَثِيرَةٌ.

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿أَيَحْسَبُونَ أَنَّمَا نُمِدُّهُمْ بِهِ مِنْ مَالٍ وَبَنِينَ * نُسَارِعُ لَهُمْ فِي الْخَيْرَاتِ بَل لَا يَشْعُرُونَ﴾ قَالَ: مُكِرَ وَاللَّهِ بِالْقَوْمِ فِي أَمْوَالِهِمْ وَأَوْلَادِهِمْ، يَا ابْنَ آدَمَ، فَلَا تَعْتَبِرِ النَّاسَ بِأَمْوَالِهِمْ وَأَوْلَادِهِمْ، وَلَكِنِ اعْتَبِرْهُمْ بِالْإِيمَانِ وَالْعَمَلِ الصَّالِحِ.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ [بْنُ عُبَيْد، حَدَّثَنَا أَبَانُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنِ الصَّبَّاحِ بْنِ محمد، عن مرة الهمداني، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدِ اللَّهِ] بْنِ مَسْعُودٍ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ قَسَم بَيْنَكُمْ أَخْلَاقَكُمْ، كَمَا قَسَمَ بَيْنَكُمْ أَرْزَاقَكُمْ، وَإِنَّ اللَّهَ يُعطي الدُّنْيَا مَنْ يُحِبّ وَمَنْ لَا يُحِبُّ، وَلَا يُعْطِي الدِّين إِلَّا لِمَنْ أَحَبَّ، فَمَنْ أَعْطَاهُ اللَّهُ الدِّينَ فَقَدْ أَحَبَّهُ، وَالَّذِي نَفْسِي بِيَدِهِ، لَا يُسْلِمُ عَبْدٌ حَتَّى يُسْلِمَ قَلْبُهُ وَلِسَانُهُ، وَلَا يُؤْمِنُ حَتَّى يَأْمَنَ جَارُهُ بَوَائِقَهُ-قَالُوا: وَمَا بَوَائِقُهُ يَا نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ؟ قَالَ: غَشْمُهُ وَظُلْمُهُ- وَلَا يَكْسِبُ عَبْدٌ مَالًا مِنْ حَرَامٍ فَيُنْفِقَ مِنْهُ فَيُبَارَكَ لَهُ فِيهِ، وَلَا يَتَصَدَّقُ بِهِ فَيُقْبَلَ مِنْهُ، وَلَا يَتْرُكُهُ خَلْفَ ظَهْرِهِ إِلَّا كَانَ زَادَهُ إِلَى النَّارِ، إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يَمْحُو السَّيِّئَ بِالسَّيِّئِ، وَلَكِنْ يَمْحُو السَّيِّئَ بِالْحَسَنِ، إِنَّ الْخَبِيثَ لَا يَمْحُو الْخَبِيثَ" .

---

## 23:57-61 — verses 57-61 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says: {Indeed, those who out of fear of their Lord are apprehensive}, meaning: they, along with their goodness, their faith, and their righteous deeds, are apprehensive of God, fearful of Him, and anxious about His scheming against them, as al-Hasan al-Basri said: The believer combines goodness with apprehension, while the hypocrite combines wrongdoing with a false sense of security.

{And those who believe in the signs of their Lord}, meaning: they believe in His cosmic signs and His legislative signs, as in the Almighty's statement reporting about Mary (peace be upon her): {And she believed in the words of her Lord and His Books} [al-Tahrim: 12], meaning: she was certain that whatever occurred was only by God's decree and predetermination, and that whatever God legislated, if it was a command, was among what He loves and is pleased with, and if it was a prohibition, was among what He dislikes and rejects, and if it concerned news of the unseen, then it is true, as God the Almighty said: {And those who do not associate partners with their Lord}, meaning: they do not worship anyone besides Him, but rather affirm His oneness and know that there is no god but God, the One, al-Samad (the Everlasting Sustainer upon whom all depend, free of need Himself), who has not taken a companion or a child, and that He has no equal and no match.

Concerning His statement: {And those who give what they give while their hearts are fearful, knowing that they are returning to their Lord}, meaning: they give what they give while fearing that it will not be accepted from them, out of fear that they may have fallen short in fulfilling the conditions of giving. This falls under the category of apprehension and caution, as Imam Ahmad said:

[chain] from A'isha, that she said: O Messenger of God, {And those who give what they give while their hearts are fearful}, is this the one who steals, commits adultery, and drinks wine, while fearing God, Mighty and Majestic? He said: "No, O daughter of Abu Bakr, O daughter of al-Siddiq, rather it is the one who prays, fasts, and gives charity, while fearing God, Mighty and Majestic."

Al-Tirmidhi and Ibn Abi Hatim likewise narrated it, from the hadith of Malik ibn Mighwal, with similar wording. And it states: "No, O daughter of al-Siddiq, rather it is those who pray, fast, and give charity, while fearing that it will not be accepted from them, {those are the ones who hasten to good deeds}." Al-Tirmidhi said: This hadith was also narrated from the hadith of Abd al-Rahman ibn Sa'id, from Abu Hazim, from Abu Hurayrah, from the Prophet ﷺ, in similar fashion.

Ibn Abbas, Muhammad ibn Ka'b al-Qurazi, and al-Hasan al-Basri likewise said this in their exegesis of this verse.

Others read this verse as: "And those who do what they do while their hearts are fearful," meaning: they do what they do while being fearful. This reading has been attributed, as a marfu' (elevated report traced to the Prophet), to the Prophet ﷺ, that he recited it in this manner.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abu Khalaf, the client of Banu Jumah, that he entered along with Ubayd ibn Umayr upon A'isha, may God be pleased with her, and she said: Welcome, Abu Asim, what keeps you from visiting us, or calling on us? He said: I fear that I would tire you out. She said: You would never do that. He said: I came to ask about a verse in the Book of God, Mighty and Majestic, how did the Messenger of God ﷺ used to recite it? She said: Which verse? He said: {Those who give what they give} or {those who do what they do}? She said: Which of the two is dearer to you? I said: By Him in whose hand is my soul, one of them is dearer to me than the whole world, or: than the world and everything in it. She said: Which one is it? I said: {Those who do what they do}. She said: I bear witness that the Messenger of God ﷺ used to recite it in that way, and that is how it was revealed, but the spelling is one letter's variance.

Isma'il ibn Muslim al-Makki, and he is weak (a transmitter of weak reliability).

The meaning according to the first reading, which is the reading of the majority, the seven canonical reciters and others, is clearer, because it says: {those are the ones who hasten to good deeds, and they are foremost in them}, thus making them among the foremost. Had the meaning followed the other reading, they would scarcely be among the foremost, but rather among the moderate or the deficient. And God the Almighty knows best.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ هُمْ مِنْ خَشْيَةِ رَبِّهِمْ مُشْفِقُونَ﴾ أَيْ: هُمْ مَعَ إِحْسَانِهِمْ وَإِيمَانِهِمْ وَعَمَلِهِمُ الصَّالِحِ، مُشْفِقُونَ مِنَ اللَّهِ خَائِفُونَ مِنْهُ، وَجِلُونَ مِنْ مَكْرِهِ بِهِمْ، كَمَا قَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ: إِنَّ الْمُؤْمِنَ جَمَعَ إِحْسَانًا وَشَفَقَةً، وَإِنَّ الْمُنَافِقَ جَمَعَ إِسَاءَةً وَأَمْنًا.

﴿وَالَّذِينَ هُمْ بِآيَاتِ رَبِّهِمْ يُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ أَيْ: يُؤْمِنُونَ بِآيَاتِهِ الْكَوْنِيَّةِ وَالشَّرْعِيَّةِ، كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى إِخْبَارًا عَنْ مَرْيَمَ، عَلَيْهَا السَّلَامُ: ﴿وَصَدَّقَتْ بِكَلِمَاتِ رَبِّهَا وَكُتُبِهِ﴾ [التَّحْرِيمِ: ١٢] ، أَيْ: أَيْقَنَتْ أَنَّ مَا كَانَ فَإِنَّمَا هُوَ عَنْ قَدَرِ اللَّهِ وَقَضَائِهِ، وَمَا شَرَعَهُ اللَّهُ فَهُوَ إِنْ كَانَ أَمْرًا فَمِمَّا يُحِبُّهُ وَيَرْضَاهُ، وَإِنْ كَانَ نَهْيًا فَهُوَ مِمَّا يَكْرَهُهُ وَيَأْبَاهُ، وَإِنْ كَانَ خَيْرًا فَهُوَ حَقٌّ، كَمَا قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ هُمْ بِرَبِّهِمْ لَا يُشْرِكُونَ﴾ أَيْ: لَا يَعْبُدُونَ مَعَهُ غَيْرَهُ، بَلْ يُوَحِّدُونَهُ وَيَعْلَمُونَ أَنَّهُ لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ أَحَدًا صَمَدًا، لَمْ يَتَّخِذْ صَاحِبَةً وَلَا وَلَدًا، وَأَنَّهُ لَا نَظِيرَ لَهُ وَلَا كُفْءَ لَهُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ يُؤْتُونَ مَا آتَوْا وَقُلُوبُهُمْ وَجِلَةٌ أَنَّهُمْ إِلَى رَبِّهِمْ رَاجِعُونَ﴾ أَيْ: يُعْطُونَ الْعَطَاءَ وَهُمْ خَائِفُونَ أَلَّا يُتَقَبَّلَ مِنْهُمْ، لِخَوْفِهِمْ أَنْ يَكُونُوا قَدْ قَصَّرُوا فِي الْقِيَامِ بِشُرُوطِ الْإِعَطَاءِ. وَهَذَا مِنْ بَابِ الْإِشْفَاقِ وَالِاحْتِيَاطِ، كَمَا قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ:

حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ آدَمَ، حَدَّثَنَا مَالِكُ بْنُ مِغْوَل، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ سَعِيدِ بْنِ وَهْبٍ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ؛ أَنَّهَا قَالَتْ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، ﴿وَالَّذِينَ يُؤْتُونَ مَا آتَوْا وَقُلُوبُهُمْ وَجِلَةٌ﴾ ، هُوَ الَّذِي يَسْرِقُ وَيَزْنِي وَيَشْرَبُ الْخَمْرَ، وَهُوَ يَخَافُ اللَّهَ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ؟ قَالَ: "لَا يَا بِنْتَ أَبِي بَكْرٍ، يَا بِنْتَ الصِّدِّيقِ، وَلَكِنَّهُ الَّذِي يُصَلِّي وَيَصُومُ وَيَتَصَدَّقُ، وَهُوَ يَخَافُ اللَّهَ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ".

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ وَابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ مَالِكِ بْنِ مِغْوَل، بِهِ بِنَحْوِهِ . وَقَالَ: "لَا يَا بِنْتَ الصِّدِّيقِ، وَلَكِنَّهُمُ الَّذِينَ يُصَلُّونَ وَيَصُومُونَ وَيَتَصَدَّقُونَ، وَهُمْ يَخَافُونَ أَلَّا يُقْبَلَ مِنْهُمْ، ﴿أُولَئِكَ يُسَارِعُونَ فِي الْخَيْرَاتِ﴾ قَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: ورُوي هَذَا الْحَدِيثُ مِنْ حديث عبد الرحمن بن سعيد، عن أَبِي حَازِمٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ نَحْوَ هَذَا .

وَهَكَذَا قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُحَمَّدُ بْنُ كَعْبٍ الْقُرَظِيُّ، وَالْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ فِي تَفْسِيرِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ.

وَقَدْ قَرَأَ آخَرُونَ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ: "وَالَّذِينَ يَأْتُونَ مَا أَتَوْا وَقُلُوبُهُمْ وَجِلَةٌ" أَيْ: يَفْعَلُونَ مَا يَفْعَلُونَ وَهُمْ خَائِفُونَ، وَرُوِيَ هَذَا مَرْفُوعًا إِلَى النَّبِيَّ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَرَأَ كَذَلِكَ.

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَفَّانُ، حَدَّثَنَا صَخْرُ بْنُ جُوَيْرِية، حَدَّثَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ الْمَكِّيُّ، حَدَّثَنِي أَبُو خَلَفٍ مَوْلَى بَنِي جُمَح: أَنَّهُ دَخَلَ مَعَ عُبَيد بْنِ عُمَيْر عَلَى عَائِشَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، فَقَالَتْ: مَرْحَبًا بِأَبِي عَاصِمٍ، مَا يَمْنَعُكَ أَنْ تَزُورَنَا -أَوْ: تُلِمّ بِنَا؟ -فَقَالَ: أَخْشَى أَنْ أمُلَّك. فَقَالَتْ: مَا كُنْتَ لِتَفْعَلَ؟ قَالَ: جِئْتُ لِأَسْأَلَ عَنْ آيَةٍ فِي كِتَابِ اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، كَيْفَ كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقْرَؤُهَا؟ قَالَتْ: أيَّة آيَةٍ؟ فَقَالَ: ﴿الَّذِينَ يَأْتُونَ مَا أَتَوْا﴾ أَوِ ﴿الَّذِينَ يُؤْتُونَ مَا آتَوْا﴾ ؟ فَقَالَتْ: أَيَّتُهُمَا أَحَبُّ إِلَيْكَ؟ فَقُلْتُ: وَالَّذِي نَفْسِي بِيَدِهِ، لِإِحْدَاهُمَا أَحَبُّ إِلَيَّ مِنَ الدُّنْيَا جَمِيعًا -أَوِ: الدُّنْيَا وَمَا فِيهَا-قَالَتْ: وَمَا هِيَ؟ فَقُلْتُ: ﴿الَّذِينَ يَأْتُونَ مَا أَتَوْا﴾ فَقَالَتْ: أَشْهَدُ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ كَذَلِكَ كَانَ يَقْرَؤُهَا، وَكَذَلِكَ أُنْزِلَتْ، وَلَكِنَّ الْهِجَاءَ حَرْفٌ .

إِسْمَاعِيلُ بْنُ مُسْلِمٍ الْمَكِّيُّ، وَهُوَ ضَعِيفٌ.

وَالْمَعْنَى عَلَى الْقِرَاءَةِ الْأُولَى -وَهِيَ قِرَاءَةُ الْجُمْهُورِ: السَّبْعَةِ وَغَيْرِهِمْ-أَظْهَرُ؛ لِأَنَّهُ قَالَ: ﴿أُولَئِكَ يُسَارِعُونَ فِي الْخَيْرَاتِ وَهُمْ لَهَا سَابِقُونَ﴾ ، فَجَعَلَهُمْ مِنَ السَّابِقِينَ. وَلَوْ كَانَ الْمَعْنَى عَلَى الْقِرَاءَةِ الْأُخْرَى لَأَوْشَكَ أَلَّا يَكُونُوا مِنَ السَّابِقِينَ، بَلْ مِنَ الْمُقْتَصِدِينَ أَوِ الْمُقَصِّرِينَ، وَاللَّهُ تَعَالَى أَعْلَمُ.

---

## 23:62-67 — verses 62-67 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing of His justice in His legislation for His servants in this world: that He does not burden any soul except with what is within its capacity, meaning: only what it is able to bear and carry out. And that on the Day of Resurrection He will hold them to account for their deeds, which He has recorded against them in a written book from which nothing is lost. Hence He says: {And with Us is a book that speaks the truth} meaning the book of deeds, {and they will not be wronged} meaning: they will not be deprived of any good at all. As for evil deeds, He pardons and overlooks many of them for His believing servants.

Then He says, rebuking the disbelievers and polytheists of Quraysh: {Nay, their hearts are in confused ignorance} meaning: heedlessness and misguidance {of this}, meaning: the Qur'an which [Allah, the Exalted] sent down upon His Messenger ﷺ.

His saying: {And they have deeds besides that which they are doing} : al-Hakam ibn Aban said, from Ikrimah, from Ibn Abbas: {And they have deeds} meaning evil ones, besides that, meaning polytheism (shirk), {which they are doing} he said: they are bound to do them. The like of this has been narrated from Mujahid, al-Hasan, and others.

Others said: {And they have deeds besides that which they are doing} meaning: evil deeds have been decreed for them which they must inevitably do before their death, so that the word of punishment becomes due against them. Something similar has been narrated from Muqatil ibn Hayyan, al-Suddi, and Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam. This is an apparent, strong, and good view. We have already cited earlier the hadith of Ibn Mas'ud: "By the One besides whom there is no god, a man may do the deeds of the people of Paradise until there is nothing between him and it but a forearm's length, then the decree overtakes him, and he does the deeds of the people of Hellfire, and so enters it."

His saying: {Until, when We seize their affluent ones with punishment, behold, they cry out for help} meaning: until the punishment of Allah, His might, and His vengeance comes upon their affluent ones, who were the fortunate ones enjoying comfort in this world, {behold, they cry out for help} meaning: they scream and cry for rescue, as the Almighty says: {And leave Me with the deniers, those of ease, and give them respite a little. Indeed, with Us are shackles and a blazing fire, and food that chokes, and a painful punishment} [al-Muzzammil: 11-13], and the Almighty says: {How many generations have We destroyed before them, and they cried out when it was no longer time for escape} [Sad: 3].

His saying: {Do not cry out for help today; indeed you will not be helped by Us} meaning: We will not shelter you from what has befallen you, whether you cry out or remain silent. There is no evasion, no escape, and no refuge; the matter has become binding and the punishment has become due.

Then He mentions the greatest of their sins, saying: {My verses were recited to you, but you used to turn back on your heels} meaning: when you were called, you refused, and when you were asked, you withheld; {That is because, when Allah alone was called upon, you disbelieved, but when partners were associated with Him, you believed. So the judgment belongs to Allah, the Most High, the Most Great} [Ghafir: 12].

His saying: {Arrogant concerning it, conversing by night, speaking foul talk} : there are two opinions regarding its interpretation. The first: that "arrogant" is a description of their state at the time of their turning away from the truth and their refusal of it, out of arrogance toward it and contempt for it and its people. On this basis, there are three views concerning the pronoun in {concerning it}:

The first: that it refers to the Sacred Precinct (al-Haram) in Mecca. They were condemned because they used to sit up at night conversing in foul, indecent speech.

The second: that the pronoun refers to the Qur'an. They used to sit up at night mentioning the Qur'an with foul speech: "It is sorcery, it is poetry, it is soothsaying," and other such false statements.

The third: that it refers to Muhammad ﷺ. They used to mention him in their night gatherings with corrupt statements, and set forth for him false comparisons, saying he was a poet, or a soothsayer, or a sorcerer, or a liar, or a madman. All of this is false. Rather he is the servant of Allah and His Messenger, whom Allah caused to prevail over them, and He brought them out of the Sacred Precinct humbled and disgraced.

It is also said that what is meant by His saying {Arrogant concerning it} is: concerning the House (the Ka'bah), boasting of it and believing themselves to be its guardians, though they were not truly so, as al-Nasa'i states in the Tafsir section of his Sunan:

[chain] Ahmad ibn Sulayman informed us, Ubayd Allah informed us, from Isra'il, from Abd al-A'la, that he heard Sa'id ibn Jubayr narrating from Ibn Abbas that he said: night conversation (al-samar) was only disliked when this verse was revealed: {Arrogant concerning it, conversing by night, speaking foul talk}. He said: arrogant concerning the House, saying "we are its people." {Conversing by night}, he said: they would act arrogantly [and hold night gatherings in it, without] maintaining it, and they would abandon and neglect it.

Ibn Abi Hatim has given a lengthy discussion here, the substance of which is as above.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ عَدْلِهِ فِي شَرْعِهِ عَلَى عِبَادِهِ فِي الدُّنْيَا: أَنَّهُ لَا يُكَلِّفُ نَفْسًا إِلَّا وُسْعَهَا، أَيْ: إِلَّا مَا تُطِيقُ حَمْلَهُ وَالْقِيَامَ بِهِ، وَأَنَّهُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ يُحَاسِبُهُمْ بِأَعْمَالِهِمُ الَّتِي كَتَبَهَا عَلَيْهِمْ فِي كِتَابٍ مَسْطُورٍ لَا يَضِيعُ مِنْهُ شَيْءٌ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَلَدَيْنَا كِتَابٌ يَنْطِقُ بِالْحَقِّ﴾ يَعْنِي: كِتَابَ الْأَعْمَالِ، ﴿وَهُمْ لَا يُظْلَمُونَ﴾ أَيْ: لَا يُبْخَسُونَ مِنَ الْخَيْرِ شَيْئًا، وَأَمَّا السَّيِّئَاتُ فَيَعْفُو وَيَصْفَحُ عَنْ كَثِيرٍ مِنْهَا لِعِبَادِهِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ مُنْكِرًا عَلَى الْكُفَّارِ وَالْمُشْرِكِينَ مِنْ قُرَيْشٍ: ﴿بَلْ قُلُوبُهُمْ فِي غَمْرَةٍ﴾ أَيْ: غَفْلَةٍ وَضَلَالَةٍ ﴿مِنْ هَذَا﴾ أَيِ: الْقُرْآنُ الَّذِي أَنْزَلَهُ [اللَّهِ تَعَالَى] عَلَى رَسُولِهِ ﷺ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلَهُمْ أَعْمَالٌ مِنْ دُونِ ذَلِكَ هُمْ لَهَا عَامِلُونَ﴾ : قَالَ الْحَكَمُ بْنُ أَبَانَ، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿وَلَهُمْ أَعْمَالٌ﴾ أَيْ: سَيِّئَةٌ مِنْ دُونِ ذَلِكَ، يَعْنِي: الشِّرْكَ، ﴿هُمْ لَهَا عَامِلُونَ﴾ قَالَ: لَا بُدَّ أَنْ يَعْمَلُوهَا. كَذَا رُوِيَ عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، وَالْحَسَنِ، وَغَيْرِ وَاحِدٍ.

وَقَالَ آخَرُونَ: ﴿وَلَهُمْ أَعْمَالٌ مِنْ دُونِ ذَلِكَ هُمْ لَهَا عَامِلُونَ﴾ أَيْ: قَدْ كُتِبَ عَلَيْهِمْ أَعْمَالٌ سَيِّئَةٌ لَا بُدَّ أَنْ يَعْمَلُوهَا قَبْلَ مَوْتِهِمْ لَا مَحَالَةَ، لِتَحِقَّ عَلَيْهِمْ كَلِمَةُ الْعَذَابِ. ورُوِي نَحو هَذَا عَنْ مُقَاتِلِ بْنِ حيَّان والسُّدِّيّ، وَعَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ. وَهُوَ ظَاهِرٌ قَوِيٌّ حَسَنٌ. وَقَدْ قَدَّمْنَا فِي حَدِيثِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ: "فَوَالَّذِي لَا إِلَهَ غَيْرُهُ، إِنَّ الرَّجُلَ لَيَعْمَلُ بِعَمَلِ أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ حَتَّى مَا يَكُونُ بَيْنَهُ وَبَيْنَهَا إِلَّا ذِرَاعٌ، فَيَسْبِقُ عَلَيْهِ الْكِتَابُ، فَيَعْمَلُ بِعَمَلِ أَهْلِ النَّارِ، فَيَدْخُلُهَا".

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا أَخَذْنَا مُتْرَفِيهِمْ بِالْعَذَابِ إِذَا هُمْ يَجْأَرُونَ﴾ يَعْنِي: حَتَّى إِذَا جَاءَ مُتْرَفِيهِمْ -وَهُمُ السُّعَدَاءُ الْمُنَعَّمُونَ فِي الدُّنْيَا-عذابُ اللَّهِ وَبَأْسَهُ وَنِقْمَتَهُ بهم ﴿إِذَا هُمْ يَجْأَرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: يَصْرُخُونَ وَيَسْتَغِيثُونَ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَذَرْنِي وَالْمُكَذِّبِينَ أُولِي النَّعْمَةِ وَمَهِّلْهُمْ قَلِيلا. إِنَّ لَدَيْنَا أَنْكَالا وَجَحِيمًا. وَطَعَامًا ذَا غُصَّةٍ وَعَذَابًا أَلِيمًا﴾ [الْمُزَّمِّلِ: ١١-١٣] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿كَمْ أَهْلَكْنَا مِنْ قَبْلِهِمْ مِنْ قَرْنٍ فَنَادَوْا وَلاتَ حِينَ مَنَاصٍ﴾ [ص: ٣] .

وقوله: ﴿لا تَجْأَرُوا الْيَوْمَ إِنَّكُمْ مِنَّا لَا تُنْصَرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: لَا نُجِيرُكُمْ مِمَّا حَلَّ بِكُمْ، سَوَاءٌ جَأَرْتُمْ أَوْ سكتُّم، لَا مَحِيدَ وَلَا مَنَاصَ وَلَا وَزَرَ لَزِمَ الْأَمْرُ وَوَجَبَ الْعَذَابُ.

ثُمَّ ذَكَرَ أَكْبَرَ ذُنُوبِهِمْ فَقَالَ: ﴿قَدْ كَانَتْ آيَاتِي تُتْلَى عَلَيْكُمْ فَكُنْتُمْ عَلَى أَعْقَابِكُمْ تَنْكِصُونَ﴾ أَيْ: إِذَا دُعِيتُمْ أَبَيْتُمْ، وَإِنْ طُلبتم امْتَنَعْتُمْ؛ ﴿ذَلِكُمْ بِأَنَّهُ إِذَا دُعِيَ اللَّهُ وَحْدَهُ كَفَرْتُمْ وَإِنْ يُشْرَكْ بِهِ تُؤْمِنُوا فَالْحُكْمُ لِلَّهِ الْعَلِيِّ الْكَبِيرِ﴾ [غَافِرٍ: ١٢] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿مُسْتَكْبِرِينَ بِهِ سَامِرًا تَهْجُرُونَ﴾ : فِي تَفْسِيرِهِ قَوْلَانِ، أَحَدُهُمَا: أَنَّ مُسْتَكْبِرِينَ حَالٌ مِنْهُمْ حِينَ نُكُوصِهِمْ عَنِ الْحَقِّ وَإِبَائِهِمْ إِيَّاهُ، اسْتِكْبَارًا عَلَيْهِ وَاحْتِقَارًا لَهُ وَلِأَهْلِهِ، فَعَلَى هَذَا الضَّمِيرُ فِي ﴿بِهِ﴾ فِيهِ ثَلَاثَةُ أَقْوَالٍ:

أَحَدُهُمَا : أَنَّهُ الْحَرَمُ بِمَكَّةَ، ذُمُّوا لِأَنَّهُمْ كَانُوا يَسْمُرُونَ بالهُجْر مِنَ الْكَلَامِ.

وَالثَّانِي: أَنَّهُ ضَمِيرُ الْقُرْآنِ، كَانُوا يَسْمُرُونَ وَيَذْكُرُونَ الْقُرْآنَ بِالْهَجْرِ مِنَ الْكَلَامِ: "إِنَّهُ سِحْرٌ، إِنَّهُ شِعْرٌ، إِنَّهُ كَهَانَةٌ" إِلَى غَيْرِ ذَلِكَ مِنَ الأقوال الباطلة.

وَالثَّالِثُ: أَنَّهُ مُحَمَّدٌ ﷺ، كَانُوا يَذْكُرُونَهُ فِي سَمَرِهِمْ بِالْأَقْوَالِ الْفَاسِدَةِ، وَيَضْرِبُونَ لَهُ الْأَمْثَالَ الْبَاطِلَةَ، مِنْ أَنَّهُ شَاعِرٌ، أَوْ كَاهِنٌ، أَوْ سَاحِرٌ، أَوْ كَذَّابٌ، أَوْ مَجْنُونٌ. وَكُلُّ ذَلِكَ بَاطِلٌ، بَلْ هُوَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ وَرَسُولُهُ، الَّذِي أَظْهَرَهُ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمْ، وَأَخْرَجَهُمْ مِنَ الْحَرَمِ صَاغِرِينَ أَذِلَّاءَ.

وَقِيلَ: الْمُرَادُ بِقَوْلُهُ: ﴿مُسْتَكْبِرِينَ بِهِ﴾ أَيْ: بِالْبَيْتِ، يَفْتَخِرُونَ بِهِ وَيَعْتَقِدُونَ أَنَّهُمْ أَوْلِيَاؤُهُ، وَلَيْسُوا بِهِمْ، كَمَا قَالَ النَّسَائِيُّ فِي التَّفْسِيرِ مِنْ سُنَنِهِ:

أَخْبَرْنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ سُلَيْمَانَ، أَخْبَرَنَا عُبَيْدُ اللَّهِ، عَنْ إِسْرَائِيلَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الْأَعْلَى، أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ سَعِيدَ بْنَ جُبَيْرٍ يُحَدِّثُ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: إِنَّمَا كُرِهَ السَّمَرُ حِينَ نَزَلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ: ﴿مُسْتَكْبِرِينَ بِهِ سَامِرًا تَهْجُرُونَ﴾ ، فَقَالَ: مُسْتَكْبِرِينَ بِالْبَيْتِ، يَقُولُونَ: نَحْنُ أَهْلُهُ، ﴿سَامِرًا﴾ قَالَ: يَتَكَبَّرُونَ [وَيَسْمُرُونَ فِيهِ، وَلَا] يُعَمِّرُونَهُ، وَيَهْجُرُونَهُ .

وَقَدْ أَطْنَبَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ هَاهُنَا بِمَاذَا حَاصِلُهُ.

---

## 23:68-75 — verses 68-75 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty is speaking in rebuke of the polytheists for their failure to comprehend the mighty Qur'an, to reflect upon it, and for turning away from it, despite the fact that they were singled out with this Book than which God sent down to no messenger anything more complete or more noble, especially since their forefathers who died in the Jahiliyyah (pre-Islamic ignorance) had no Book reach them and no warner come to them. So it would have been fitting for these people to meet the favor God had bestowed upon them by accepting it, giving thanks for it, striving to understand it, and acting upon its requirements throughout the hours of night and the edges of day, just as the noble ones among them did, those who submitted and followed the Messenger ﷺ, and with whom God was pleased.

Qatadah said regarding {Have they not reflected upon the word}: by God, if they had reflected upon it and understood it, they would have found in the Qur'an a deterrent from disobeying God, but they clung to what was ambiguous, and thereby they were destroyed.

Then He says, in rebuke of the disbelievers among the Quraysh: {Or did they not recognize their Messenger, so that they deny him} That is: do they not know Muhammad and his truthfulness, his trustworthiness, and the integrity with which he grew up among them? Can they possibly deny that and speak falsely about it? This is why Ja'far ibn Abi Talib, may God be pleased with him, said to the Negus, the king of Abyssinia: "O King, God has sent to us a messenger whose lineage, truthfulness, and trustworthiness we know." Likewise al-Mughirah ibn Shu'bah said the same to the deputy of Kisra when he confronted them in single combat, and likewise Abu Sufyan Sakhr ibn Harb said the same to the King of Rome, Heraclius, when he asked him and his companions about the attributes of the Prophet ﷺ, his lineage, his truthfulness, and his trustworthiness. They were at that time still disbelievers who had not submitted, yet even so they could not do otherwise than speak the truth, and so they acknowledged it.

His saying: {Or do they say that madness is in him} relates the claim of the polytheists about the Prophet ﷺ, that he had invented the Qur'an, that is, fabricated it from himself, or that madness afflicted him so that he did not know what he was saying. God informs us of them that their hearts did not believe in him, while they knew the falseness of what they said about the Qur'an, for there had come to them from the speech of God something that could not be borne nor resisted. He had challenged them and all the people of the earth to produce anything like it, and they were not able to, nor will they ever be able to, for all eternity. This is why He said: {Rather, he has brought them the truth, but most of them detest the truth} It may be that this is a circumstantial clause, meaning: in the state of most of them detesting the truth, or it may be an independent new statement of fact. God knows best.

Qatadah said: it was mentioned to us that the Prophet of God ﷺ met a man and said to him, "Submit (become Muslim)." The man said: "You are calling me to a matter I detest." The Prophet of God ﷺ said: "Even if you detest it." And it was mentioned to us that he met another man and said to him, "Submit," and this weighed heavily and grew great upon him, so the Prophet of God said to him: "Tell me, if you were on a rough and difficult path, and you met a man whose face you knew and whose lineage you knew, and he called you to a wide, easy path, would you follow him?" He said: "Yes." So he said: "By the One in whose hand is the soul of Muhammad, you are upon a path rougher than that one if you were to remain upon it, and I am calling you to something easier than that if you were called to it." And it was mentioned to us that the Prophet of God ﷺ met a man and said to him, "Submit," and this weighed heavily upon him, so the Prophet of God ﷺ said to him: "Tell me about your two young servants: one of them, when he speaks to you, tells you the truth, and when you entrust him with something he delivers it to you faithfully; is he dearer to you, or the young servant who, when he speaks to you, lies to you, and when you entrust him with something, betrays you?" He said: "Rather, the servant who speaks truthfully to me and who delivers faithfully what I entrust to him." The Prophet ﷺ said: "Such are you before your Lord."

His saying: {And if the truth had followed their desires, the heavens and the earth and whoever is in them would have been ruined} Mujahid, Abu Salih, and al-Suddi said: al-Haqq (the Truth) here is God, Mighty and Majestic, and the meaning is: if God had granted them what was in their souls of desire, and had legislated matters in accordance with that, {the heavens and the earth and whoever is in them would have been ruined}, that is, because of the corruption of their desires and their contradiction with one another, just as He tells us of them in their saying: {Why was this Qur'an not sent down upon a great man of the two cities?} then He says: {Is it they who distribute the mercy of your Lord?} [al-Zukhruf: 31-32]. And the Almighty says: {Say: if you possessed the treasures of the mercy of my Lord, you would surely withhold them for fear of spending, and man is ever stingy} [al-Isra: 100]. And He says: {Or have they a share of dominion? Then indeed they would not give the people so much as a speck} [al-Nisa: 53]. In all of this is a clarification of the incapacity of servants and the disagreement of their opinions and desires, and that He, exalted, alone is perfect in all His attributes, His words, His deeds, His legislation, His decree, and His governance of His creation, exalted and sanctified is He, so there is no god besides Him and no lord other than Him.

Then He says: {Rather, We have brought them their remembrance}, meaning the Qur'an, {but they turn away from their remembrance}.

His saying: {Or do you ask them for a payment} al-Hasan said: a wage. Qatadah said: a reward. {But the payment of your Lord is better} That is, you do not ask them for a wage, nor a reward, nor anything at all in return for calling them to guidance, but rather you seek with that the abundant reward of God, just as He said: {Say: whatever wage I might have asked of you is yours; my wage is only from God} [Saba: 47], and He said: {Say: I do not ask you for any wage for it, nor am I one of those who pretend} [Sad: 86], and He said: {Say: I do not ask you for any wage for it, except love for the near of kin} [al-Shura: 23], and the Almighty says: {And there came from the farthest part of the city a man running; he said: O my people, follow the messengers. Follow those who do not ask you for any wage, and who are rightly guided} [Ya-Sin: 20-21].

His saying: {And indeed, you call them to a straight path. And indeed, those who do not believe in the Hereafter are surely deviating from the path} Imam Ahmad said:

[chain] narrated by Hasan ibn Musa, from Hammad ibn Salamah, from Ali ibn Zayd ibn Jud'an, from Yusuf ibn Mihran, from Ibn Abbas: that the Messenger of God ﷺ, in what the sleeper sees, was approached by two angels, one of whom sat at his feet and the other at his head. The one at his feet said to the one at his head: "Give a parable of this man and his nation." He said: "The parable of him and his nation is like a group of travelers who arrived at the edge of a wasteland, and they had with them neither enough provisions to cross the wasteland nor enough to go back. While they were in that state, a man came to them wearing a fine striped garment, and he said: 'What would you say if I brought you to lush meadows and abundant watering pools, would you follow me?' They said: 'Yes.' So he set off and brought them to lush meadows and abundant watering pools, and they ate and drank and grew fat. Then he said to them: 'Did I not find you in that state, and did you not promise me that if I brought you to lush meadows and abundant watering pools you would follow me?' They said: 'Yes indeed.' He said: 'Ahead of you are meadows lusher than these, and pools more abundant than these, so follow me.' A group of them said: 'He has spoken truly, by God, let us follow him,' while another group said: 'We are content with this, we will remain here.'"

Al-Hafiz Abu Ya'la al-Mawsili said: [chain] narrated by Zuhayr, from Yunus ibn Muhammad, from Ya'qub ibn Abd Allah al-Ash'ari, from Hafs ibn Humayd, from Ikrimah, from Ibn Abbas, from Umar ibn al-Khattab, may God be pleased with him, who said: the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "I am holding onto your waist-belts saying: come away from the Fire, come away from the Fire, but you overpower me and fling yourselves into it as moths and locusts fling themselves. I am about to release your belts, while I am your forerunner at the Basin (al-Hawd). You will come to me together and scattered, and I will recognize you by your marks and your names, just as a man recognizes a stray camel among his own camels. Then you will be led away, some to the right and some to the left, and I will implore the Lord of the worlds concerning you: 'O Lord, my people, O Lord, my nation.'

Then it will be said: 'O Muhammad, you do not know what they did after you; they kept walking backward on their heels after you.' I will surely recognize one of you coming on the Day of Resurrection carrying a sheep that bleats, calling out: 'O Muhammad, O Muhammad!' and I will say: 'I have no power to do anything for you, I had already conveyed the message.' And I will surely recognize one of you coming on the Day of Resurrection carrying a camel that groans, calling out: 'O Muhammad, O Muhammad!' and I will say: 'I have no power to do anything, I had already conveyed the message.' And I will surely recognize one of you coming on the Day of Resurrection carrying a horse that neighs, calling out: 'O Muhammad, O Muhammad!' and I will say: 'I have no power to do anything for you, I had already conveyed the message.' And I will surely recognize one of you coming on the Day of Resurrection carrying a waterskin of tanned leather, calling out: 'O Muhammad, O Muhammad!' and I will say: 'I have no power to do anything for you, I had already conveyed the message.'"

Ali ibn al-Madini said: this is a hadith with a hasan (sound) chain, except that Hafs ibn Humayd is majhul (unknown), and I do not know of anyone who narrated from him besides Ya'qub ibn Abd Allah al-Ash'ari al-Qummi.

I say: rather, Ash'ath ibn Ishaq also narrated from him, and Yahya ibn Ma'in said of him: sound. Al-Nasa'i and Ibn Hibban both declared him reliable.

His saying: {And indeed, those who do not believe in the Hereafter are surely deviating from the path} that is, they are turning aside, deviating, and swerving. The Arabs say: "So-and-so nakaba (turned aside) from the road" when he strayed from it.

His saying: {And if We had mercy on them and removed what distress is upon them, they would surely persist in their transgression, wandering blindly} The Almighty informs us of their harshness in their disbelief, that if He had relieved their afflictions and made them understand the Qur'an, they still would not have submitted to it, but would have continued in their disbelief, their obstinacy, and their transgression, just as the Almighty says: {And if God had known any good in them, He would have made them hear, but even if He had made them hear, they would have turned away, being averse} [al-Anfal: 23], and He says: {And if you could see when they are made to stand before the Fire, and they say: would that we could be sent back, and we would not deny the signs of our Lord, and we would be among the believers. Rather, what they used to hide before has become apparent to them. And if they were sent back, they would surely return to what they were forbidden, and indeed they are liars. And they say: there is nothing but our life in this world, and we will not be resurrected} [al-An'am: 27-29]. This is an instance of God's knowledge of what would not occur, of how it would be if it did occur.

Al-Dahhak said, from Ibn Abbas: everything in which the word "law" (if) occurs refers to something that will never happen at all.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُنْكِرًا عَلَى الْمُشْرِكِينَ فِي عَدَمِ تَفَهُّمِهِمْ لِلْقُرْآنِ الْعَظِيمِ، وَتَدَبُّرِهِمْ لَهُ وَإِعْرَاضِهِمْ عَنْهُ، مَعَ أَنَّهُمْ قَدْ خُصُّوا بِهَذَا الْكِتَابِ الَّذِي لَمْ يُنَزِّلِ اللَّهُ عَلَى رَسُولٍ أَكْمَلَ مِنْهُ وَلَا أَشْرَفَ، لَا سِيَّمَا وَآبَاؤُهُمُ الَّذِينَ مَاتُوا فِي الْجَاهِلِيَّةِ، حَيْثُ لَمْ يَبْلُغْهُمْ كِتَابٌ وَلَا أَتَاهُمْ نَذِيرٌ، فَكَانَ اللَّائِقُ بِهَؤُلَاءِ أَنْ يُقَابِلُوا النِّعْمَةَ الَّتِي أَسْدَاهَا اللَّهُ إِلَيْهِمْ بِقَبُولِهَا، وَالْقِيَامِ بِشُكْرِهَا وَتَفَهُّمِهَا، وَالْعَمَلِ بِمُقْتَضَاهَا آنَاءَ اللَّيْلِ وَأَطْرَافَ النَّهَارِ، كَمَا فَعَلَهُ النُّجَبَاءُ مِنْهُمْ مِمَّنْ أَسْلَمَ وَاتَّبَعَ الرَّسُولَ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ، وَرَضِيَ عَنْهُمْ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: ﴿أَفَلَمْ يَدَّبَّرُوا الْقَوْلَ﴾ إذًا وَاللَّهِ يَجِدُونَ فِي الْقُرْآنِ زَاجِرًا عَنْ مَعْصِيَةِ اللَّهِ لَوْ تَدَبَّرَهُ الْقَوْمُ وَعَقَلُوهُ، وَلَكِنَّهُمْ أَخَذُوا بِمَا تَشَابَهَ، فَهَلَكُوا عند ذلك.

ثُمَّ قَالَ مُنْكِرًا عَلَى الْكَافِرِينَ مِنْ قُرَيْشٍ: ﴿أَمْ لَمْ يَعْرِفُوا رَسُولَهُمْ فَهُمْ لَهُ مُنْكِرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: أَفَهُمْ لَا يَعْرِفُونَ مُحَمَّدًا وَصِدْقَهُ وَأَمَانَتَهُ وَصِيَانَتَهُ الَّتِي نَشَأَ بِهَا فِيهِمْ، أَفَيَقْدِرُونَ عَلَى إِنْكَارِ ذَلِكَ وَالْمُبَاهَتَةِ فِيهِ؟ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ جَعْفَرَ بْنَ أَبِي طَالِبٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، لِلنَّجَاشِيِّ مَلِكِ الْحَبَشَةِ: أَيُّهَا الْمَلِكُ، إِنَّ اللَّهَ بَعَثَ إِلَيْنَا رَسُولًا نَعْرِفُ نَسَبَهُ وَصِدْقَهُ وَأَمَانَتَهُ. وَهَكَذَا قَالَ الْمُغِيرَةُ بْنُ شُعْبَةَ لِنَائِبِ كِسْرَى حِينَ بَارَزَهُمْ وَكَذَلِكَ قَالَ أَبُو سُفْيَانَ صَخْرُ بْنُ حَرْبٍ لِمَلِكِ الرُّومِ هِرَقْلَ، حِينَ سَأَلَهُ وَأَصْحَابَهُ عَنْ صِفَاتِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ وَنَسَبِهِ وَصِدْقِهِ وَأَمَانَتِهِ، وَكَانُوا بَعْدُ كَفَّارًا لَمْ يُسْلِمُوا، وَمَعَ هَذَا مَا أَمْكَنَهُمْ إِلَّا الصِّدْقُ فَاعْتَرَفُوا بِذَلِكَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَمْ يَقُولُونَ بِهِ جِنَّةٌ﴾ يَحْكِي قَوْلَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ أَنَّهُ تقوَّل الْقُرْآنَ، أَيِ: افْتَرَاهُ مِنْ عِنْدِهِ، أَوْ أَنَّ بِهِ جُنُونًا لَا يَدْرِي مَا يَقُولُ. وَأَخْبَرَ عَنْهُمْ أَنَّ قُلُوبَهُمْ لَا تُؤْمِنُ بِهِ، وَهُمْ يَعْلَمُونَ بُطْلَانَ مَا يَقُولُونَهُ فِي الْقُرْآنِ، فَإِنَّهُ قَدْ أَتَاهُمْ مِنْ كَلَامِ اللَّهِ مَا لَا يُطاق وَلَا يُدافع، وَقَدْ تَحَدَّاهُمْ وَجَمِيعَ أَهْلِ الْأَرْضِ أَنْ يَأْتُوا بِمِثْلِهِ، فَمَا اسْتَطَاعُوا وَلَا يَسْتَطِيعُونَ أَبَدَ الْآبِدِينَ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿بَلْ جَاءَهُمْ بِالْحَقِّ وَأَكْثَرُهُمْ لِلْحَقِّ كَارِهُونَ﴾ يُحْتَمَلُ أَنْ تَكُونَ هَذِهِ جُمْلَةٌ حَالِيَّةٌ، أَيْ: فِي حَالِ كَرَاهَةِ أَكْثَرِهِمْ لِلْحَقِّ، وَيُحْتَمَلُ أَنْ تَكُونَ خَبَرِيَّةً مُسْتَأْنَفَةً، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: ذُكر لَنَا أَنَّ نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ ﷺ لَقِيَ رَجُلًا فَقَالَ لَهُ: "أَسْلِمْ" فَقَالَ الرَّجُلُ: إِنَّكَ لَتَدْعُونِي إِلَى أَمْرٍ أَنَا لَهُ كَارِهٌ. فَقَالَ نَبِيُّ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "وَإِنْ كُنْتَ كَارِهًا". وذُكِر لَنَا أَنَّهُ لَقِيَ رَجُلًا فَقَالَ لَهُ: "أَسْلِمْ" فَتَصَعَّده ذَلِكَ وَكَبُرَ عَلَيْهِ، فَقَالَ لَهُ نَبِيُّ اللَّهِ: "أَرَأَيْتَ لَوْ كنتَ فِي طَرِيقٍ وَعْر وَعْث، فَلَقِيتَ رَجُلًا تَعْرِفُ وَجْهَهُ، وَتَعْرِفُ نَسَبَهُ، فَدَعَاكَ إِلَى طَرِيقٍ وَاسِعٍ سَهْلٍ، أَكُنْتَ مُتَّبِعَهُ ؟ " قَالَ: نَعَمْ. فَقَالَ: "فَوَالَّذِي نَفْسُ مُحَمَّدٍ بِيَدِهِ، إِنَّكَ لَفِي أَوْعَرِ مِنْ ذَلِكَ الطَّرِيقِ لَوْ قَدْ كُنْتَ عَلَيْهِ، وَإِنِّي لَأَدْعُوَكَ إِلَى أَسْهَلِ مِنْ ذَلِكَ لَوْ دُعِيتَ إِلَيْهِ". وَذُكِرَ لَنَا أَنَّ نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ ﷺ لَقِيَ رَجُلًا فَقَالَ لَهُ: "أَسْلِمْ" فَتَصَعَّدَه ذَلِكَ، فَقَالَ لَهُ نَبِيُّ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أَرَأَيْتَ فَتَيَيْكَ، أَحَدُهُمَا إِذَا حَدَّثَكَ صَدَقَكَ، وَإِذَا ائْتَمَنْتَهُ أَدَّى إِلَيْكَ أَهْوَ أَحَبُّ إِلَيْكَ، أَمْ فَتَاكَ الَّذِي إِذَا حَدَّثَكَ كَذَبَكَ وَإِذَا ائْتَمَنْتَهُ خَانَكَ؟ ". قَالَ: بَلْ فَتَايَ الَّذِي إِذَا حَدَّثَنِي صَدَقَنِي، وَإِذَا ائْتَمَنْتُهُ أَدَّى إِلَيَّ. فَقَالَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ: "كَذَاكُمْ أَنْتُمْ عِنْدَ رَبِّكُمْ".

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلَوِ اتَّبَعَ الْحَقُّ أَهْوَاءَهُمْ لَفَسَدَتِ السَّمَاوَاتُ وَالأرْضُ وَمَنْ فِيهِنَّ﴾ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَأَبُو صَالِحٍ وَالسُّدِّيُّ: الْحَقُّ هُوَ اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، وَالْمُرَادُ: لَوْ أَجَابَهُمُ اللَّهُ إِلَى مَا فِي أَنْفُسِهِمْ مِنَ الْهَوَى، وَشَرَعَ الْأُمُورَ عَلَى وِفْقِ ذَلِكَ ﴿لَفَسَدَتِ السَّمَاوَاتُ وَالأرْضُ وَمَنْ فِيهِنَّ﴾ أَيْ: لِفَسَادِ أَهْوَائِهِمْ وَاخْتِلَافِهَا، كَمَا أَخْبَرَ عَنْهُمْ فِي قَوْلِهِمْ: ﴿لَوْلا نزلَ هَذَا الْقُرْآنُ عَلَى رَجُلٍ مِنَ الْقَرْيَتَيْنِ عَظِيمٍ﴾ ثُمَّ قَالَ: ﴿أَهُمْ يَقْسِمُونَ رَحْمَةَ رَبِّكَ﴾ [الزُّخْرُفِ: ٣١، ٣٢] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿قُلْ لَوْ أَنْتُمْ تَمْلِكُونَ خَزَائِنَ رَحْمَةِ رَبِّي إِذًا لأمْسَكْتُمْ خَشْيَةَ الإنْفَاقِ وَكَانَ الإنْسَانُ قَتُورًا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ:١٠٠] وَقَالَ: ﴿أَمْ لَهُمْ نَصِيبٌ مِنَ الْمُلْكِ فَإِذًا لَا يُؤْتُونَ النَّاسَ نَقِيرًا﴾ [النساء: ٥٣] ، فَفِي هَذَا كُلِّهِ تَبْيِينُ عَجْزِ الْعِبَادِ وَاخْتِلَافِ آرَائِهِمْ وَأَهْوَائِهِمْ، وَأَنَّهُ تَعَالَى هُوَ الْكَامِلُ فِي جَمِيعِ صِفَاتِهِ وَأَقْوَالِهِ وَأَفْعَالِهِ، وَشَرْعِهِ وَقَدَرِهِ، وَتَدْبِيرِهِ لِخَلْقِهِ تَعَالَى وَتَقَدَّسَ، فَلَا إِلَهَ غَيْرُهُ، وَلَا رَبَّ سِوَاهُ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ: ﴿بَلْ أَتَيْنَاهُمْ بِذِكْرِهِمْ﴾ يَعْنِي: الْقُرْآنَ، ﴿فَهُمْ عَنْ ذِكْرِهِمْ مُعْرِضُونَ﴾ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَمْ تَسْأَلُهُمْ خَرْجًا﴾ : قَالَ الْحَسَنُ: أَجْرًا. وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: جَعْلًا ﴿فَخَرَاجُ رَبِّكَ خَيْرٌ﴾ أَيْ أَنْتَ لَا تَسْأَلُهُمْ أُجْرَةً وَلَا جَعْلًا وَلَا شَيْئًا عَلَى دَعْوَتِكَ إِيَّاهُمْ إِلَى الْهُدَى، بَلْ أَنْتَ فِي ذَلِكَ تَحْتَسِبُ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ جَزِيلَ ثَوَابِهِ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿قُلْ مَا سَأَلْتُكُمْ مِنْ أَجْرٍ فَهُوَ لَكُمْ إِنْ أَجْرِيَ إِلا عَلَى اللَّهِ﴾ [سَبَأٍ: ٤٧] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿قُلْ مَا أَسْأَلُكُمْ عَلَيْهِ مِنْ أَجْرٍ وَمَا أَنَا مِنَ الْمُتَكَلِّفِينَ﴾ [ص: ٨٦] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿قُلْ لَا أَسْأَلُكُمْ عَلَيْهِ أَجْرًا إِلا الْمَوَدَّةَ فِي الْقُرْبَى﴾ [الشُّورَى: ٢٣] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَجَاءَ مِنْ أَقْصَى الْمَدِينَةِ رَجُلٌ يَسْعَى قَالَ يَا قَوْمِ اتَّبِعُوا الْمُرْسَلِينَ اتَّبِعُوا مَنْ لَا يَسْأَلُكُمْ أَجْرًا وَهُمْ مُهْتَدُونَ﴾ [يس: ٢٠، ٢١] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِنَّكَ لَتَدْعُوهُمْ إِلَى صِرَاطٍ مُسْتَقِيمٍ. وَإِنَّ الَّذِينَ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ بِالآخِرَةِ عَنِ الصِّرَاطِ لَنَاكِبُونَ﴾ قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ:

حَدَّثَنَا حَسَنُ بْنُ مُوسَى، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادُ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ زَيْدِ بْنِ جُدْعَان، عَنْ يُوسُفَ بْنِ مِهْران، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ؛ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَتَاهُ -فِيمَا يَرَى النَّائِمُ-مَلَكَانِ، فَقَعَدَ أَحَدُهُمَا عِنْدَ رِجْلَيْهِ، وَالْآخِرُ عِنْدَ رَأْسِهِ، فَقَالَ الَّذِي عِنْدَ رِجْلَيْهِ لِلَّذِي عِنْدَ رَأْسِهِ: اضْرِبْ مَثَل هَذَا وَمَثَلَ أُمَّتِهِ. فَقَالَ: إِنَّ مَثَلَه وَمَثَلَ أُمَّتِهِ، كَمَثَلِ قَوْمٍ سُفْر انْتَهَوْا إِلَى رَأْسِ مَفَازة، فَلَمْ يَكُنْ مَعَهُمْ مِنَ الزَّادِ مَا يَقْطَعُونَ بِهِ الْمَفَازَةَ وَلَا مَا يَرْجِعُونَ بِهِ، فَبَيْنَا هُمْ كَذَلِكَ إِذْ أَتَاهُمْ رَجُلٌ فِي حُلَّةٍ حِبَرَةٍ، فَقَالَ: أَرَأَيْتُمْ إِنْ وَرَدْتُ بِكُمْ رِيَاضًا مُعْشِبَةً، وَحِيَاضًا رِوَاءً تَتَّبِعُونِي؟ فَقَالُوا: نَعَمْ. قَالَ: فَانْطَلَقَ، فَأَوْرَدَهُمْ رِيَاضًا مُعْشِبَةً وَحِيَاضًا رُوَاءً، فَأَكَلُوا وَشَرِبُوا وَسَمِنُوا فَقَالَ لَهُمْ: أَلَمْ أَلْفِكُمْ عَلَى تِلْكَ الْحَالِ، فَجَعَلْتُمْ لِي إِنْ وَرَدْتُ بِكُمْ رِيَاضًا مُعْشِبَةً وَحِيَاضًا رُوَاءً أَنْ تَتَّبِعُونِي؟ قَالُوا : بَلَى، قَالَ: فَإِنَّ بَيْنَ أَيْدِيكُمْ رِيَاضًا أَعْشَبُ مِنْ هَذِهِ، وَحِيَاضًا هِيَ أَرَوَى مِنْ هَذِهِ، فَاتَّبِعُونِي. قَالَ: فَقَالَتْ طَائِفَةٌ: صَدَقَ وَاللَّهِ، لِنَتَّبِعْهُ. وَقَالَتْ طَائِفَةٌ: قَدْ رَضِينَا بِهَذَا نُقِيمُ عَلَيْهِ .

وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو يُعْلَى الْمَوْصِلِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا زُهَيْرٌ، حَدَّثَنَا يُونُسُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا يَعْقُوبُ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ الْأَشْعَرِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا حَفْصُ بْنُ حُمَيْدٍ، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، عَنْ عُمَرَ بْنِ الْخَطَّابِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنِّي مُمْسِكٌ بِحَجْزِكُمْ: هَلُمَّ عَنِ النَّارِ، هَلُمَّ عَنِ النَّارِ، وَتَغْلِبُونِي وَتُقَاحِمُونَ فِيهَا تَقَاحُم الْفَرَاشَ وَالْجَنَادِبِ، فَأُوشِكُ أَنْ أُرْسِلَ حَجْزَكُمْ وَأَنَا فَرَطكم عَلَى الْحَوْضِ، فَتَرِدُونَ عَلَيَّ مَعًا وَأَشْتَاتًا، أَعْرِفُكُمْ بِسِيمَاكُمْ وَأَسْمَائِكُمْ، كَمَا يَعْرِفُ الرَّجُلُ الْغَرِيبَ مِنَ الْإِبِلِ فِي إِبِلِهِ، فيُذْهَب بِكُمْ ذَاتَ الْيَمِينِ وَذَاتَ الشِّمَالِ، فَأُنَاشِدُ فِيكُمْ رَبَّ الْعَالَمِينَ: أَيْ رَبِّ، قومي، أي رب أمتي.

فَيُقَالُ: يَا مُحَمَّدُ، إِنَّكَ لَا تَدْرِي مَا أَحْدَثُوا بَعْدَكَ، إِنَّهُمْ كَانُوا يَمْشُونَ بَعْدَكَ الْقَهْقَرَى عَلَى أَعْقَابِهِمْ، فَلَأَعْرِفَنَّ أَحَدَكُمْ يَأْتِي يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ يَحْمِلُ شَاةً لَهَا ثُغَاءٌ، يُنَادِي: يَا مُحَمَّدُ، يَا مُحَمَّدُ. فَأَقُولُ: لَا أَمْلِكُ لَكَ شَيْئًا. قَدْ بَلَّغْتُ، وَلَأَعْرِفَنَّ أَحَدَكُمْ يَأْتِي يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ يَحْمِلُ بَعِيرَا لَهُ رُغَاء، يُنَادِي: يَا مُحَمَّدُ، يَا مُحَمَّدُ. فَأَقُولُ: لَا أَمْلِكُ شَيْئًا، قَدْ بَلَّغْتُ، وَلَأَعْرِفَنَّ أَحَدَكُمْ يَأْتِي يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ يَحْمِلُ فَرَسًا لَهَا حَمْحَمَةٌ، فَيُنَادِي: يَا مُحَمَّدُ، يَا مُحَمَّدُ، فَأَقُولُ: لَا أَمْلِكُ لَكَ شَيْئًا، قَدْ بَلَّغْتُ، وَلَأَعْرِفَنَّ أَحَدَكُمْ يَأْتِي يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ يَحْمِلُ سِقَاءً مِنْ أُدْمٍ، يُنَادِي: يَا مُحَمَّدُ، يَا مُحَمَّدُ: فَأَقُولُ: لَا أَمْلِكُ لَكَ شَيْئًا قَدْ بَلَّغْتُ" .

وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ الْمَدِينِيِّ: هَذَا حَدِيثٌ حَسَنُ الْإِسْنَادِ، إِلَّا أَنَّ حَفْصَ بْنَ حُمَيْدٍ مَجْهُولٌ، لَا أَعْلَمَ رَوَى عَنْهُ غَيْرَ يَعْقُوبَ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ الْأَشْعَرِيِّ الْقَمِّيِّ.

قُلْتُ: بَلْ قَدْ رَوَى عَنْهُ أَيْضًا أَشْعَثُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، وَقَالَ فِيهِ يَحْيَى بْنُ مَعِينٍ: صَالِحٌ. وَوَثَّقَهُ النَّسَائِيُّ وَابْنُ حِبَّانَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِنَّ الَّذِينَ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ بِالآخِرَةِ عَنِ الصِّرَاطِ لَنَاكِبُونَ﴾ أَيْ: لَعَادِلُونَ جَائِرُونَ مُنْحَرِفُونَ. تَقُولُ الْعَرَبُ: نَكَبَ فَلَانٌ عَنِ الطَّرِيقِ: إِذَا زَاغَ عَنْهَا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلَوْ رَحِمْنَاهُمْ وَكَشَفْنَا مَا بِهِمْ مِنْ ضُرٍّ لَلَجُّوا فِي طُغْيَانِهِمْ يَعْمَهُونَ﴾ : يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ غِلَظِهِمْ فِي كُفْرِهِمْ بِأَنَّهُ لَوْ أَرَاحَ عِلَلَهُمْ وَأَفْهَمَهُمُ الْقُرْآنَ، لَمَا انْقَادُوا لَهُ وَلَاسْتَمَرُّوا عَلَى كُفْرِهِمْ وَعِنَادِهِمْ وَطُغْيَانِهِمْ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَوْ عَلِمَ اللَّهُ فِيهِمْ خَيْرًا لأسْمَعَهُمْ وَلَوْ أَسْمَعَهُمْ لَتَوَلَّوْا وَهُمْ مُعْرِضُونَ﴾ [الْأَنْفَالِ: ٢٣] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿وَلَوْ تَرَى إِذْ وُقِفُوا عَلَى النَّارِ فَقَالُوا يَا لَيْتَنَا نُرَدُّ وَلا نُكَذِّبَ بِآيَاتِ رَبِّنَا وَنَكُونَ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ. بَلْ بَدَا لَهُمْ مَا كَانُوا يُخْفُونَ مِنْ قَبْلُ وَلَوْ رُدُّوا لَعَادُوا لِمَا نُهُوا عَنْهُ وَإِنَّهُمْ لَكَاذِبُونَ. وَقَالُوا إِنْ هِيَ إِلا حَيَاتُنَا الدُّنْيَا وَمَا نَحْنُ بِمَبْعُوثِينَ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ٢٧-٢٩] ، فَهَذَا مِنْ بَابِ عِلْمِهِ تَعَالَى بِمَا لَا يَكُونُ، لَوْ كَانَ كَيْفَ يَكُونُ .

[وَ] قَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: كُلُّ مَا فِيهِ "لَوْ"، فَهُوَ مِمَّا لا يكون أبدا.

---

## 23:76-83 — verses 76-83 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says: {And We seized them with punishment}, meaning: We tried them with calamities and hardships, {but they did not humble themselves to their Lord, nor did they supplicate}, meaning: that did not turn them away from the disbelief and defiance they were engaged in. Rather, they continued in their misguidance and error. {But they did not humble themselves}, meaning: they did not show submissiveness, {nor did they supplicate}, meaning: they did not call upon Him, just as the Almighty said: {Why then, when Our punishment came to them, did they not humble themselves? But their hearts became hardened, and Satan made attractive to them what they used to do} [al-An'am: 43].

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Ibn Abbas said: Abu Sufyan came to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ and said, "O Muhammad, I adjure you by Allah and by kinship, for we have eaten al-'ilhiz," meaning fur and blood mixed together. Then Allah revealed: {And We seized them with punishment, but they did not humble themselves to their Lord, nor did they supplicate}.

An-Nasa'i likewise narrated it from Muhammad ibn Aqil, from Ali ibn al-Husayn, from his father, with the same content. The origin of this hadith is found in the two Sahihs: that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ invoked against Quraysh when they persisted in defiance, saying, "O Allah, aid me against them with seven years like the seven years of Yusuf."

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Wahb ibn Kaysan said: Wahb ibn Munabbih was imprisoned, and a man among the sons said to him, "Shall I not recite to you a line of poetry, O Abu Abdillah?" Wahb said: "We are in a small measure of Allah's punishment, and Allah, the Almighty, says: {And We seized them with punishment, but they did not humble themselves to their Lord, nor did they supplicate}." He said: Wahb then fasted three consecutive days, and it was said to him, "What is this fasting for, O Abu Abdillah?" He said: "Something new was brought upon us, so we brought about something new," meaning: imprisonment was newly brought upon us, so we brought about an increase in worship.

As for His saying: {Until, when We open upon them a gate of severe punishment, behold, they are in despair}, meaning: until when Allah's command comes to them, and the Hour comes upon them suddenly, and they are seized by Allah's punishment in ways they had not reckoned with, at that point they fall into despair of every good, lose hope of every relief, and their hopes and expectations are cut off.

Then the Almighty mentions His favor upon His servants in that He gave them hearing, sight, and hearts, that is, the intellects and understanding by which they perceive things and take heed from the signs in the universe that point to the oneness of Allah the Almighty, and that He is the One who acts as He wills by His own choice.

As for His saying: {Little do you give thanks}, meaning: how little is your gratitude to Allah for what He has bestowed upon you, similar to His saying: {And most of the people, even if you eagerly desire it, will not be believers} [Yusuf: 103].

Then the Almighty informs of His tremendous power and overwhelming dominion in creating mankind and dispersing them throughout all regions of the earth, with their differing races, languages, and characteristics. Then on the Day of Resurrection He will gather the first of them and the last of them for the appointed time of a known day, leaving out none of them, small or great, male or female, exalted or lowly, but that He will bring each one back just as He originated them. Hence He says: {And He is the One who gives life and causes death}, meaning: He gives life to decayed bones and causes nations to perish. {And His is the alternation of night and day}, meaning: it is by His command that night and day are subjected, each of them pursuing the other in swift succession, following one after another without pause, and never separating by a time belonging to something other than themselves, as the Almighty says: {It is not for the sun to overtake the moon, nor does the night outstrip the day; each floats in an orbit} [Ya-Sin: 40].

As for His saying: {Will you not then reason?}, meaning: do you not have intellects that would guide you to the Mighty, the All-Knowing, who has overpowered all things, dominated all things, and to whom all things submit?

Then He says, informing of those who deny the resurrection, who resemble the deniers who came before them: {Rather, they say the like of what the former peoples said. They said, "When we are dead and have become dust and bones, are we indeed to be resurrected?"}, that is, they regard the occurrence of that as far-fetched, given that they will have turned into decayed remains. {We and our forefathers were promised this before. This is nothing but the tales of the ancients}, meaning: they claim that resurrection is impossible, and that only one who has received such notions from the books of the ancients and their fabrications could speak of it. This denial and rejection of theirs is like His saying, informing of them: {What, even when we are decayed bones? They say, "That then would be a losing return." But it will be only a single shout, and behold, they are on the surface of the earth} [an-Nazi'at: 11-14]. And the Almighty says: {Does man not consider that We created him from a drop of sperm, yet behold, he is an open disputant? And he coins for Us a similitude, and forgets his own creation. He says, "Who will give life to bones when they are decayed?" Say: "He will give them life who produced them the first time, and He is All-Knowing of every creation"} [Ya-Sin: 77-79].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَقَدْ أَخَذْنَاهُمْ بِالْعَذَابِ﴾ أَيِ: ابْتَلَيْنَاهُمْ بِالْمَصَائِبِ وَالشَّدَائِدِ، ﴿فَمَا اسْتَكَانُوا لِرَبِّهِمْ وَمَا يَتَضَرَّعُونَ﴾ أَيْ: فَمَا رَدَّهُمْ ذَلِكَ عَمَّا كَانُوا فِيهِ مِنَ الْكُفْرِ وَالْمُخَالَفَةِ، بَلِ اسْتَمَرُّوا عَلَى ضَلَالِهِمْ وَغَيِّهِمْ. ﴿فَمَا اسْتَكَانُوا﴾ أَيْ: مَا خَشَعُوا، ﴿وَمَا يَتَضَرَّعُونَ﴾ أَيْ: مَا دَعَوْا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَلَوْلا إِذْ جَاءَهُمْ بَأْسُنَا تَضَرَّعُوا وَلَكِنْ قَسَتْ قُلُوبُهُمْ وَزَيَّنَ لَهُمُ الشَّيْطَانُ مَا كَانُوا يَعْمَلُونَ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ٤٣] .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ الْحُسَيْنِ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بن حمزة المروزي، حدثنا علي ابن الْحُسَيْنِ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، عَنْ يَزِيدَ -يَعْنِي: النَّحْوِيَّ-عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، أَنَّهُ قَالَ: جَاءَ أَبُو سُفْيَانَ إِلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَقَالَ: يَا مُحَمَّدُ، أَنْشُدُكَ اللَّهَ وَالرَّحِمَ، فَقَدْ أَكَلْنَا الْعِلْهِزَ -يَعْنِي: الْوَبَرَ وَالدَّمَ-فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: ﴿وَلَقَدْ أَخَذْنَاهُمْ بِالْعَذَابِ فَمَا اسْتَكَانُوا لِرَبِّهِمْ وَمَا يَتَضَرَّعُونَ﴾

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ النَّسَائِيُّ عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَقِيلٍ، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ الْحُسَيْنِ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، بِهِ . وَأَصْلُ هَذَا الْحَدِيثِ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ دَعَا عَلَى قُرَيْشٍ حِينَ اسْتَعْصَوْا فَقَالَ: "اللَّهُمَّ أَعِنِّي عَلَيْهِمْ بِسَبْعٍ كَسَبْعِ يُوسُفَ" .
